  <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

    <body>
      <div n="6" type="sthāna">

        <head>[uttaratantram]</head>

        <div n="31" type="adhyāya">

          <head>ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.1"> athāto revatīpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.3"> aśvagandhā ca śṛṅgī ca sārivā sapunarnavā |
            <caesura/>
             sahe tathā vidārī ca kaṣāyāḥ secane hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.4"> tailamabhyañjane kāryaṃ kuṣṭhe sarjarase 'pi ca |
            <caesura/>
             palaṅkaṣāyāṃ nalade tathā girikadambake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.5"> dhavāśvakarṇakakubhadhātakītindukīṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kākolyādigaṇe caiva pānīyaṃ sarpiriṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6ab"> kulatthāḥ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ ca pradehaḥ sārvagandhikaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6cd"> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi yavā yavaphalo ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.7"> sandhyayor ubhayoḥ kāryam etad uddhūpanaṃ śiśoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             varuṇāriṣṭakamayaṃ rucakaṃ saindukaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.8"> satataṃ dhārayec cāpi kṛtaṃ vā pautrajīvikam |
            <caesura/>
             śuklāḥ sumanaso lājāḥ payaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.9"> balirnivedyo gotīrthe revatyai prayatātmanā |
            <caesura/>
             saṅgame ca bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryād dhātrīkumārayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.10"> nānāvastradharā devī citramālyānulepanā |
            <caesura/>
             calatkuṇḍalinī śyāmā revatī te prasīdatu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.11"> upāsate yāṃ satataṃ devyo vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lambā karālā vinatā tathaiva bahuputrikā |
            <caesura/>
             revatī śuṣkanāmā yā sā te devī prasīdatu ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśurtasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre revatīpratiṣedho
            nāma (pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||31 || </p>
        </div>
        <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.1"> athātaḥ pūtanāratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.3"> kapotavaṅkāraluko varuṇaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āsphotā caiva yojyāḥ syurbālānāṃ pariṣecane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.4"> vacā vayaḥsthā golomī haritālaṃ manaḥśilā |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaṃ sarjarasaś caiva tailārthe varga iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.5"> hitaṃ ghṛtaṃ tugākṣīryāṃ siddhaṃ madhurakeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhatālīśakhadiracandanasyandane tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.6"> devadāruvacāhiṅgukuṣṭhaṃ girikadambarakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             elā hareṇavaś cāpi yojyā uddhūpane sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.7"> gandhanākulikumbhīke majjāno badarasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             karkaṭāsthi ghṛtaṃ cāpi dhūpanaṃ sarṣapaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.8"> kākādanīṃ citraphalāṃ bimbīṃ guñjāṃ ca dhārayet |
            <caesura/>
             matsyaudanaṃ ca kurvīta kṛśarāṃ palalaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śarāvasaṃpuṭe kṛtvā baliṃ śūnyagṛhe haret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9ab"> ucchiṣṭenābhiṣekeṇa śiśoḥ snapanamiṣyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9cd"> pūjyā ca pūtanā devī balibhiḥ sopahārakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.10"> malināmbarasaṃvītā malinā rūkṣamūrdhajā |
            <caesura/>
             śūnyāgārāśritā devī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.11"> durdarśanā sudurgandhā karālā meghakālikā |
            <caesura/>
             bhinnagārāśrayā devī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre (ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ,
            āditaḥ) dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
          <head>trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.1"> athāto 'ndhapūtanāprasiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.3"> tiktakadrumapatrāṇāṃ kāryaḥ kvātho 'vasecane |
            <caesura/>
             surā sauvīrakaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.4"> tathā sarjarasaś caiva tailārtham upadiśyate |
            <caesura/>
             pippalyaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ vargo madhurako madhu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5ab"> śālapārṇī bṛhatyau ca ghṛtārtham upadiśyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5cd"> sarvagandhaiḥ pradehaś ca gātreṣv akṣṇoś ca śītalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.6"> purīṣaṃ kaukkuṭaṃ keśāṃś carma sarpatvacaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             jīrṇāṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghāṭīṃ dhūmanāyopakalpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.7"> kukkuṭīṃ markaṭīṃ śimbīmanantāṃ cāpi dhārayet |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsamāmaṃ tathā pakvaṃ śoṇitaṃ ca catuṣpathe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.8"> nivedyam antaś ca gṛhe śiśo rakṣānimittataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śiśoś ca snapanaṃ kuryāt sarvagandhodakaiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.9"> karālā piṅgalā muṇḍā kaṣāyāmbaravāsinī |
            <caesura/>
             devī bālam imaṃ prītā saṃrakṣatv andhapūtanā ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
            'ndhapūtanāpratiṣedho nāma (saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.1"> athātaḥ śītapūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.3"> kapitthaṃ suvahāṃ bimbīṃ tathā bilvaṃ pracībalam |
            <caesura/>
             nandīṃ bhallātakaṃ cāpi pariṣeke prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.4"> bastamūtraṃ gavāṃ mūtraṃ mustaṃ ca suradāru ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaṃ ca sarvagandhāṃś ca tailārthamavacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.5"> rohiṇīsarjakhadirapalāśakakubhatvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             niṣkvāthya tasminniṣkvāthe sakṣīraṃ vipacedghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.6"> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi bastagandhāmahestvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nimbapatrāṇi madhukaṃ dhūpanārthaṃ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.7"> dhārayed api lambāṃ ca guñjāṃ kākādanīṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nadyāṃ mudgakṛtaiś cānnais tarpayec chītapūtanām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.8"> devyai deyaś copahāro vāruṇī rudhiraṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             jalāśayānte bālasya snapanaṃ copadiśyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.9"> mudgaudanāśanā devī surāśoṇitapāyinī |
            <caesura/>
             jalāśayālayā devī pātu tvāṃ śītapūtanā ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
            śītapūtanāpratiṣedho nāma (aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||34 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.1"> athāto mukhamaṇḍikāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.3"> kapitthabilvatarkārīvāṃśīgandharvahastakāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kuberākṣī ca yojyāḥ syurbālānāṃ pariṣecane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.4"> svarasairbhṛṅgavṛkṣāṇāṃ tathājaharigandhayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ vasāṃ ca saṃyojya pacedabhyañjane śiśoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.5"> madhūlikāyāṃ payasi tugākṣīryāṃ gaṇe tathā |
            <caesura/>
             madhure pañcamūle ca kanīyasi ghṛtaṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.6"> vacā sarjarasaḥ kuṣṭhaṃ sarpiś coddhūpanaṃ hitam |
            <caesura/>
             dhārayed api jihvāś ca cāṣacīrallisarpajāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.7"> varṇakaṃ cūrṇakaṃ mālyam añjanaṃ pāradaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             manaḥśilāṃ copaharedgoṣṭhamadhye baliṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.8"> pāyasaṃ sapuroḍāśaṃ balyartham upasaṃharet |
            <caesura/>
             mantrapūtābhir adbhiś ca tatraiva snapanaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.9"> alaṅkṛtā rūpavatī subhagā kāmarūpiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             goṣṭhamadhyālayaratā pātu tvāṃ mukhamaṇḍikā ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
            mukhamaṇḍikāpratiṣedho nāma (navamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.1"> athāto naigameṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.3"> bilvāgnimanthapūtīkāḥ kāryāḥ syuḥ pariṣecane |
            <caesura/>
             surā sabījaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ pariṣeke ca śasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.4"> priyaṅgusaralānantāśatapuṣpākuṭannaṭaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pacettailaṃ sagomūtrairdadhimastvamlakāñjikaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.5"> pañcamūladvayakvāthe kṣīre madhurakeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             pacedghṛtaṃ ca medhāvī kharjūrīmastake 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6ab"> vacāṃ vayaḥsthāṃ golomīṃ jaṭilāṃ cāpi dhārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6cd"> utsādanaṃ hitaṃ cātra skandāpasmāranāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.7"> siddhārthakavacāhiṅgukuṣṭhaṃ caivākṣataiḥ saha |
            <caesura/>
             bhallātakājamodāś ca hitamuddhūpanaṃ śiśoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.8"> markaṭolūkagṛdhrāṇāṃ purīṣāṇi navagrahe |
            <caesura/>
             dhūpaḥ supte jane kāryo bālasya hitamicchatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.9"> tilataṇḍulakaṃ mālyaṃ bhakṣyāṃś ca vividhānapi |
            <caesura/>
             kumārapitṛmeṣāya vṛkṣamūle nivedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10ab"> adhastād vaṭavṛkṣasya snapanaṃ copadiśyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10cd"> baliṃ nyagrodhavṛkṣeṣu tithau ṣaṣṭhyāṃ nivedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.11"> ajānanaś calākṣibhrūḥ kāmarūpī mahāyaśāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bālaṃ bālapitā devo naigameṣo 'bhir akṣatu ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
            naigameṣapratiṣedho nāma (daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||36 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="37" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.1"> athāto grahotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2a"/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.3"> navaskandādayaḥ proktā bālānāṃ ya ime grahāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrīmanto divyavapuṣo nārīpuruṣavigrahāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.4"> ete guhasya rakṣārthaṃ kṛttikomāgniśūlibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sṛṣṭāḥ śaravaṇasthasya rakṣitasyātmatejasā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.5"> strīvigrahā grahā ye tu nānārūpā mayeritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gaṅgomākṛttikānāṃ te bhāgā rājasatāmasāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.6"> naigameṣas tu pārvatyā sṛṣṭo meṣānano grahaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kumāradhārī devasya guhasyātmasamaḥ sakhā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.7"> skandāpasmārasaṃjño yaḥ so 'gnināgnisamadyutiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa ca skandasakhā nāma viśākha iti cocyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.8"> skandaḥ sṛṣṭo bhagavatā devena tripurāriṇā |
            <caesura/>
             bibharti cāparāṃ saṃjñāṃ kumāra iti sa grahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.9"> bālalīlādharo yo 'yaṃ devo rudrāgnisṃbhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mithyācāreṣu bhagavān svayaṃ naiṣa pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.10"> kumāraḥ skandasāmānyādatra kecidapaṇḍitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gṛhṇātītyalpavijñānā bruvate dehacintakāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.11"> tato bhagavati skande surasenāpatau kṛte |
            <caesura/>
             upatasthurgrahāḥ sarve dīptaśaktidharaṃ guham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.12"> ūcuḥ prāñjalayaś cainaṃ vṛttiṃ naḥ saṃvidhatsva vai |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāmarthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devamacodayat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.13"> tato grahāṃstānuvāca bhagavān bhaganetrahṛt |
            <caesura/>
             tiryagyoniṃ mānuṣaṃ ca tritayaṃ jagat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.14"> parasparopakāreṇa vartate dhāryate 'pi ca |
            <caesura/>
             devā manuṣyān prīṇanti tairyagyonīṃs tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.15"> vartamānairyathākālaṃ śītavarṣoṣṇamārutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ijyāñjalinamaskārajapahomavratādibhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.16"> narāḥ samyak prayuktaiś ca prīṇanti tridiveśvarān |
            <caesura/>
             bhāgadheyaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca śeṣaṃ kiñcin na vidyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.17"> tad yuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttirbāleṣv eva bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             kuleṣu yeṣu nejyante devāḥ pitara eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.18"> brāhmaṇāḥ sādhavaś caiva guravo 'tithayas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nivṛttācāraśauceṣu parapākopajīviṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.19"> utsannabalibhikṣeṣu bhinnakāṃsyopabhojiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             gṛheṣu teṣu ye bālāstān gṛhṇīdhvamaśaṅkitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.20"> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā bālān gṛhṇanti cāpy ataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.21"> grahopasṛṣṭā bālās tu duś cikitsyatamā matāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cāpi dhruvaṃ skandagrahe matam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.22"> skandagraho 'tyugratamaḥ sarveṣv eva yataḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             anyo vā sarvarūpas tu na sādhyo graha ucyate ||</l>
          <p xml:id="SS.6.37.24a" ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kumāratantre grahotpattyadhyāyo nāma (ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptatriṃśattamo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||37 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.1"> athāto yonivyāpatpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.3"> pravṛddhaliṅgaṃ puruṣaṃ yātyartham upasevate |
            <caesura/>
             rūkṣadurbalabālā yā tasyā vāyuḥ prakupyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.4ab"> sa duṣṭo yonim āsādya yonirogāya kalpate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.4cd"> trayāṇām api doṣāṇāṃ yathāsvaṃ lakṣaṇena tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.5"> viṃśatir vyāpado yoner nirdiṣṭā rogasaṃgrahe |
            <caesura/>
             mithyācāreṇa yāḥ strīṇāṃ praduṣṭenārtavena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.6ab"> jāyante bījadoṣāc ca
            <caesura/>
             daivāc ca śṛṇu tāḥ pṛthak |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.6cd"> udāvartā tathā vandhyā viplutā ca pariplutā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.7"> vātalā ceti vātotthāḥ pittotthā rudhirakṣarā |
            <caesura/>
             vāminī snāṃsinī cāpi putraghnī pittalā ca yā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.8"> atyānandā ca yā yoniḥ karṇinī caraṇādvayam |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmalā ca kaphāj jñeyā ṣaṇḍākhyā phalinī tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.9ab"> mahatī sūcivaktrā ca sarvajeti tridoṣajā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.9cd">saphenilam udāvartā rajaḥ kṛcchreṇa muñcati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.10"> vandhyāṃ naṣṭārtavāṃ vidyād viplutāṃ nityavedanām |
            <caesura/>
             pariplutāyāṃ bhavati grāmyadharme rujā bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.11"> vātalā karkaśā stabdhā śūlanistodapīḍitā |
            <caesura/>
             catasṛṣv api cādyāsu bhavanty anilavedanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.12"> sadāhaṃ prakṣaratyasraṃ yasyāṃ sā lohitakṣarā |
            <caesura/>
             savātam udgired bījaṃ vāminī rajasā yutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.13"> prasraṃsinī syandate tu kṣobhitā duḥprasūś ca yā |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaṃ sthitaṃ hanti garbhaṃ putraghnī raktasaṃsravāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.14"> atyarthaṃ pittalā yonir dāhapākajvarānvitā |
            <caesura/>
             catasṛṣv api cādyāsu pittaliṅgocchrayo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.15"> atyānandā na santoṣaṃ grāmyadharmeṇa gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             karṇinyāṃ karṇikā yonau śleṣmāsṛgbhyāṃ prajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.16"> maithune 'caraṇā pūrvaṃ puruṣād atiricyate |
            <caesura/>
             bahuśaś cāticaraṇād anyā bījaṃ na vindati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.17"> śleṣmalā picchilā yoniḥ kaṇḍūyuktātiśītalā |
            <caesura/>
             catasṛṣv api cādy āsu śleṣmaliṅgocchritir bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.18"> anārtavastanā ṣaṇḍī kharasparśā ca maithune |
            <caesura/>
             atikāyagṛhītāyās taruṇyāḥ phalinī bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.19"> vivṛtātimahāyoniḥ sūcīvaktrātisaṃvṛtā |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaliṅgasamutthānā sarvadoṣaprakopajā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.20"> catasṛṣv api cādyāsu sarvaliṅgocchritir bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             pañcāsādhyā bhavantīmā yonayaḥ sarvadoṣajāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.21"> pratidoṣaṃ tu sādhyāsu snehādikrama iṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             dadyād uttarabastīṃś ca viśeṣeṇa yathoditān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.22"> karkaśāṃ śītalāṃ stabdhām alpasparśāṃ ca maithune |
            <caesura/>
             kumbhīsvedair upacaret sānūpaudakasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.23"> madhurauṣadhasaṃyuktān veśavārāṃś ca yoniṣu |
            <caesura/>
             nikṣiped dhārayec cāpi picutailam atandritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.24"> dhāvanāni ca pathyāni kurvītāpūraṇāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             oṣacoṣānvitāsūktaṃ kuryāc chītaṃ vidhiṃ bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.25"> durgandhāṃ picchilāṃ cāpi cūrṇaiḥ pañcakaṣāyajaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrayed rājavṛkṣādikaṣāyaiś cāpi dhāvanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.26"> yonyāṃ tu pūyasrāviṇyāṃ śodhanadravyasaṃbhṛtaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sagomūtraiḥ salavaṇaiḥ śodhanaṃ hitam iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.27"> bṛhatīphalakalkasya dviharidrāyutasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇḍūmatīm alpasparśāṃ pūrayed dhūpayet tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.28"> vartiṃ pradadyāt karṇinyāṃ śodhanadravyasaṃbhṛtām |
            <caesura/>
             prasraṃsinīṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ kṣīrasvinnāṃ praveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.29"> pidhāya veśavāreṇa tato bandhaṃ samācaret |
            <caesura/>
             pratidoṣaṃ vidadhyāc ca surāriṣṭāsavān bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.30"> prātaḥ prātarniṣeveta rasonāduddhṛtaṃ rasam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīramāṃsarasaprāyam āhāraṃ vidadhīta ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.31"> śukrārtavādayo doṣāḥ stanarogāś ca kīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             klaibyasthānāni mūḍhasya garbhasya vidhir eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.38.32"> garbhiṇī prati rogeṣu cikitsā cāpy udāhṛtā |
            <caesura/>
             sarvathā tāṃ prayuñjīta yonivyāpatsu buddhimān |
            <caesura/>
             apaprajātā<pc> </pc>rogāṃś ca cikitsed uttarād bhiṣak ||</l>
          <p xml:id="trailer.6.38">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
            yonivyāpatpratiṣedho nāma (dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, ādito ')aṣṭatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||38 ||
            <caesura/>
             uttaratantre dvitīyaṃ kaumāratantraṃ samāptam ||2 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1"> athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3.1"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3"> yenāmṛtam apāṃ madhyād uddhṛtaṃ pūrvajanmani |
            <caesura/>
             yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4"> śiṣyās taṃ devam āsīnaṃ papracchuḥ suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5"> samāsād vyāsataś caiva brūhi no bhiṣajāṃ vara |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6"> upadravās tu vraṇinaḥ kṛcchrasādhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7ab"> tasmād upadravān kṛtsnān brūhi naḥ sacikitsitān |
          </l>
          
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7cd"> 
             sarvakāyacikitsāsu ye dṛṣṭāḥ paramarṣiṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8"> teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajāṃ varaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9"> rudrakopāgnisaṃbhūtaḥ sarvabhūtapratāpanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tais tair nāmabhir anyeṣāṃ sattvānāṃ parikīrtyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10"> janmādau nidhane caiva prāyo viśati dehinam |
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvavikārāṇām ayaṃ rājā prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11"> ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyo viṣahate tu tam |
            <caesura/>
             karmaṇā labhate yasmād devatvaṃ mānusād api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.12"> punaś caiva cyutaḥ svargān mānuṣyam anuvartate |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt te devabhāvena sahante mānuṣā jvaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13"> śeṣāḥ sarve vipadyante tairyagyonā jvarārditāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svedāvarodhaḥ santāpaḥ sarvāṅgagrahaṇaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14"> vikārā yugapad yasmin jvaraḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaiḥ pṛthak samastaiś ca dvandvair āgantur eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.15"> anekakāraṇotpannaḥ smṛtas tv aṣṭavidho jvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ prakupitāḥ sveṣu kāleṣu svaiḥ prakopaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.16"> vyāpya deham aśeṣeṇa jvaram āpādayanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭāḥ svahetubhir doṣāḥ prāpyām āśayam ūṣmaṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.17"> sahitā rasam āgatya rasasvedapravāhiṇām |
            <caesura/>
             srotasāṃ mārgam āvṛtya mandīkṛtya hutāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.18"> nirasya bahir ūṣmāṇaṃ paktisthānāc ca kevalam |
            <caesura/>
             śarīraṃ samabhivyāpya svakāleṣu jvarāgamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19ab"> janayaty atha vṛddhiṃ vā svavarṇaṃ ca tvagādiṣu |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19cd"> mithyāti<pc> </pc>yuktair api ca snehādyaiḥ karmabhir nṛṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.20"> vividhād abhighātāc ca rogotthānāt prapākataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śramāt kṣayād ajīrṇāc ca viṣāt sātmyartuparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.21"> oṣadhīpuṣpagandhāc ca śokān nakṣatrapīḍayā |
            <caesura/>
             abhicārābhiśāpābhyāṃ manobhūtābhiśaṅkayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.22"> strīṇām apaprajātānāṃ prajātānāṃ tathāhitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             stanyāvataraṇe caiva jvaro doṣaiḥ pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.23"> tair vegavadbhir bahudhā samudbhrāntair vimārgagaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vikṣipyamāṇo 'ntaragnir bhavaty āśu bahiś caraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.24"> ruṇaddhi cāpy apāṃ dhātuṃ yasmāt tasmāj jvarāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhavaty atyuṣṇagātraś ca jvaritastena cocyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.25"> śramo 'ratirvivarṇatvaṃ vairasyaṃ nayanaplavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             icchādveṣau muhuś cāpi śītavātātapādiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.26"> jṛmbhāṅgamardo gurutā romaharṣo 'rucis tamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apraharṣaś ca śītaṃ ca bhavaty utpatsyati jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.27"> sāmānyato viśeṣāt tu jṛmbhātyarthaṃ samīraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             pittānnayanayor dāhaḥ kaphānnannābhinandanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.28"> sarvaliṅgasamavāyaḥ sarvadoṣaprakopaje |
            <caesura/>
             dvayor dvayos tu rūpeṇa saṃsṛṣṭaṃ dvandvajaṃ viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.29"> vepathur viṣamo vegaḥ kaṇṭhauṣṭhapariśoṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             nidrānāśaḥ kṣutaḥ stambho gātrāṇāṃ raukṣyam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.30"> śirohṛdgātrarugvaktravairasyaṃ baddhaviṭkatā |
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbhādhmānṃa tathā śūlaṃ bhavaty anilaje jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.31"> vegastīkṣṇo 'tisāraś ca nidrālpatvaṃ tathā vamiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhauṣṭhamukhanāsānāṃ pākaḥ svedaś ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.32"> pralāpaḥ kaṭutā vaktre mūrcchā dāho madastṛṣā |
            <caesura/>
             pītaviṇmūtranetratvaṃ paittike bhrama eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.33"> gauravaṃ śītamutkleśo romaharṣo 'tinidratā |
            <caesura/>
             srotorodho rugalpatvaṃ praseko madhurāsyatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.34"> nātyuṣṇagātratā chardiraṅgasādo 'vipākatā |
            <caesura/>
             pratiśyāyo 'ruciḥ kāsaḥ kaphaje 'kṣṇoś ca śuklatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.35"> nidrānāśo bhramaḥ śvāsastandrā suptāṅgatāruciḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇā moho madaḥ stambho dāhaḥ śītaṃ hṛdi vyathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.36"> paktiś cireṇa doṣāṇāmunmādaḥ śyāvadantatā |
            <caesura/>
             rasanā paruṣā kṛṣṇā sandhimūrdhāsthijā rujaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.37"> nirbhugne kaluṣe netre karṇau śabdaruganvitau |
            <caesura/>
             pralāpaḥ srotasāṃ pākaḥ kūjanaṃ cetanācyutiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.38"> svedamūtrapurīṣāṇām alpaśaḥ sucirāt srutiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaje sarvaliṅgāni viśeṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.39"> nātyuṣṇaśīto 'lpasaṃjño bhrāntaprekṣī hatasvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kharajihvaḥ śuṣkakaṇṭhaḥ svedaviṇmūtravarjitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.40"> sāsro nirbhugnahṛdayo bhaktadveṣī hataprabhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śvasannipatitaḥ śete pralāpopadravāyutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.41"> tam abhinyāsam ity āhur hataujasam athāpare |
            <caesura/>
             sannipātajvaraṃ kṛcchram asādhyam apare viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.42"> nidropetam abhinyāsaṃ kṣīṇamenaṃ hataujasam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃnyastagātraṃ saṃnyāsaṃ vidyāt sarvātmake jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.43"> ojo visraṃsate yasya pittānilasamucchrayāt |
            <caesura/>
             sa gātrastambhaśītābhyāṃ śayanepsuracetanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.44"> api jāgrat svapan jantustandrāluś ca pralāpavān |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā srastāṅgo mandasantāpavedanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.45"> ojonirodhajaṃ tasya jānīyāt kuśalo bhis ak |
            <caesura/>
             saptame vidase prāpte daśame dvādaśe 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.46"> punar dhorataro bhūtvā praśamaṃ yāti hanti vā |
            <caesura/>
             dvidoṣocchrāyaliṅgās tu dvandvajās trividhāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.47"> tṛṣṇā mūrcchā bhramo dāhaḥ svapnanāśaḥ śirorujā |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhāsyaśoṣo vamathū romaharṣo 'rucis tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.48"> parvbhedaś ca jṛmbhā ca vātapittajvarākṛtiḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.317"> paittike madhurais tiktaiḥ siddhaṃ sarpiś ca pūjyate |
            <caesura/>
             ślaiṣmike kaṭutiktaiś ca saṃsṛṣṭānītareṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.318"> hṛtāvaśeṣaṃ pittaṃ tu tvaksthaṃ janayati jvaram |
            <caesura/>
             pibed ikṣurasaṃ tatra śītaṃ vā śarkarodakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.319"> śāliṣaṣṭikayor annam aśnīyāt kṣīrasaṃplutam |
            <caesura/>
             kaphavātotthayor eva svedābhyaṅgau prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.320"> ghṛtaṃ dvādaśarātrāt tu deyaṃ sarvajvareṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             tenāntareṇāśayaṃ svaṃ gatā doṣā bhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.321"> dhānūn prakṣobhayan doṣo mokṣakāle balīyate |
            <caesura/>
             tena vyākulacittas tu mriyamāṇa ivehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.322"> laghutvaṃ śirasaḥ svedo mukhamāpāṇḍu pāki ca |
            <caesura/>
             kṣavathuś cānnakāṅkṣā ca jvaram uktasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.323"> śambhukrodhodbhavo ghoro balavarṇāgnisādakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rogarāṭ roghasaṃghāto jvara ity upadiśyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.324"> vyāpitvāt sarvasaṃsparśāt kṛcchratvād antasaṃbhavāt |
            <caesura/>
             antako hyeṣa bhūtānāṃ jvara ity upadiśyate ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            jvarapratiṣedho nāma (prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ādita) ekonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||39 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.1"> athāto 'tīsārapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.3"> gurvatisnigdharūkṣoṣṇadravasthūlātiśītalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇairasātmyaiś cāpi bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.4"> snehādyairatiyuktaiś ca mithyāyuktairviṣādbhayāt |
            <caesura/>
             śokādduṣṭāmbumadyātipānāt sātmyartuparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.5"> jalātiramaṇairvegavighātaiḥ kṛmidoṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nṛṇāṃ bhavaty atīsāro lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.6"> saṃśamyāpāṃdhāturantaḥ kṛśānuṃ varcomiśro mārutena praṇunnaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddho 'tīvādhaḥ saratyeṣa yasmādvyādhiṃ ghoraṃ taṃ tvatīsāram āhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.7"> ekaikaśaḥ sarvaśaś cāpi doṣaiḥ śokenānyaḥ ṣaṣṭha āmena coktaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kecit prāhurnaikarūpaprakāraṃ naivety evaṃ kāśirājastvavocat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.8"> doṣāvasthāstasya naikaprakārāḥ kāle kāle vyādhitasyodbhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             hṛnnābhipāyūdarakukṣitodagātrāvasādānilasannirodhāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.9"> viṭsaṅga ādhmānamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatas tasya puraḥsarāṇi |
            <caesura/>
             śūlāviṣṭaḥ saktamūtro 'ntrakūjī srastāpānaḥ sannakaṭyūrugaṅghaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.10"> varco muñcatyalpamalpaṃ saphenaṃ rūkṣaṃ śyāvaṃ sānilaṃ mārutena |
            <caesura/>
             durgandhyuṣṇaṃ vegavanmāṃsatoyaprakhyaṃ bhinnaṃ svinnadeho 'titīkṣṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.11"> pittāt pītaṃ nīlamālohitaṃ vā tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhapākajvarārtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tandrānidrāgauravotkleśasadīvegāśaṅkī sṛṣṭaviṭko 'pi bhūyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.12"> śuklaṃ sāndraṃ śleṣmaṇā śleṣmayuktaṃ bhaktadveṣī niḥsvanaṃ
            hṛṣṭaromā |
            <caesura/>
             tandrāyukto mohasādāsyaśoṣī varcaḥ kuryānnaikavarṇaṃ tṛṣārtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.13"> sarvodbhūte sarvaliṅgopapattiḥ kṛcchraś cāyaṃ bālavṛddheṣv
            asādhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tais tairbhāvaiḥ paktimāvidhya(āviśya)jantoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.14"> koṣṭhaṃ gatvā kṣobhayatyasya raktaṃ taccādhastāt kākaṇantīprakāśam
            |
            <caesura/>
             varcomiśraṃ niḥpurīṣaṃ sagandhaṃ nirgandhaṃ vā sāryate tena kṛcchrāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.15"> śokotpanno duścikitsyo 'timātraṃ rogo vaidyaiḥ kaṣṭa eṣa pradiṣṭaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             āmājīrṇopadrutāḥ kṣobhayantaḥ koṣṭhaṃ doṣāḥ saṃpraduṣṭāḥ sabhaktam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.16"> nānāvarṇaṃ naikaśaḥ sārayanti kṛcchrājjantoḥ ṣaṣṭhamenaṃ vadanti | </l>
          <l/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.17"> saṃsṛṣṭamebhir doṣaistu nyastamapsvavasīdati |
            <caesura/>
             purīṣaṃ bhṛśadurgandhi vicchinnaṃ cāmasaṃjñakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.18"> etānyeva tu liṅgāni viparītāni yasya tu |
            <caesura/>
             lāghavaṃ ca manuṣyasya tasya pakvaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.19"> sarpirbhedovesavārāmbutailamajjākṣīrakṣaudrarūpaṃ sravedyat |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhābhaṃ mastuluṅgopamaṃ vā visraṃ śītaṃ pretagandhyañjanābham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.20"> rājīmadvā candrakaiḥ santataṃ vā pūyaprakhyaṃ kardamābhaṃ
            tathoṣṇam |
            <caesura/>
             hanyādetadyat pratīpaṃ bhavec ca kṣīṇaṃ hanyuś copasargāḥ prabhūtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.21"> asaṃvṛtagudaṃ kṣīṇaṃ durādhmātam upadrutam |
            <caesura/>
             gude pakve gatoṣmāṇamatīsārakiṇaṃ tyajet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.22"> śarīriṇāmatīsāraḥ saṃbhūto yena kenacit |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāṇām eva liṅgāni kadācinnātivartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.23"> snehājīrṇanimittas tu bahuśūlapravāhikaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             visūcikānimittas tu cānyo 'jīrṇanimittajaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viṣārśaḥkṛmisaṃmūto yathāsvaṃ doṣalakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.24"> āmapakvakramaṃ hitvā nātisāre kriyā yataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarve 'tisārās tu jñeyāḥ pakvāmalakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.25"> tatrādau laṅghanaṃ kāryamatisāreṣu dehinām |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ pācanasaṃyukto yavāgvādikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.26"> athavā vāmayitvāme śūlādhmānanipīḍitam |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīsaindhavāmbhobhir laṅghanādyair upācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.27"> kāryaṃ ca vamanasyānte pradravaṃ laghubhojanam |
            <caesura/>
             khaḍayūṣayavāgūṣu pippalyādyaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.28"> anena vidhinā cāmaṃ yasya vai nopaśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             haridrādiṃ vacādiṃ vā pibet prātaḥ sa mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.29"> āmātīsāriṇāṃ kāryaṃ nādau saṃgrahaṇaṃ nṛṇām |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāṃ doṣā vibaddhāḥ prāgjanayanty āmayānimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.30"> plīhapāṇḍvāmayānāhamehakuṣṭhodarajvarān |
            <caesura/>
             śophagulmagrahaṇyarśaḥśūlālasakahṛdgrahān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.31"> saśūlaṃ bahuśaḥ kṛcchrādvibaddhaṃ yo 'tisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             doṣān sannicitān tasya pathyābhiḥ saṃpravartayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.32"> yo 'tidravaṃ prabhūtaṃ ca purīṣamatisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             tasyādau vamanaṃ kuryāt paś cāllaṅghanapācanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.33"> stokaṃ stokaṃ vibaddhaṃ vā saśūlaṃ yo 'tisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             abhayāpippalīkalkaiḥ sukhoṣṇais taṃ virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.34"> āme ca laṅghanaṃ śastamādau pācanam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             yogāś cātra pravakṣyante tvāmātīsāranāśanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.35"> kaliṅgātiviṣāhiṅgusauvarcalavacābhayāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             devadāruvacāmustānāgarātiviṣābhayāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.36"> abhayā dhānyakaṃ mustaṃ pippalī nāgaraṃ vacā |
            <caesura/>
             nāgaraṃ dhānyakaṃ mustaṃ vālakaṃ bilvam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.37"> mustaṃ parpaṭakaṃ śuṇṭhī vacā prativiṣābhayā |
            <caesura/>
             abhayātiviṣā hiṅgu vacā sauvarcalaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.38"> citrakaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ vacā kaṭukarohiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhā vatsakabījāni harītakyo mahauṣadham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.39"> mūrvā nirdahanī pāṭhā tryūṣaṇaṃ gajapippalī |
            <caesura/>
             siddhārthakā bhadradāru śatāhvā kaṭurohiṇī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.40"> elā sāvarakaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ haridre kauṭajā yavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             meṣaśṛṅgī tvagele ca kṛmighnaṃ vṛkṣakāṇi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.41"> vṛkṣādanī vīratarurbṛhatyau dve sahe tathā |
            <caesura/>
             aralutvak taindukī ca dāḍimī kauṭajī śamī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.42"> pāṭhā tejovatī mustaṃ pippalī kauṭajaṃ phalam |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolaṃ(paṭolī) dīpyako bilvaṃ haridre devadāru ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.43"> viḍaṅgamabhayā pāṭhā śṛṅgaveraṃ ghanaṃ vacā |
            <caesura/>
             vacā vatsakabījāni saindhavaṃ kaṭurohiṇī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.44"> hiṅgurvatsakabījāni vacā bilvaśalāṭu ca |
            <caesura/>
             nāgarātiviṣe mustaṃ pippalyo vātsakaṃ phalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.45"> mahauṣadhaṃ prativiṣā mustaṃ cetyāmapācanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prayojyā viṃśatiryogāḥ ślokārdhavihitāstvime || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.46"> dhānyāmloṣṇāmbumadyānāṃ pibedanyatamena vā |
            <caesura/>
             niṣkvāthān vā pibedeṣāṃ sukhoṣṇān sādhu sādhitān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.47"> payasyutkvāthya mustānāṃ viṃśatiṃ triguṇāmbhasi |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīrāvaśiṣṭaṃ tatpītaṃ hantyāmaṃ śūlam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.48"> nikhilenopadiṣṭo 'yaṃ vidhirāmopaśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             harītakīmativiṣāṃ hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ vacām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.49"> pibet sukhāmbunā janturāmātisārapīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolaṃ dīpyakaṃ bilvaṃ vacāpippalināgaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.50"> mustaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca pibedvāpi sukhāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             śṛṅgaveraṃ guḍūcīṃ ca pibeduṣṇena vāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.51"> lavaṇānyatha pippalyo viḍaṅgāni harītakī |
            <caesura/>
             citrakaṃ śiṃśapā pāṭhā śārṅgeṣṭā lavaṇāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.52"> hiṅgurvṛkṣakabījāni lavaṇāni ca bhāgaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hastidantyatha pippalyaḥ kalkāvakṣasamau smṛtau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.53"> vacā guḍūcīkāṇḍāni yogo 'yaṃ paramo mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ete sukhāmbunā yogā deyāḥ paś ca satāṃ matāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.54"> nivṛtteṣvāmaśūleṣu yasya na praguṇo 'nilaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             stokaṃ stokaṃ rujāmac ca saśūlaṃ yo 'tisāryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.55"> sakṣāralavaṇairyuktaṃ mandāgniḥ sa pibed ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīranāgaracāṅgarīkoladadhyamlasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.56"> sarpiracchaṃ pibedvāpi śūlātīsāraśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā tailaghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ savyoṣājāticitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.57"> sabilvapippalīmūladāḍimair vā ruganvitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nikhilo vidhirukto 'yaṃ vātaśleṣmopaśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.58"> tīkṣṇoṣṇavarjyamenaṃ tu vidadhyātpittaje bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             yathoktam upavāsānte yavāgūś ca praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.59"> balayor aṃśumatyāṃ ca śvadaṃṣṭrabṛhatīṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             śatāvaryāṃ ca saṃsiddhāḥ suśītā madhusaṃyutāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.60"> mudgādiṣu ca yūṣāḥ syurdravyairetaiḥ susaṃskṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdubhir dīpanaistiktairdravyaiḥ syādāmapācanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.61"> haridrātiviṣāpāṭhāvatsabījarasāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             rasāñjanaṃ haridre dve bījāni kuṭajasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.62"> pāṭhā guḍūcī bhūnimbas tathaiva kaṭurohiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             etaiḥ ślokārdhanirdiṣṭaiḥ kvāthāḥ syuḥ pittapācanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.63"> mustaṃ kuṭajabījāni bhūnimbaṃ sarasāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             dārvī durālabhā bilvaṃ vālakaṃ raktacandanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.64"> candanaṃ vālakaṃ mustaṃ bhūnimbaṃ sadurālabham |
            <caesura/>
             mṛṇālaṃ candanaṃ rodhraṃ nāgaraṃ nīlamutpalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.65"> pāṭhā mustaṃ haridre dve pippalī kauṭajaṃ phalam |
            <caesura/>
             phalatvacaṃ vatsakasya śṛṅgaveraṃ ghanaṃ vacā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.66"> ṣaḍete 'bhihitā yogāḥ pittātīsāranāśanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bilvaśakrayavāmbhodabālakātiviṣākṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyo hantyatīsāraṃ sāmaṃ pittasamudbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.67"> madhukotpalabilvābdahrīberośīranāgaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtaḥ kvātho madhuyutaḥ pittātīsāranāśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.68"> yadā pakvo 'pyatīsāraḥ sarasyeva muhurmuhuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             grahaṇyā mārdavājjantos tatra saṃstambhanaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.69"> samaṅgā dhātakīpuṣpaṃ mañjiṣṭhā lodhramustakam |
            <caesura/>
             śālmalīveṣṭako rodhraṃ vṛkṣadāḍimayostvacau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.70"> āmrāsthimadhyaṃ lodhraṃ ca bilvamadhyaṃ priyaṅgavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhukaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ ca dīrghavṛntatvageva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.71"> catvāra ete yogāḥ syuḥ pakvātīsāranāśanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uktā ya upayojyāste sakṣaudrāstaṇḍulāmbunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.72"> maustaṃ kaṣāyamekaṃ vā peyaṃ madhusamāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             lodhrāmbaṣṭhāpriyaṅgvādīn gaṇānevaṃ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.73"> padmāṃ samaṅgāṃ madhukaṃ bilvajambūśalāṭu ca |
            <caesura/>
             pibettaṇḍulatoyena sakṣaudramagadaṅkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.74"> kacchurāmūlakalkaṃ vāpy udumbaraphalopamam |
            <caesura/>
             payasyā candanaṃ padmā sitāmustābjakeśaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.75"> pakvātisāraṃ yogo 'yaṃ jayetpītaḥ saśoṇitam |
            <caesura/>
             nirāmarūpaṃ śūlārtaṃ laṅghanādyaiś ca karṣitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.76"> naraṃ rūkṣamavekṣyāgniṃ sakṣāraṃ pāyayed ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             balābṛhatyaṃśumatīkacchurāmūlasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.77"> madhūkṣitaṃ samadhukaṃ pibec chūlairabhidrutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dārvībilvakaṇādrākṣākaṭukendrayavairghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.78"> sādhitaṃ hantyatīsāraṃ vātapittakaphātmakam |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā cāmlena saṃpakvaṃ savyoṣājājicitrakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.79"> sacavyapippalīmūlaṃ dāḍimair vā rugarditaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             payo ghṛtaṃ ca madhu ca pibec chūlairabhidrutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.80"> sitājamodakaṭvaṅgamadhukairavacūrṇitam |
            <caesura/>
             avedanaṃ susaṃpakvaṃ dīptāgneḥ sucirotthitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.81"> nānāvarṇamatīsāraṃ puṭapākair upācaret |
            <caesura/>
             tvakpiṇḍaṃ dīrghavṛntasya padmakesarasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.82"> kāśmarīpadmapatraiś cāveṣṭya sūtreṇa saṃdṛḍham |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdāvaliptaṃ sukṛtamaṅgāreṣv avakūlayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.83"> svinnamuddhṛtya niṣpīḍya rasamādāya taṃ tataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītaṃ madhuyutaṃ kṛtvā pāyayetodarāmaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.84"> jīvantīmeṣaśṛṅgyādiṣvevaṃ dravyeṣu sādhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tittiriṃ luñcitaṃ samyak niṣkṛṣṭāntraṃ tu pūrayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.85"> nyagrodhāditvacāṃ kalkaiḥ pūrvavaccāvakūlayet |
            <caesura/>
             rasamādāya tasyātha susvinnasya samākṣikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.86"> śarkaropahitaṃ śītaṃ pāyayetodarāmaye |
            <caesura/>
             lodhracandanayaṣṭyāhvadārvīpāṭhāsitotpalān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.87"> taṇḍulodakasṃpiṣṭān dīrghavṛntatvaganvitān |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvavat kūlitāt tasmād rasamādāya śītalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.88"> madhvāktaṃ pāyayec caitat kaphapittodarāmaye |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ prarohaiḥ kurvīta vaṭādīnaṃ vidhānavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.89"> puṭapākān yathāyogaṃ jāṅgalopahitān śubhān |
            <caesura/>
             bahuśleṣma saraktaṃ ca mandavātaṃ cirotthitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.90"> kauṭajaṃ phāṇitaṃ vāpi hantyatīsāramojasā |
            <caesura/>
             ambaṣṭhādimadhuyutaṃ pippalyādisamanvitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.91"> pṛśniparṇībalābilvavālakotpaladhānyakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sanāgaraiḥ pibet peyāṃ sādhitāmudarāmayī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.92"> aralutvak priyaṅguṃ ca madhukaṃ dāḍimāṅkurān |
            <caesura/>
             āvāpya piṣṭvā dadhani yavāgūṃ sādhayed dravām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.93"> eṣā sarvānatīsārān hanti pakvānasaṃśayam |
            <caesura/>
             rasāñjanaṃ sātiviṣaṃ tvagbījaṃ kauṭajaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.94"> dhātakī nāgaraṃ caiva pāyayettaṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ raktajaṃ ghnanti ete madhusamāyutāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.95"> madhukaṃ bilvapeśī ca śarkarāmadhusaṃyutā |
            <caesura/>
             atīsāraṃ nihanyuś ca śāliṣaṣṭikayoḥ kaṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.96"> tad vallīḍhaṃ madhuyutaṃ badarīmūlam eva tu |
            <caesura/>
             badaryarjunajambvāmraśallakīvetasatvacaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.97"> śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyuktāḥ pītā ghnantyudarāmayam |
            <caesura/>
             etair eva yavāgūṃś ca ṣaḍān yūṣāṃś ca kārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.98"> pānīyāni ca tṛṣṇāsu dravyeṣveteṣu buddhimān |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtaṃ śālmalivṛnteṣu kaṣāyaṃ himasaṃjñitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.99"> niśāparyuṣitaṃ peyaṃ sakṣaudraṃ madhukānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             vibaddhavātaviṭ śūlaparītaḥ sapravāhikaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.100"> saraktapittaś ca payaḥ pibettṛṣṇāsamanvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathāmṛtaṃ yathā kṣīramatīsāreṣu pūjitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.101"> cirotthiteṣu tat peyamapāṃ bhāgaistribhiḥ śṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaśeṣaṃ harettaddhi tasmāt pathyatamaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.102"> hitaḥ snehavireko vā bastayaḥ picchilāś ca ye |
            <caesura/>
             picchilasvarase siddhaṃ hitaṃ ca ghṛtam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.103"> śakṛtā yas tu saṃsṛṣṭamatisāryeta śoṇitam |
            <caesura/>
             prāk paścād vā purīṣasya saruk saparikartikaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.104"> kṣīriśuṅgāśṛtaṃ sarpiḥ pibet sakṣaudraśarkaram |
            <caesura/>
             dārvītvakpippalīśuṇṭhīlākṣāśakrayavairghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.105"> saṃyuktaṃ bhadrarohiṇyā pakvaṃ peyādimiśritam |
            <caesura/>
             tridoṣam apy atīsāraṃ pītaṃ hanti sudāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.106"> gaurave vamanaṃ pathyaṃ yasya syāt prabalaḥ kaphaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jvare dāhe saviṅbandhe mārutādraktapittavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.107"> saṃpakve bahudoṣe ca vibandhe mūtraśodhanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kāryamāsthāpanaṃ kṣipraṃ tathā caivānuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.108"> pravāhaṇe gudabhraṃśe mūtrāghāte kaṭigrahe |
            <caesura/>
             madhurāmlaiḥ śṛtaṃ tailaṃ sarpir vāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.109"> gudapākas tu pittena yasya syādahitāśinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya pittaharāḥ sekāstatsiddhāś cānuvāsanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.110"> dadhimaṇḍasurābilvasiddhaṃ tailaṃ samārute |
            <caesura/>
             bhojane ca hitaṃ kṣīraṃ kacchurāmūlasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.111"> alpālpaṃ bahuśo raktaṃ sarugya upaveśyate |
            <caesura/>
             yadā vāyur vibaddhaś ca picchābastis tadā hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.112"> prāyeṇa gudadaurbalyaṃ dīrghakālātisāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             bhavettasmād dhitaṃ teṣāṃ gude tailāvacāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.113"> kapitthaśālmalīphañjīvaṭakārpāsadāḍimāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yūthikā kacchurā śeluḥ śaṇaś cuccūś ca dādhikāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.114"> śālaparṇī pṛśniparṇī bṛhatī kaṇṭakārikā |
            <caesura/>
             balāśvadaṃṣṭrābilvāni pāṭhānāgaradhānyakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.115"> eṣa āhārasaṃyoge hitaḥ sarvātisāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tilakalko hitaś cātra maudgo mudgarasas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.116"> pittātisārī yo martyaḥ pittalāny atiṣevate |
            <caesura/>
             pittaṃ praduṣṭaṃ tasyāśu raktātīsārabhāvahet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.117"> jvaraṃ śūlaṃ tṛṣāṃ dāhaṃ gudapākaṃ ca dāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             yo raktaṃ śakṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ paścād vā pratisāryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.118"> sa pallavairvaṭādīnaṃ sasarpiḥ sādhitaṃ payaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pibet saśarkarākṣaudramathavāpyabhimathya tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.119"> navanītamatho lihyāttakraṃ cānupibettataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             priyālaśālmalīplakṣaśallakītiniśatvacaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.120"> kṣīre vimṛditāḥ pītāḥ sakṣaudrā raktanāśanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhukaṃ śarkarāṃ lodhraṃ payasyāmatha sārivām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.121"> pibec chāgena payasā sakṣaudraṃ raktanāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhāṃ sārivāṃ lodhraṃ padmakaṃ kumudotpalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.122"> pibet padmāṃ ca dugdhena chāgenāsṛkpraśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarotpalalodhrāṇi samaṅgā madhukaṃ tilāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.123"> tilāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ sayaṣṭyāhvāḥ samaṅgā cotpalāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             tilā mocaraso lodhraṃ tathaiva madhukotpalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.124"> kacchurā tilakalkaś ca yogāś catvāra eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             ājena payasā peyāḥ sarakte madhusaṃyutāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.125"> drave sarakte sravati bālabilvaṃ saphāṇitam |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudratailaṃ prāgeva lihyādāśu hitaṃ hi tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.126"> kośakāraṃ ghṛte bhṛṣṭaṃ lājacūrṇaṃ sitā madhu |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ raktapittotthaṃ līḍhaṃ hantyudarāmayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.127"> bilvamadhyaṃ samadhukaṃ śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyuto yogaḥ pittaraktotthitaṃ jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.128"> yogān sāṃgrāhikāṃś cānyān pibetsakṣaudraśarkarān |
            <caesura/>
             nyagrodhādiṣu kuryāc ca puṭapākān yatheritān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.129"> gudāpāke ca ye uktāste 'trāpi vidhayaḥ smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rujāyāṃ cāpraśāmyantyāṃ picchāvastirhito bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.130"> saktaviḍ doṣabahulaṃ dīptāgniryo 'tisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgatriphalākṛṣṇākaṣāyais taṃ virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.131"> athavairaṇḍasiddhena payasā kevalena vā |
            <caesura/>
             yavāgūrvitareccāsya vātaghnairdīpanaiḥ kṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.132"> dīptāgnirniṣpurīṣo yaḥ sāryate phenilaṃ śakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             sa pibet phāṇitaṃ śuṇṭhīdadhitailapayoghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.133"> svinnāni guḍatailābhyāṃ bhakṣayed badarāṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             svinnāni piṣṭavadvāpi samaṃ bilvaśalāṭubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.134"> dadhnopayujya kulmāṣān śvetāmanupibet surām |
            <caesura/>
             śaśamāṃsaṃ sarudhiraṃ samaṅgāṃ saghṛtaṃ dadhi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.135"> khādedvipācya seveta mṛdvannaṃ śakṛtaḥ kṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             saṃskṛto yamake māṣayavakolarasaḥ śubhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.136"> bhojanārthaṃ pradātavyo dadhidāḍimasādhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṃ bilvaśalāṭūni nāgaraṃ cāmlapeṣitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.137"> dadhnaḥ saraś ca yamake bhṛṣṭo varcaḥkṣaye hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ kṣīṇavarcā yo dīptāgniratisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             sa pibeddīpanairyuktaṃ sarpiḥ saṃgrāhakaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.138"> vāyuḥ pravṛddho nicitaṃ balāsaṃ nudatyadhastādahitāśanasya |
            <caesura/>
             pravāhamāṇasya muhurmalāktaṃ pravāhikāṃ tāṃ pravadanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.139"> pravāhikā vātakṛtā saśūlā pittāt sadāhā sakaphā kaphāc ca |
            <caesura/>
             saśoṇitā śoṇitasaṃbhavā tu tāḥ sneharūkṣaprabhavā matās tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.140"> tāsāmatīsāravadādiśec ca liṅgaṃ kramaṃ cāmavipakvatāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             na śāntimāyāti vilaṅghanairyā yogair udīrṇā yadi pācanair vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.141"> tāṃ kṣīramevāśu śṛtaṃ nihanti tailaṃ tilāḥ picchilabastayaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             ārdraiḥ kuśaiḥ saṃpariveṣṭitāni vṛntānyathārdrāṇi hi śālmalīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.142"> pkvāni samyak puṭapākayogenāpothya tebhyo rasamādadīta |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ tailahavirvimiśraṃ kalkena yaṣṭīmadhukasya vāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.143"> bastiṃ vidadhyādbhiṣagapramattaḥ pravāhikāmūtrapurīṣasaṅge |
            <caesura/>
             dvipañjcamūlīkvathitena śūle pravāhamāṇasya samākṣikeṇa || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.144"> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanamagryamuktaṃ tailena yuñjyādanuvāsanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnavarge lavaṇeṣu caiva tailaṃ ca siddhaṃ hitamannapāne || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.145"> lodhraṃ viḍaṃ bilvaśalāṭu caiva lihyāc ca tailena kaṭutrikāḍhyam
            |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā sasāreṇa samākṣikeṇa bhuñjīta niś cāraka(niḥsāraka))pīḍitas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.146"> sutaptakupyakvathitena vāpi kṣīreṇa śītena madhuplutena |
            <caesura/>
             śūlārdito vyoṣavidārigandhāsiddhena dugdhena hitāya bhojyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.147"> vātaghnasaṃgrāhikadīpanīyaiḥ kṛtān ṣaḍāṃś cāpy upabhojayec ca |
            <caesura/>
             khādec ca matsyān rasamāpnuyāc ca vātaghnasiddhaṃ saghṛtaṃ satailam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.148"> eṇāvyajānāṃ tu vaṭapravālaiḥ siddhāni sārdhaṃ piśitāni khādet |
            <caesura/>
             medhyasya(medyasya) siddhaṃ tvatha vāpi raktaṃ bastasya dadhnā ghṛtatailayuktam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.149"> khādet pradehaiḥ śikhilāvajair vā bhuñjīta yūṣairdadhibhiś ca
            mukhyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             māṣān susiddhān ghṛtamaṇḍayuktān khādec ca dadhnā maricopadaṃśān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.150"> mahāruje mūtrakṛcchre bhiṣag bastiṃ pradāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             payomadhughṛtonmiśraṃ madhukotpalasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.151"> sa bastiḥ śamayettasya raktaṃ dāhamatho jvaram |
            <caesura/>
             madhurauṣadhasiddhaṃ ca hitaṃ tasyānuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.152"> rātrāvahani vā nityaṃ rujārto yo bhaven naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā yathā satailaḥ syādvātaśāntis tathā tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.153"> praśānte mārute cāpi śāntiṃ yāti pravāhikā |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt pravāhikāroge mārutaṃ śamayed bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.154"> pāṭhājamodākuṭajotpalaṃ ca śuṇṭhī samā māgadhikāś ca piṣṭāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sukhāmbupītāḥ śamayanti rogaṃ medhyāṇḍasiddhaṃ saghṛtaṃ payo vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.155"> śuṇṭhīṃ ghṛtaṃ sakṣavakaṃ satailaṃ vipācya līḍhvāmayamāśu hanyāt
            |
            <caesura/>
             gajāśanākumbhikadāḍimānāṃ rasaiḥ kṛtā tailaghṛte sadadhni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.156"> bilvānvitā pathyatamā yavāgūrdhāroṣṇadugdhasya tathā ca pānam |
            <caesura/>
             laghūni pathyānyatha dīpanāni snigdhāni bhojyānyudarāmayeṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.157"> hitāya nityaṃ vitaredvibhajya yogāṃś ca tāṃstān bhiṣagapramattaḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.158"> tṛṣṇāpanayanī laghvī dīpanī bastiśodhanī |
            <caesura/>
             jvare caivātisāre ca yavāgūḥ sarvadā hitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.159"> rūkṣājjāte kriyā snigdhā rūkṣā snehanimittaje |
            <caesura/>
             bhayaje sāntvanāpūrvā śokaje śokanāśinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.160"> viṣārśaḥkṛmisaṃbhūte hitā cobhayaśarmadā |
            <caesura/>
             chardimūrcchātṛḍādyāṃś ca sādhayed avirodhataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.161"> samavāye tu doṣāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ pittamupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             jvare caivātisāre ca sarvatrānyatra mārutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.162"> yasyoccāraṃ vinā mūtraṃ samyag vāyuś ca gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             dīptāgnerlaghukoṣṭhasya sthitastasyodarāmayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.163"> karmajā vyādhayaḥ keciddoṣajāḥ santi cāpare |
            <caesura/>
             karmadoṣodbhavāś cānye karmajāsteṣv ahetukāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.164"> naśyanti tvakriyābhis te kriyābhiḥ karmasaṃkṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             śāmyanti doṣasaṃbhūtā doṣasaṃkṣayahetubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.165"> teṣāmalpanidānā ye pratikaṣṭā bhavanti ca |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdavo bahudoṣā vā karmadoṣodbhavās tu te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.166"> karmadoṣakṣayakṛtā teṣāṃ siddhirvidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             duṣyati grahaṇī jantoragnisādanahetubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.167"> atisāre nivṛtte 'pi mandāgnerahitāśinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhūyaḥ saṃdūṣito vahnirgrahaṇīmabhidūṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.168"> tasmāt kāryaḥ parīhārastvatīsāre viriktavat |
            <caesura/>
             yāvan na prakṛtisthaḥ syāddoṣataḥ prāṇatas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.169"> ṣaṣṭhī pittadharā nāma yā kalā parikīrtitā |
            <caesura/>
             pakvāmāśayamadhyasthā grahaṇī sā prakīrtitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.170"> grahaṇyā balamagnirhi sa cāpi grahaṇīṃ śritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt saṃdūṣite vahnau grahaṇī saṃpraduṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.171"> ekaśaḥ sarvaśaś caiva doṣairatyarthamucchritaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sā duṣṭā bahuśo bhuktamāmam eva vimuñcati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.172"> pakvaṃ vā sarujaṃ pūti muhurbaddhaṃ muhurdravam |
            <caesura/>
             grahaṇīrogamāhustamāyurvedavido janāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.173"> tasyotpattau vidāho+āne sadanālasyatṛṭklamāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             balakṣayo 'ruciḥ kāsaḥ karṇakṣveḍo 'ntrakūjanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.174"> atha jāte bhavejjantuḥ śūnapādakaraḥ kṛśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             parvaruglaulyatṛṭchardijvarārocakadāhavām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.175"> udgirec chuktatiktāmlalohadhūmāmagandhikam |
            <caesura/>
             prasekamukhavairasyatamakārucipīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.176"> vātācchūlādhikaiḥ pāyuhṛtpārśvodaramastakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittāt sadāhairgurubhiḥ kaphāttribhyastrilakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.177"> doṣavarṇairnakhais tadvad viṇmūtranayanānanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hṛtpāṇḍūdaragulmārśaḥplīhāśaṅkhī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.178"> yathā doṣocchrayaṃ tasya viśuddhasya yathākramam |
            <caesura/>
             peyādiṃ vitaret samyag dīpanīyopasaṃbhṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.179"> tataḥ pācanasaṃgrāhidīpanīyagaṇatrayam |
            <caesura/>
             pibet prātaḥ surāriṣṭasnehamūtrasukhāmbubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.180"> takreṇa vātha takraṃ vā kevalaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmigulmodarārśoghnīḥ kriyāś cātrāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.181"> cūrṇaṃ hiṅgvādikaṃ cātra ghṛtaṃ vā plīhanāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             kalkena magadhādeś ca cāṅgerīsvarasena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.182"> caturguṇena dadhnā ca ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ hitaṃ bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             jvarādīn avirodhāc ca sādhayet svaiś cikitsitaiḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            'tisārapratiṣedho nāma (dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ/) catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||40 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="41" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.1"> athātaḥ śoṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.3"> anekarogānugato bahurogapurogamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             durvijñeyo durnivāraḥ śoṣo vyādhirmahābalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.4"> saṃśoṣaṇādrasādīnāṃ śoṣa ity abhidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             kriyākṣayakaratvāc ca kṣaya ity ucyate punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.5"> rājñaś candramaso yasmād abhūd eṣa kilāmayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt taṃ rājayakṣmeti kecidāhuḥ punarjanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.6"> sa vyastair jāyate doṣair iti kecid vadanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             ekādaśānām ekasmin sānnidhyāt tantrayuktitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.7"> kriyāṇām avibhāgena prāgekotpādanena ca |
            <caesura/>
             eka eva mataḥ śoṣaḥ sannipātātmako hy ataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.8"> udrekāttatra liṅgāni doṣāṇāṃ nipatanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             ksayādvegapratīghātādāghātādviṣamāśanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.9"> jāyate kupitairdoṣairvyāptadehasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaphapradhānairdoṣairhi ruddheṣu rasavartmasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.10"> ativyavāyino vāpi kṣīṇe retasyanantaram |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīyante dhātavaḥ sarve tataḥ śuṣyanti mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.11"> bhaktadveṣo jvaraḥ śvāsaḥ kāsaḥ śoṇitadarśanam |
            <caesura/>
             svarabhedaś ca jāyeta ṣaḍrūpe rājayakṣmaṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.12"> svarabhedo 'nilāñchūlaṃ saṃlocaś cāṃsapārśvayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jvaro dāho 'tisāraś ca pittādraktasya cāgamaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.13"> śirasaḥ paripūrṇatvamabhaktacchanda eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             kāsaḥ kaṇṭhasya coddhvaṃso vijñeyaḥ kaphakopataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.14"> ekādaśabhir ebhir vā ṣaḍbhir vāpi samanvitam |
            <caesura/>
             (kāsātīsārapārśvārtisvarabhedārucijvaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.15"> tribhir vā pīḍitaṃ liṅgairjvarakāsāsṛgāmayaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ) jahyācchoṣārditaṃ jantumicchan suvipulaṃ yaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.16"> vyāyaśokasthāviryavyāyāmadhvopavāsataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇoraḥkṣatapīḍābhyāṃ śoṣānanye vadanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.17"> vyavāyaśoṣī śukrasya kṣayaliṅgair upadrutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāṇḍudeho yathāpūrvaṃ kṣīyante cāsya dhātavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.18"> pradhyānaśīlaḥ srastāṅgaḥ śokaśoṣyapi tādṛśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vinā śukraksayakṛtairvikārairabhilakṣitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.19"> jarāśoṣī kṛśo mandavīryabuddhibalendiryaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kampano 'rucimān bhinnakāṃsyapātrahatasvaraḥ(naḥ) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.20"> ṣṭhīvati śleṣmaṇā hīnaṃ gauravārucipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃprasrutāsyanāsākṣaḥ suptarūkṣamalacchaviḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.21"> adhvapraśoṣī srastāṅgaḥ saṃbhṛṣṭaparuṣacchaviḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prasuptagātrāvayavaḥ śuṣkaklomagalānanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.22"> vyāyāmaśoṣī bhūyiṣṭhamebhir eva samanvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uraḥkṣatakṛtairliṅgaiḥ saṃyuktaś ca kṣatādvinā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.23"> raktakṣayād vedanābhis tathaivāhārayantraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇitasya bhavec choṣaḥ sa cāsādhyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.24"> vyāyāmabhārādhyayanair abhighātātimaithunaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             karmaṇā cāpy urasyena vakṣo yasya vidāritam |
            <caesura/>
             tasyor asi kṣate raktaṃ pūyaḥ śleṣmā ca gacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.25"> kāsamānaś chardayec ca pītaraktāsitāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃtaptavakṣāḥ so 'tyarthaṃ dūyanātparitāmyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.26"> durgandhavadanocchvāso bhinnavarṇasvaro naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             keṣāṃcidevaṃ śoṣo hi kāraṇairbhedamāgataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.27"> na tatra doṣaliṅgānāṃ samastānāṃ nipātanam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣayā eva hi te jñeyāḥ pratyekaṃ dhātusaṃjñitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.28"> cikitsitaṃ tu teṣāṃ hi prāguktaṃ dhātusaṃkṣaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.29">
            śvāsāṅgasādakaphasaṃsravatāluśoṣacchardyagnisādamadapīnasapāṇḍunidrāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śoṣe bhaviṣyati bhavanti sa cāpi jantuḥ śuklekṣaṇe bhavati māṃsaparo ririṃsuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.30"> svapneṣu kākaśukaśallakinīlakaṇṭhagṛdhrās tathaiva kapayaḥ
            kṛkalāsakāś ca |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vāhayanti sa nadīrvijalāś ca paśyec chuṣkāṃstarūn pavanadhūmadavārditāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.31"> mahāśanaṃ kṣīyamāṇamatīsāranipīḍitam |
            <caesura/>
             śūnamuṣkodaraṃ caiva yakṣmiṇaṃ parivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.32"> upācaredātmavantaṃ dīptāgnimakṛśaṃ navam |
            <caesura/>
             sthirādivargasiddhena dhṛtenājāvikena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.33"> snigdhasya mṛdu kartavyamūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ tathā kāryaṃ śirasaś ca virecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.34"> yavagodhūmaśālīṃś ca rasairbhuñjīta śodhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dṛḍhe 'gnau bṛṃhayec cāpi nivṛttopadravaṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.35"> vyavāyaśoṣiṇaṃ prāyo bhajante vātajā gadāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bṛṃhaṇīyo vidhistasmai hitaḥ snighdo 'nilāpahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.36"> kākānulūkānnakulān biḍālān gaṇḍūpadān vyālabileśayākhūn |
            <caesura/>
             gṛdhrāṃś ca dadyādvividhaiḥ pravādaiḥ sasaindhavān sarṣapatailabhṛṣṭān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.37"> deyāni māṃsāni ca jāṅgalāni mudgāḍhakīsūparasāś ca hṛdyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kharoṣṭranāgāśvatarāśvajāni deyāni māṃsāni sukalpitāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.38"> māṃsopadaṃśāṃś ca pibedariṣṭān mārdvīkayuktān madirāś ca sevyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             arkāmṛtākṣārajaloṣitebhyaḥ kṛtvā yavebhyo vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.39"> khādet pibet sarpirajāvikaṃ vā kṛśo yavāgvā saha bhaktakāle |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ trikaṭu pralihyāc cavyāviḍaṅgopahitaṃ kṣayārtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.40"> māṃsādamāṃseṣu ghṛtaṃ ca siddhaṃ śosāpahaṃ kṣaudrakaṇāsametam |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitāmāgadhikāvalehaḥ sakṣaudratailaḥ kṣayarogaghātī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.41"> ghṛtena cājena samākṣikeṇa turaṅgagandhātilamāṣacūrṇam |
            <caesura/>
             sitāśvagandhāmagadhodbhavānāṃ cūrṇaṃ ghṛtakṣaudrayutaṃ pralihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.42"> kṣīraṃ pibed vāpy atha vājigandhāvipakvamevaṃ labhate 'ṅgapuṣṭim |
            <caesura/>
             tad utthitaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ sitāḍhyaṃ prātaḥ pibed vāpi payonupānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.43"> utsādane cāpi turaṅgagandhā yojyā yavāś caiva punarnave ca |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtsne vṛṣe tatkusumaiś ca siddhaṃ sarpiḥ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.44"> yakṣmāṇam etat prabalaṃ ca kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ ca hanyād api pāṇḍutāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             śakṛdrasā gośvagajāvyajānāṃ kvāthā mitāś cāpi tathaiva bhāgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.45"> mūrvāharidrākhadiradrumāṇāṃ kṣīrasya bhāgastvaparo ghṛtasya |
            <caesura/>
             bhāgān daśautān vipacedvidhijño dattvā trivargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.46"> kaṭutrikaṃ caiva sabhadradāru ghṛtottamaṃ yakṣmanivāraṇāya |
            <caesura/>
             dve pañcamūlyau varuṇaṃ karañjaṃ bhallātakaṃ bilvapunarnave ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.47"> yavān kulatthān badarāṇi bhārgīṃ pāṭhāṃ hutāśaṃ samahīkadambam |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ vipaceddhi tasya ṣaḍbhir hi pātrairghṛtapātramekam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.48"> vyoṣaṃ mahāvṛkṣapayo 'bhayāṃ ca cavyaṃ surākhyaṃ lavaṇottamaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             etad dhi śoṣaṃ jaṭharāṇi caiva hanyāt pramehāṃś ca sahānilena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.49"> gośvāvyajebhaiṇakharoṣṭrajātaiḥ śakṛdrasakṣīrarasakṣatotthaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāśvagandhāmagadhāsitābhiḥ siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ yakṣmavikārahāri || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.50"> elājamodāmalakābhayākṣagāyatryariṣṭāsanaśālasārān |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgabhallātakacitrakogrākaṭutrikāmbhodasurāṣṭrajāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.51"> paktvā jale tena paceddhi sarpistasmin susiddhe tvavatārite ca |
            <caesura/>
             triṃśatpalānyatra sitopalāyā dattvā tugākṣīripalāni ṣaṭ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.52"> prasthe ghṛtasya dviguṇaṃ ca dadyāt kṣaudraṃ tato manthahataṃ
            vidadhyāt |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ palaṃ prātarataḥ pralihya paścāt pibet kṣīramatandritaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.53"> etad dhi medhyaṃ paramaṃ pavitraṃ cakṣuṣyamāyuṣyamatho yaśasyam |
            <caesura/>
             yakṣmāṇamāśu vyapahanti caitat pāṇḍvāmayaṃ caiva bhagandaraṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.54"> śvāsaṃ ca hanti svarabhedakāsahṛtplīhagulmagrahaṇīgadāṃś ca |
            <caesura/>
             na cātra kiṃcit parivarjanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ caitadupāsyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.55"> plīhodaroktaṃ vihitaṃ ca sarpistrīṇyeva cānyāni hitāni cātra |
            <caesura/>
             upadravāṃś ca svaravaikṛtādīn jayed yathāsvaṃ prasamīkṣya śāstram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.56"> ajāśakṛnmūtrapayoghṛtāsṛṅmāṃsālayāni pratisevamānaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snānādinānāvidhinā jahāti māsādaśeṣaṃ niyamena śoṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.57"> rasonayogaṃ vidhivat kṣayārtaḥ kṣīreṇa vā nāgabalāprayogam |
            <caesura/>
             seveta vā māgadhikāvidhānaṃ tathopayogaṃ jatuno 'śmajasya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.58"> śokaṃ striyaṃ krodhamasūyanaṃ ca tyajedudārān viṣayān bhajeta |
            <caesura/>
             vaidyān dvijātīṃstridaśān gurūś ca vācaś ca puṇyāḥ śṛṇuyādbijebhyaḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre (tṛtīyo
            'dhyāyaḥ, ādita) ekacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||41 ||</p>
