        <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvicatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.1"> athāto gulmapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.3"> yathoktaiḥ kopanairdoṣāḥ kupitāḥ koṣṭhamāgatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             janayanti nṛṇāṃ gulmaṃ sa pañcavidha ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.4"> hṛdbastyor antare granthiḥ saṃcārī yadi vācalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cayāpacayavān vṛttaḥ sa gulma iti kīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5ab"> pañca gulmāśrayā nṝṇāṃ pārśve hṛnnābhibastayaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5cd">gupitānilamūlatvād gūḍhamūlodayād api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.6ab"> gulmavad vā viśālatvād gulma ity abhidhīyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.6cd">sa yasmād ātmani cayaṃ gacchaty apsv iva budbudaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.7"> antaḥ sarati yasmāc ca na pākam upayātyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa vyastair jāyate doṣaiḥ samastair api cocchritaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.8"> puruṣāṇāṃ tathā strīṇāṃ jñeyo raktena cāparaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sadanaṃ madantā vahner āṭopo 'ntravikūjanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.9ab"> viṇmūtrānilasaṅgaś ca sauhityās ahatā tathā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.9cd"> dveṣo 'nne vāyurūrdhvaṃ ca pūrvarūpeṣu gulminām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.10"> hṛtkukṣiśūlaṃ mukhakaṇṭhaśoṣo vāyor nirodho viṣamāgnitā ca |
            <caesura/>
             te te vikārāḥ pavanātmakāś ca bhavanti gulme 'nilasaṃbhave tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.11"> svedajvarāhāravidāhadāhāstṛṣṇāṅgarāgaḥ kaṭuvaktratā ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittasya liṅgānyakhilāni yāni pittātmake tāni bhavanti gulme || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.12"> staimity am anne 'ruciraṅgasādaś chardiḥ praseko madhurāsyatā ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphasya liṅgāni ca yāni tāni bhavanti gulme kaphasaṃbhave tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.13"> sarvātmakaḥ sarvavikārayuktaḥ so 'sādhya uktaḥ kṣatajaṃ pravakṣye
            |
            <caesura/>
             navaprasūtāhitabhojanā yā yā cāmagarbhaṃ visṛjedṛtau vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.14"> vāyur hi tasyāḥ parigṛhya raktaṃ karoti gulmaṃ sarujaṃ sadāham |
            <caesura/>
             paittasya liṅgena samānaliṅgaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ cāpy aparaṃ nibodha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.15"> na spandate nodarameti vṛddhiṃ bhavanti liṅgāni ca garbhiṇīnām |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ garbhakālātigame caikitsyamasṛgbhavaṃ gulmamuśanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.16"> vātagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ yuktaṃ snehavirecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             upācared yathākālaṃ nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.17"> pittagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ kākolyādighṛtena tu |
            <caesura/>
             viriktaṃ madhurairyogairnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.18"> śleṣmagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ pippalyādighṛtena tu |
            <caesura/>
             tīkṣṇairviriktaṃ tad rūpairnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.19"> sannipātotthite gulme tridoṣaghno vidhirhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittavadraktagulminyā nāryāḥ kāryaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.20"> viśeṣamaparaṃ cāsyāḥ śṛṇu raktavibhedanam |
            <caesura/>
             palāśakṣāratoyena siddhaṃ sarpiḥ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.21ab"> dadyād uttarabastiṃ ca pippalyādighṛtena tu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.21cd"> uṣṇair vā bhedayed bhinne vidhirāsṛgdaro hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.22"> ānūpaudakamajjāno vasā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhi |
            <caesura/>
             vipakvam ekataḥ śastaṃ vātagulme 'nuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.23"> jāṅgalaikaśaphānāṃ tu vasā sarpiś ca paittike |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ jāṅgalamajjāna evaṃ gulme kaphotthite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.24"> dhātrīphalānāṃ svarase ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vipaced ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāsaindhavopetaṃ tad dhitaṃ vātagulmine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.25"> citrakavyoṣasindhūtthapṛthvīkācavyadāḍimaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dīpyakagranthikājājīhapuṣādhānyakaiḥ samaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.26"> dadhyāranālabadaramūlakasvarasairghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             tatpibedvātagulmāgnidaurbalyāṭopaśūlanut || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.27"> hiṅgusauvarcalājājīviḍadāḍimadīpyakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             puṣkaravyoṣadhānyāmlavetasakṣāracitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.28"> śaṭīvacājagandhailāsurasaiś ca vipācitam |
            <caesura/>
             śūlānāhaharaṃ sarpirdadhnā cānilagulminām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.29"> viḍadāḍimasindhūtthahutabhugvyoṣajīrakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṅgusauvarcalakṣārarugvṛkṣāmlāmlavetasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.30"> bījapūrarasopetaṃ sarpirdadhicaturguṇam |
            <caesura/>
             sādhitṃ dādhikaṃ nāma gulmahṛt plīhaśūlajit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.31"> rasonasvarase sarpiḥ pañcamūlarasānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             surāranāladadhyamlamūlakasvarasaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.32"> vyoṣadāḍimavṛkṣāmlayavānīcavyasaindhavaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṅgvamlavetasājājīdīpyakaiś ca samāṃśikaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.33"> siddhaṃ gulmagrahaṇyarśaḥśvāsonmādakṣayajvarān |
            <caesura/>
             kāsāpasmāramandāgniplīhaśūlānilāñjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.34"> dadhi sauvīrakaṃ sarpiḥ kvāthau mudgakulatthajau |
            <caesura/>
             pañcāḍhakāni vipaced āvāpya dvipalāny atha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.35"> sauvarcalaṃ sarjikāṃ ca devadārv atha saindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             vātagulmāpahaṃ sarpir etad dīpanam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.36"> tṛṇamūlakaṣāye tu jīvanīyaiḥ pacedghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             nyagrodhādigaṇe vāpi gaṇe vāpy utpalādike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.37"> raktapittotthitaṃ ghnanti ghṛtāny etāny asaṃśayam |
            <caesura/>
             āragvadhādau vipaceddīpanīyayutaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.38"> kṣāravarge pacec cānyat pacen mūtragaṇe 'param |
            <caesura/>
             ghnanti gulmaṃ kaphodbhūtaṃ ghṛtānyetānyasaṃśayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.39"> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ cāpi cikitsetsānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ hiṅgvādikaṃ vāpi ghṛtaṃ vā plīhanāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.40"> pibed gulmāpahaṃ kāle sarpistailvakam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             tilekṣurakapālāśasārṣapaṃ yāvanālajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.41"> bhasma mūlakajaṃ cāpi gojāvikharahantinām |
            <caesura/>
             mūtreṇa mahiṣīṇāṃ ca pālikaiś cāvacūrṇitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.42"> kuṣṭhasaindhavayaṣṭyāhvanāgarakṛmighātibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sājamodaiś ca daśabhiḥ sāmudrāc ca palairyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.43"> ayaḥpātre 'gninālpena paktvā lehyam(laham) athoddharet |
            <caesura/>
             tasya mātrāṃ pibed dadhnā surayā sarpiṣāpi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.44"> dhānyāmlenoṣṇatoyena kaulatthena rasena vā |
            <caesura/>
             gulmān vātavikārāṃś ca kṣāro 'yaṃ hantyasaṃśayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.45"> svarjikākuṣṭhasahitaḥ kṣāraḥ ketakijo 'pi vā |
            <caesura/>
             tailena śamayet pīto gulmaṃ pavanasaṃbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.46"> pītaṃ sukhāmbunā vāpi svarjikākuṣṭhasaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             vṛś cīvamurubūkaṃ(vṛś cīramurubūkaṃ) ca varṣābhūrbṛhatīdvayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.47"> citrakaṃ ca jaladroṇe paktvā pādāvaśeṣitam |
            <caesura/>
             māgadhīciktrakakṣaudralipte kumbhe nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.48"> madhunaḥ prasthamāvāpya pathyācūrṇārdhasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             busoṣitaṃ daśāhaṃ tu jīrṇabhaktaḥ piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.49"> ariṣṭo 'yaṃ jayed gulmamavipākamarocakam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhānikumbharajanītrikaṭutriphalāgnikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.50"> lavaṇaṃ vṛkṣabījaṃ ca tulyaṃ syād anavo guḍaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pathyābhir vā yutaṃ cūrṇaṃ gavāṃ mūtrayutaṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.51"> guṭikāstadghṛnībhūtaṃ kṛtvā khādedabhuktavān |
            <caesura/>
             gulmaplīhāgnisādāṃtā nāśayeyuraśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.52"> hṛdrogaṃ grahaṇīdoṣaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca dāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             saśūle sonnate 'spande dāhapākaruganvite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.53ab"> gulme raktaṃ jalaukobhiḥ sirāmokṣeṇa vā haret |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.53cd"> sukhoṣṇā jāṅgalarasāḥ susnigdhā vyaktasaindhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.54ab"> kaṭutrikasamāyuktā hitāḥ pāne tu gulminām |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.54cd"> peyā vātaharaiḥ siddhāḥ kaulatthāḥ saṃskṛtā rasāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.55"> khalāḥ sapañcamūlāś ca gulmināṃ bhojane hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             baddhavarconilānāṃ tu sārdrakaṃ kṣīramiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.56"> kumbhīpiṇḍeṣṭakāsvedān kārayet kuśalo bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             gulminaḥ sarva evoktā durvirecyatamā bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.57"> ataśaitāṃs tu susvinnān sraṃsanenopapādayet |
            <caesura/>
             vimlāpanābhyañjanāni tathaiva dahanāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.58"> upanāhāś ca kartavyāḥ sukhoṣṇāḥ sālvaṇādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             udaroktāni sarpīṃṣi mūtravartikriyās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.59"> lavaṇāni ca yojyāni yānyuktānyanilāmaye |
            <caesura/>
             vātavarconirodhe tu sāmudrārdrakasarṣapaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.60"> kṛtvā pāyau vidhātavyā vartayo maricottarāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dantīcitrakamūleṣu tathā vātahareṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.61"> kuryād ariṣṭān sarvāṃś ca ślokasthāne yatheritān |
            <caesura/>
             khādedvāpyaṅkurān bhṛṣṭān pūtīkanṛpavṛkṣayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.62"> ūrdhvavātaṃ manuṣyaṃ ca gulminaṃ na nirūhayet |
            <caesura/>
             pibettrivṛnnāgaraṃ vā saguḍāṃ vā harītakīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.63"> gugguluṃ trivṛtāṃ dantīṃ dravantīṃ saindhavaṃ vacām |
            <caesura/>
             mūtramadyapayodrākṣārasairvīkṣya balābalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.64"> evaṃ pīlūni bhṛṣṭāni pibet salavaṇāni tu |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakasaindhavaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.65"> yuktā hanti surā gulmaṃ śīghraṃ kāle prayojitā |
            <caesura/>
             baddhaviṇmāruto gulmī bhuñjīta payasā yavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.66"> kulmāṣān vā bahusnehān bhakṣyellavaṇottarān |
            <caesura/>
             athāsyopadravaḥ śūlaḥ kathaṃcid upajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.67"> śūlaṃ nikhānitamivāsukhaṃ yena tu vattyasau |
            <caesura/>
             tatra viṇmūtrasaṃrodhaḥ kṛcchrocchvāsaḥ sthirāṅgatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.68"> tṛṣṇā dāho bhramo 'nnasya vidagdhaparivṛddhitā |
            <caesura/>
             romaharṣo 'ruciś chardir bhuktavṛddhir jaḍāṅgatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.69"> vāyvādibhir yathāsaṅkhyāṃ miśrair vā vīkṣya yojayet |
            <caesura/>
             pathyātrilavaṇaṃ kṣāraṃ hiṅgutumburupauṣkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.70"> yavānīṃ ca haridrāṃ ca viḍaṅgānyamlavetasam |
            <caesura/>
             vidārītriphalābhīruśṛṅgāṭīguḍaśarkarāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.71"> kāśmarīphalayaṣṭyāhvaparūṣakahimāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaḍgranthātiviṣādārupathyāmaricavṛkṣajān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.72"> kṛṣṇāmūlakacanvyaṃ ca nāgarakṣāracitrakān |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmlakāñjikakṣīratoyaiḥ ślokasamāpanān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.73"> yathākramaṃ vimiśrāṃś ca dvandve sarvāṃś ca sarvaje |
            <caesura/>
             tathaiva sekāvagāhapradehābhyaṅgabhojanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.74"> śiśirodakapūrṇānāṃ bhājanānāṃ ca dhāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             vamanonmardanasvedalaṅghanakṣapaṇakriyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.75"> snehādiś ca karamaḥ sarvo viśeṣeṇopadiśyate |
            <caesura/>
             vallūraṃ mūlakaṃ matsyān śuṣkaśākāni vaidalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.76"> na khādedālukaṃ gulmī madhurāṇi phalāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             vinā gulmena yacchūlaṃ gulmasthāneṣu jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.77"> nidānaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi rūpaṃ ca sacikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ nigrahādatibhojanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.78"> ajīrṇādhyaśanāyāsaviruddhānnopasevanāt |
            <caesura/>
             pānīyapānāt kṣutkāle virūḍhānāṃ ca sevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.79"> piṣṭānnaśuṣkamāṃsānām upayogāttathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃvidhānāṃ dravyāṇāmanyeṣāṃ copasevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.80"> vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ koṣṭhe śūlaṃ saṃjanayed bhṛśam |
            <caesura/>
             nirucchvāsī bhavettena vedanāpīḍito naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.81"> śaṅkusphoṭanavattasya yasmāttīvrāś ca vedanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śūlāsaktasya lakṣyante tasmācchūlamihocyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.82"> nirāhārasya yasyaiva tīvraṃ śūlamudīryate |
            <caesura/>
             prastabdhagātro bhavati kṛcchreṇocchvasitīva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.83"> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi kṛcchreṇa kurute naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             etairliṅgairvijānīyācchūlaṃ vātasamudbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.84"> tṛṣṇā dāho mado mūrcchā tīvraṃ śūlaṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             śītābhikāmo bhavati śītenaiva praśāmyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.85"> etairliṅgairvijānīyācchūlaṃ pittasamudbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             śūlenotpīḍyamānasya hṛllāsa upajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.86"> atīva pūrṇakoṣṭhatvaṃ tathaiva gurugātratā |
            <caesura/>
             etacchleṣmasamutthasya śūlasyoktaṃ nidarśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.87"> sarvāṇi dṛṣṭvā rūpāṇi nirdiśetsānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             sannipātasamutthānamasādhyaṃ taṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.88"> śūlānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ cikitsāṃ tu nibodha me |
            <caesura/>
             āśukārī hi pavanastasmāt taṃ tvarayā jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.89"> tasya śūlābhipannasya sveda eva sukhāvahaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyasaiḥ kṛśarāpiṇḍaiḥ snigdhair vā piśitairhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.90"> trivṛcchākena vā snigdhamuṣṇaṃ bhiñjīta bhojanam |
            <caesura/>
             cirabilvāṅkurān vāpi tailabhṛṣṭāṃs tu bhakṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.91"> vaihaṅgāṃś ca rasān snigdhān jāṅgalān śūlapīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathālābhaṃ niṣeveta māṃsāni bilaśāyinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.92"> surā sauvīrakaṃ cukraṃ mastūdaśvittathā dadhi |
            <caesura/>
             sakālalavaṇaṃ peyaṃ śūle vātasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.93"> kulatthayūṣo yuktāmlo lāvakīyūṣasaṃskṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sasaindhavaḥ samarico vātaśūlavināśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.94"> viḍaṅgaśigrukampillapathyāśyāmāmlavetasān |
            <caesura/>
             surasāmaśvamūtrīṃ ca sauvarcalayutān pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.95"> madyena vātajaṃ śūlaṃ kṣipram eva praśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthvīkājājicavikāyavānīvyoṣacitrakāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.96"> pippalyaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ saindhavaṃ ceti cūrṇayet |
            <caesura/>
             tāni cūrṇāni payasā pibet kāmbalikena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.97"> madhvāsavena cukreṇa surāsauvīrakeṇa vā |
            <caesura/>
             athavaitāni(athacaitāni) cūrṇāni mātuluṅgarasena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.98"> tathā badarayūṣeṇa bhāvitāni punaḥ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāni hiṅgupragāḍhāni saha śarkarayā pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.99"> saha dāḍimasāreṇa vartiḥ kāryā bhiṣagjitā |
            <caesura/>
             sā vartirvātikaṃ śūlaṃ kṣipram eva vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.100"> guḍatailena vā līḍhā pītā madyena vā punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bubhukṣāprabhave śūle laghu saṃtarpaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.101"> uṣṇaiḥ kṣīrairyavāgūbhiḥ snigdhairmāṃsarasais tathā |
            <caesura/>
             vātaśūle samutpanne rūkṣaṃ snigdhena bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.102"> susaṃskṛtāḥ pradeyāḥ syurghṛtapūrā viśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāruṇīṃ ca pibejjantus tathā saṃpadyate sukhī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.103"> etadvātasamutthasya śūlasyoktaṃ cikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             atha pittasamutthasya kriyāṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.104"> sa sukhaṃ chardayitvā tu pītvā śītodakaṃ naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītalāni ca seveta sarvāṇyuṣṇāni varjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.105"> maṇirājatatāmrāṇi bhājanāni ca sarvaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāripūrṇāni tānyasya śūlasyopari nikṣipet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.106"> guḍaḥ śāliryavāḥ kṣīraṃ sarpiḥpānaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni bheṣajaṃ pittaśūlinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.107"> rasān seveta pittaghnān pittalāni vivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             pālāśaṃ dhānvanaṃ vāpi pibedyūṣaṃ saśarkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.108"> parūṣakāṇi mṛdvīkākharjūrodakajānyapi |
            <caesura/>
             tat pibec charkarāyuktaṃ pittaśūlanivāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.109"> aśane bhuktamātre tu prakopaḥ ślaiṣmikasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             vamanaṃ kārayettatra pippalīvāriṇā bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.110"> rūkṣaḥ svedaḥ prayojyaḥ syād anyāś coṣṇāḥ kriyā hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pippalī śṛṅgaveraṃ ca śleṣmaśūle bhiṣagjitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.111"> pāṭhāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ tathā kaṭukarohiṇīm |
            <caesura/>
             citrakasya ca niryūhe pibedyūṣaṃ sahārjakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.112"> eraṇḍaphalamūlāni mūlaṃ gokṣurakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             śālaparṇīṃ pṛśniparṇīṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.113"> dadyācchṛgālavinnāṃ ca sahadevāṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mahāsahāṃ kṣudrasahāṃ mūlamikṣurakasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.114"> etat saṃbhṛtya saṃbhāraṃ jaladroṇe vipācayet |
            <caesura/>
             caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu yavakṣārayutaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.115"> vātikaṃ paittikaṃ vāpi ślaiṣmikaṃ sānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             prasahya nāśayec chūlaṃ chinnābhram iva mārutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.116"> pippalī svarjikākṣāro yavāś citraka eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             sevyaṃ caitat samānīya bhasma kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.117"> tad uṣṇavāriṇā pītaṃ śleṣmaśūle bhiṣagjitam |
            <caesura/>
             ruṇaddhi mārutaṃ śleṣmā kukṣipārśvavyavasthitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.118"> sa saṃruddhaḥ karotyāśu sādhmānaṃ guḍguḍāyanam |
            <caesura/>
             sūcībhir iva nistodaṃ kṛcchrocchvāsī tadā naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.119"> nānnaṃ vāñchati no nidrām upaity artinipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pārśvaśūlaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kaphānilasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.120"> tatra puṣkaramūlāni hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ viḍam |
            <caesura/>
             saindhavaṃ tumburuṃ pathyāṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tu pāyayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.121"> pārśvahṛdbastiśūleṣu yavakvāthena saṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥ plīhodaroktaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ vā hiṅgusaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.122"> bījapūrakasāraṃ vā payasā saha sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             eraṇḍatailamathavā madyamas tu payorasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.123"> bhojayec cāpi payasā jāṅgalena rasena vā |
            <caesura/>
             prakupyati yadā kukṣau vahnimākramya mārutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.124"> tadāsya bhojanaṃ bhuktaṃ sopastambhaṃ na pacyate |
            <caesura/>
             ucchvasity āmaśakṛtā śūlenāhanyate muhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.125"> naivāsane na śayane tiṣṭhan vā labhate sukham |
            <caesura/>
             kukṣiśūla iti khyāto vātādāmasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.126"> vamanaṃ kārayettatra laṅghayed vā yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃsargapācanaṃ kuryād amlair dīpanasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.127"> nāgaraṃ dīpyakaṃ cavyaṃ hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ viḍam |
            <caesura/>
             mātuluṅgasya bījāni tathā śyāmorubūkayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.128"> bṛhatyāḥ kaṇṭakāryāś ca kvāthaṃ śūlaharaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             vacā sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu kuṣṭhaṃ sātiviṣābhayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.129"> kuṭajasya ca bījāni sadyaḥśūlaharāṇi tu |
            <caesura/>
             virecane prayuñjīta jñātvā doṣabalābalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.130"> snehabastīn nirūhāṃś ca kuryād doṣanibarhaṇān |
            <caesura/>
             upanāhāḥ snehasekā dhānyāmlapariṣecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.131"> avagāhāś ca śasyante yac cānyad api tad dhitam |
            <caesura/>
             kaphapittāvaruddhas tu māruto rasamūrcchitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.132"> hṛdisthaḥ kurute śūlamucchvāsārodhakaṃ param |
            <caesura/>
             sa hṛcchūla iti khyāto rasamārutasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.133"> tatrāpi karmābhihitaṃ yadi uktaṃ hṛdvikāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             saṃrodhāt kupito vāyuri bastim āvṛtya tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.134"> bastivaṅkṣaṇanābhīṣu tataḥ śūlo 'sya jāyate |
            <caesura/>
             viṇmūtravātasaṃrodhī bastiśūlaḥ sa mārutāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.135"> nābhyāṃ vaṅkṣaṇapārśveṣu kukṣau meḍhrāntramardakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtramāvṛtya gṛhṇāti mūtraśūlaḥ sa mārutāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.136"> vāyuḥ prakupito yasya rūkṣāhārasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             malaṃ ruṇaddhi koṣṭhasthaṃ mandīkṛtya tu pāvakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.137"> śūlaṃ saṃjanayaṃstīvraṃ srotāṃsyāvṛtya tasya hi |
            <caesura/>
             dakṣiṇaṃ yadi vā vāmaṃ kukṣimādāya jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.138"> sarvatra vardhate kṣipraṃ bhramannatha saghoṣavān |
            <caesura/>
             pipāsā vardhate tīvrā bhramo mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.139"> uccārito mūtritaś ca na śāntimadhigacchati |
            <caesura/>
             viṭśūlametajjānīyādbhiṣak paramadāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.140"> kṣipraṃ doṣaharaṃ kāryaṃ bhiṣajā sādhu jānatā |
            <caesura/>
             svedanaṃ śamanaṃ caiva nirūhāḥ snehabastayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.141"> pūrvoddiṣṭān pāyayeta yogān koṣṭhaviśodhanān |
            <caesura/>
             udāvartaharāś cāsya kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sukhāvahāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.142"> atimātraṃ yadā bhuktaṃ pāvake mṛdutāṃ gate |
            <caesura/>
             sthirībhūtaṃ tu tatkoṣṭhe vāyurāvṛtya tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.143"> avipākagataṃ hy annaṃ śūlaṃ tīvraṃ karotyati |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchādhmānaṃ vidāhaś ca hṛdutkleśo vilambikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.144"> viricyate chardayati kampate 'tha vimuhyati |
            <caesura/>
             avipākād bhavec chūlas tv annadoṣasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.145"> vamanaṃ laṅghanaṃ svedaḥ pācanaṃ phalavartayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārāś cūrṇāni guṭikāḥ śasyante śūlanāśanāḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             gulmāvasthāḥ kriyāḥ kāryā yathāvat sarvaśūlinām ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            gulmapratiṣedho nāma (caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||42 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
          <head>tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.1"> athāto hṛdrogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.3"> vegāghātoṣṇarūkṣānnairatimātropasevitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇairasātmyaiś cāpi(cāti) bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.4"> dūṣayitvā rasaṃ doṣā viguṇā hṛdayaṃ gatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kurvanti hṛdaye bādhāṃ hṛdrogaṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.5"> caturvidhaḥ sa doṣaiḥ syāt kṛmibhiś ca pṛthak pṛthak |
            <caesura/>
             lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi cikitsitamanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.6"> āyamyate mārutaje hṛdayaṃ tudyate tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nirmathyate dīryate ca sphoṭyate pāṭyate 'pi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.7"> tṛṣṇoṣādāhacoṣāḥ syuḥ paittike hṛdayaklamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhūmāyanaṃ ca mūrcchā ca svedaḥ śoṣo mukhasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.8"> gauravaṃ kaphasaṃsrāvo 'ruciḥ stambho 'gnimārdavam |
            <caesura/>
             mādhuryam api cāsyasya balāsāvatate hṛdi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.9"> utkleśaḥ ṣṭhīvanaṃ todaḥ śūlo hṛllāsakastamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aruciḥ śyāvnetratvaṃ śoṣaś ca kṛmije bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.10"> bhramaklamau sādaśoṣau jñeyās teṣām upadravāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmije kṛmijātīnāṃ ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ ca ye matāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.11"> vātopasṛṣṭe hṛdaye vāmayet snigdhamāturam |
            <caesura/>
             dvipañcamūlakvāthena sasnehalavaṇena tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.12"> pippalyelāvacāhiṅguyavabhasmāni saindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalamatho śuṇṭhīmajamodāṃ ca cūrṇitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.13"> phaladhānyāmlakaulatthadadhimadyāsavādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayeta viśuddhaṃ ca snehenānyatamena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.14"> bhojayejjīrṇaśālyannaṃ jāṅgalaiḥ saghṛtai rasaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnasiddhaṃ tailaṃ ca dadyādbastiṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.15"> śrīparṇīmadhukakṣaudrasitotpalajalairvamet |
            <caesura/>
             pittopasṛṣṭe hṛdaye seveta madhuraiḥ śṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.16"> ghṛtaṃ kaṣāyāṃś coddiṣṭān pittajvaravināśanān |
            <caesura/>
             tṛptasya ca rasairmukhyairmadhuraiḥ saghṛtairbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.17"> sakṣaudraṃ vitaredbastau tailaṃ madhukasādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             vacānimbakaṣāyābhyāṃ vāntaṃ hṛdi kaphātmake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.18"> cūrṇaṃ tu pāyayetoktaṃ vātaje bhojayec ca tam |
            <caesura/>
             phalādimatha mustādiṃ triphalāṃ vā piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.19"> śyāmātrivṛtkalkayutaṃ ghṛtaṃ vāpi virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             balātailairvidadhyāc ca bastiṃ bastiviśāradaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.20"> kṛmihṛdrogiṇaṃ snigdhaṃ bhojayet piśitaudanam |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā ca palalopetaṃ tryahaṃ paścād virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.21"> sugandhibhiḥ salavaṇairyogaiḥ sājājiśarkaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgagāḍhaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ pāyayetāpyanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.22"> hṛdayasthāḥ patantyevamadhastāt krimayo nṛṇām |
            <caesura/>
             yavānnaṃ vitareccāsya saviḍaṅgamataḥ param ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            hṛdrogapratiṣedho nāma (pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||43 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.1"> athātaḥ pāṇḍurogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvandariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.3"> vyavāyamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamatīva tīkṣṇam |
            <caesura/>
             niṣevamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.4"> pāṇḍvāmayo 'ṣṭārdhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ pṛthaksamastairyugapac ca
            doṣaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarveṣu caiteṣv iha pāṇḍubhāvo yato 'dhiko 'taḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.5"> tvaksphoṭanaṃ ṣṭhīvanagātrasādau mṛdbhakṣaṇaṃ prekṣaṇakūṭaśothaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatas tasya puraḥsarāṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.6"> sa kāmalāpānakipāṇḍurogaḥ kumbhāhvayo
            lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vibhāṣyate lakṣaṇamasya kṛtsnaṃ nibodha vakṣyāmyanupūrvaśastat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.7"> kṛṣṇekṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.8"> pītekṣaṇaṃ pītasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.9"> śuklekṣaṇaṃ śuklasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.10"> sarvātmake sarvam idaṃvyavasyed vakṣyāmi liṅgānyatha kāmalāyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yo hyāmayānte sahasānnamamlamadyādapathyāni ca tasya pittam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.11"> karoti pāṇḍuṃ vadanaṃ viśeṣāt pūrveritau tandribalakṣayau ca |
            <caesura/>
             bhedas tu tasyāḥ khalu kumbhasāhvaḥ śopho mahāṃs tatra ca parvabhedaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.12"> jvarāṅgamardabhramasādatandrākṣayānvito
            lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vātapittāddharipītanīlaṃ halīmakaṃ nāma vadanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.13"> upadravās teṣv aruciḥ pipāsā chardirjvaro mūrdharujāgnisādaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śophas tathā kaṇṭhagato 'balatvaṃ mūrcchā klamo hṛdyavapīḍanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.14"> sādhyaṃ tu pāṇḍvāmayinaṃ samīkṣya snigdhaṃ ghṛtenordhvamadhaś ca
            śuddham |
            <caesura/>
             saṃpādayet kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhairharītakīcūrṇayutaiḥ prayogaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.15"> pibed ghṛtaṃ vā rajanīvipakvaṃ yantraiphalaṃ tailvakam eva vāpi |
            <caesura/>
             virecanadravyakṛtaṃ pibedvā yogāṃś ca vairecanidān ghṛtena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.16"> mūtre nikumbhārdhapalaṃ vipācya pibed abhīkṣṇaṃ kuḍavārdhamātram |
            <caesura/>
             khāded guḍaṃ vāpy abhayāvipakvamāragvadhādikvathitaṃ pibedvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.17"> ayorajovyoṣaviḍaṅgacūrṇaṃ lihyād dharidrāṃ triphalānvitāṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             sarpir madhubhyāṃ vidadhīta vāpi śāstrapradeśābhihitāṃś ca yogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.18"> ahrec ca doṣān bahuśo 'lpamātrān śvayed dhi doṣeṣv atinirhṛteṣu |
            <caesura/>
             dhātrīphalānāṃ rasamikṣujaṃ ca manthaṃ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.19"> ubhe bṛhatyau rajanīṃ śukākhyāṃ kākādanīṃ cāpi sakākamācīm |
            <caesura/>
             ādāribimbīṃ sakadambapuṣpīṃ vipācya sarpirvipacet kaṣāye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.20"> tat pāṇḍutāṃ hantyupayujyamānaṃ kṣīeṇa vā māgadhikā yathāgni |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ca yaṣṭīmadhujaṃ kaṣāyaṃ cūrṇaṃ samaṃ vā madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.21"> gomūtrayuktaṃ triphalādalānāṃ dattvāyasaṃ cūrṇamanalpakālam |
            <caesura/>
             pravālamuktāñjanaśaṅkhacūrṇaṃ lihyāttathā kāñcanagairikottham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.22"> ājaṃ śakṛtsyāt kuḍavapramāṇaṃ viḍaṃ haridrā lavaṇottamaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthak palāṃśāni samagrametaccūrṇaṃ hitāśī madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.23"> maṇḍūralohāgniviḍaṅgapathyāvyoṣāṃśakaḥ sarvasamānatāpyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrāsuto 'yaṃ madhunāvalehaḥ pāṇḍvāmayaṃ hantyacireṇa ghoram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.24"> bibhītakāyomalanāgarāṇāṃ cūrṇaṃ tilānāṃ ca guḍaś ca mukhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             takrānupāno vaṭakaḥ prayuktaḥ kṣiṇoti ghorānapi pāṇḍurogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.25"> sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu kirātatiktaṃ kalāyamātrāṇi sukhāmbunā vā |
            <caesura/>
             mūrvāharidrāmalakaṃ ca lihyāt sthitaṃ gavāṃ saptadināni mūtre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.26"> mūlaṃ balācitrakayoḥ pibedvā pāṇḍvāmayārto 'kṣasamaṃ hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             sukhāmbunā vā lavaṇena tulyaṃ śigroḥ phalaṃ kṣīrabhujopayojyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.27"> nyagrodhavargasya pibet kaṣāyaṃ śītaṃ sitākṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             śālādikaṃ cāpy atha sāracūrṇaṃ dhātrīphalaṃ vā madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.28"> viḍaṅgamustatriphalājamodaparūṣakavyoṣavinirdahanyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍaśarkare ca tathaiva sarpirmadhunī śume ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.29"> saṃbhārametadvipacennidhāya sārodake sāravato gaṇasya |
            <caesura/>
             jātaṃ ca lehyaṃ matimān viditvā nidhāpayenmokṣakaje samudge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.30"> hantyeṣa lehaḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaṃ saśothamugrām api kāmalāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkarā kāmalināṃ tribhaṇḍī hitā gavākṣī saguḍā ca śuṇṭhī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.31"> kāleyake cāpi ghṛtaṃ vipakvaṃ hitaṃ ca tat syād rajanīvimiśram |
            <caesura/>
             dhātuṃ nadījaṃ jatu śailajaṃ vā kumbhāhvaye mūtrayutaṃ pibedvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.32"> mūtre sthitaṃ saindhavasaṃprayuktaṃ māsaṃ pibedvāpi hi lohakiṭṭam
            |
            <caesura/>
             dagdhvākṣakāṣṭhairmalamāyasaṃ vā gomūtranirvāpitamaṣṭavārān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.33"> vicūrṇya līḍhaṃ madhunācireṇa kumbhāhvayaṃ pāṇḍugadaṃ nihanyāt |
            <caesura/>
             sindhūdbhavaṃ vāgnisamaṃ ca kṛtvā kṣiptvā ca mūtre sakṛdeva taptam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.34"> lauhaṃ ca kiṭṭaṃ bahuśaś ca taptvā nirvāpya mūtre bahuśas tathaiva
            |
            <caesura/>
             ekīkṛtaṃ gojalapiṣṭametadaikadhyamāvāpya pacedukhāyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.35"> yathā na dahyeta tathā viśuṣkaṃ cūrṇīkṛtaṃ peyamudaśvitā tat |
            <caesura/>
             takraudanāśī vijayeta rogaṃ pāṇḍuṃ tathā dīpayate 'nalaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.36"> drākṣāguḍūcyāmalakīrasaiś ca siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ lāgharake(lāghavake)
            hitaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             gauḍānariṣṭān madhuśarkarāś ca mūtrāsavān kṣārakṛtāṃs tathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.37"> snigdhān rasānāmalakair upetān kolānvitān vāpi hi jāṅgalānām |
            <caesura/>
             seveta śophābhihitāṃś ca yogān pāṇḍvāmayī śāliyavāṃś ca nityam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.38"> śvāsātisārārucikāsamūrcchātṛṭchardiśūlajvaraśophadāhān |
            <caesura/>
             tathāvipākasvaramedasādān jayed yathāsvaṃ prasamīkṣya śāstram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.39"> anteṣu śūnaṃ parihīnamadhyaṃ mlānaṃ tathānteṣu ca madhyaśūnam |
            <caesura/>
             gude ca śephasyatha muṣkaśūnaṃ pratāmyamānaṃ ca visaṃjñakalpam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.40"> vivarjayet pāṇḍukinaṃ yaśo 'rthī tathātisārajvarapīḍitaṃ ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            pāṇḍurogapratiṣedho nāma (ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||44
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.1"> athāto raktapittapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3"> krodhaśokabhayāyāsaviruddhān nātapānalān |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭvamlalabaṇakṣāratīkṣṇoṣṇātividāhinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4"> nityam abhyasato duṣṭo rasaḥ pittaṃ prakopayet |
            <caesura/>
             vidagdhaṃ svaguṇaiḥ pittaṃ vidahatyāśu śoṇitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5"> tataḥ pravartate raktam ūrdhvaṃ cādho dvidhāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             āmāśayād vrajed ūrdhvam adhaḥ pakvāśayād vrajet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab"> vidagdhayor dvayoś cāpi dvidhā bhāgaṃ pravartate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6cd">kecit sayakṛtaḥ plīhnaḥ pravadanty asṛjo gatim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7ab"> ūrdhvaṃ sādhyam adho yāpyam asādhyaṃ yugapadgatam |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7cd"> sadanaṃ śītakāmitvaṃ kaṇṭhadhūmāyanaṃ vamiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.8"> lohagandhiś ca niḥśvāso bhavaty asmin bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             bāhyāsṛglakṣaṇais tasya saṅkhyā doṣocchritīr viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9"> daurbalyaśvāsakāsajvaravamathumadāstandritādāhamūrcchā bhukte cānne
            vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā hṛdyatulyā ca pīḍā |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇā kaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca davanaṃ pūtiniṣṭhīvanaṃ ca dveṣo bhakte 'vipāko
            viratir api rate raktapittopasargāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10"> māṃsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam iva ca yat kardamāmbhonibhaṃ vā
            medaḥpūyāsrakalpaṃ yakṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābham |
            <caesura/>
             yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlaṃ bhṛśam atikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārās tad varjyaṃ raktapittaṃ
            surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyaṃ vibhāti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.11"> nādau saṃgrāhyam udriktaṃ yad asṛgbalino 'śnataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tat pāṇḍugrahaṇīkuṣṭhaplīhagulmajvarāvaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.12"> adhaḥpravṛttaṃ vamanair ūrdhvagaṃ ca virecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jayed anyatarad vāpi kṣīṇasya śamanair asṛk || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.13"> atipravṛddhadoṣasya pūrvaṃ lohitapittinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             akṣīṇabalamāṃsāgneḥ kartavyamapatarpaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.14"> laṅghitasya tataḥ peyāṃ vidadhyāt svalpataṇḍulām |
            <caesura/>
             rasayūṣau pradātavyau surabhis nehasaṃskṛtau |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ pācanaṃ lehān sarpīṣi vividhāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.15"> drākṣāmadhukakāśmaryasitāyuktaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭīmadhukayuktaṃ ca sakṣaudraṃ vamanaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.16"> payāṃsi śītāni rasāś ca jāṅgalāḥ satīnayūṣāś ca saśāliṣaṣṭikāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolaśelūsuniṣaṇṇayūthikāvaṭātimuktāṅkurasinduvārajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.17"> hitaṃ ca śākaṃ ghṛtasaṃskṛtaṃ sadā tathaiva
            dhātrīphaladāḍimānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             rasāś ca pārāvataśaṅkhakūrmajās tathā yavāgvo vihitā ghṛtottarāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.18"> santānikāś cotpalavargasādhite kṣīre praśastā madhuśarkarottarāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             himāḥ pradehā madhurā gaṇāś ca ye ghṛtāni pathyāni ca raktapittinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.19"> madhūkaśobhāñjanakovidārajaiḥ priyaṅgukāyāḥ kusumaiś ca cūrṇitaiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             bhiṣag vidadhyāc caturaḥ samākṣikān hitāya lehānasṛjaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.20"> lihyāc ca dūrvāvaṭajāṃś ca pallavān madhudvitīyān sitakarṇikasya
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ca kharjūraphalaṃ samākṣikaṃ phalāni cānyāny api tadguṇānyatha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21ab"> raktātisāraproktāṃś ca yogān atrāpi yojayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21cd">śuddhekṣukāṇḍamāpothya nave kumbhe himāmbhasā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.22"> yojayitvā kṣiped rātrāvākāśe sotpalaṃ tu tat |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ srutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ pibec choṇitapittavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.23"> pibec chītakaṣāyaṃ vā jambvāmrārjunasaṃbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             udumbaraphalaṃ piṣṭvā pibet tad rasam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.24"> trapuṣīmūlakalkaṃ vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.25"> candanaṃ madhukaṃ rodhram evam eva samaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             karañjabījam evaṃ vā sitākṣaudrayutaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.26"> majjānamiṅgudasyaivaṃ piben madhukasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇaṃ lavaṇaṃ bījaṃ kārañjaṃ dadhimastunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.27"> pibed vāpi tryahaṃ martyo raktapittābhipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktapittaharāḥ śastāḥ ṣaḍete yogasattamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.28"> pathyāś caivāvapīḍeṣu ghrāṇataḥ prasrute 'sṛji |
            <caesura/>
             atinisrutarakto vā kṣaudrayuktaṃ pibed asṛk |
            <caesura/>
             yakṛd vā bhakṣayed ājamāmaṃ pittasamāyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.29"> palāśavṛkṣasvarase vipakvaṃ
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ suśītam |
            <caesura/>
             vanaspatīnāṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā
            <caesura/>
             saśarkaraṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibed vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.30"> drākṣāmuśīrāṇy atha padmakaṃ sitā pṛthakpalāṃśānyudake samāvapet |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaṃ niśāṃ tadrudhir āmayaṃ jayet pītaṃ payo vāmbusamaṃ hitāśinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.31"> turaṅgavarcaḥsvarasaṃ samākṣikaṃ pibet sitākṣaudrayutaṃ vṛṣasya vā
            |
            <caesura/>
             lihet tathā vāstukabījacūrṇaṃ kṣaudrānvitaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.32"> lihyāc ca lājāñjanacūrṇamekamevaṃ sitākṣaudrayutāṃ tugākhyām |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ sitāṃ tiktakarohiṇīṃ ca himāmbunā vā madhukena yuktām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33ab"> pathyāmahiṃsrāṃ rajanīṃ ghṛtaṃ ca
            <caesura/>
             lihyāt tathā śoṇitapittarogī |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33cd"> vāsākaṣāyotpalamṛtpriyaṅgurodhrāñjanāmbhoruhakeśarāṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.34"> pītvā sitākṣaudrayutāni jahyāt pittasṛjo vegamudīrṇamāśu |
            <caesura/>
             gāyatrijambvarjunakovidāraśirīṣarodhrāśanaśālmalīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.35"> puṣpāṇi śigroś ca vicūrṇya leho madhvanvitaḥ śoṇitapittaroge |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudramindīvarabhasmavāri karañjabījaṃ madhusarpiṣī ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36ab"> jambvarjunāmrakvathitaṃ ca toyaṃ ghnanti trayaḥ pittam asṛk ca
            yogāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36cd"> mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca mātuluṅgyāḥ piṣṭvā pibettaṇḍuladhāvanena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.37"> ghrāṇapravṛtte jalamāśu deyaṃ saśarkaraṃ nāsikayā payo vā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣārasaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibedvā saśarkaraṃ cekṣurasaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.38"> śītopacāraṃ madhuraṃ ca kuryād
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣataḥ śoṇitapittaroge |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāghṛtakṣaudrasitāyutena
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhādivipācitena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.39"> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanam agryam uktaṃ
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpy anuvāsanārtham |
            <caesura/>
             priyaṅgurodhrāñjanagairikotpalaiḥ
            <caesura/>
             suvarṇakālīyakaraktacandanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.40"> sitāśvagandhāmbudayaṣṭikāhvayair
            <caesura/>
             mṛṇālasaugandhikatulyapeṣitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nirūhya cainaṃ payasā samākṣikair
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaplutaiḥ śītajalāvasecitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.41"> kṣīraudanaṃ bhuktam athānuvāsayed
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtena yaṣṭīmadhusādhitena ca |
            <caesura/>
             adhovahaṃ śoṇitameṣa nāśayet
            <caesura/>
             tathātisāraṃ rudhirasya dustaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.42"> virekayoge tvati caiva śasyate
            <caesura/>
             vāmyaś ca rakte vijite balānvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.43"> evaṃvidhā uttarabāstayaś ca mūtrāśayasthe rudhire vidheyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pravṛttarakteṣu ca pāyujeṣu kuryād vidhānaṃ khalu raktapaittam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.44"> vidhiś cāsṛgdare 'pyeṣa strīṇāṃ kāryo vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             śastrakarmaṇi raktaṃ ca yasyātīva pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.45"> trayāṇām api doṣāṇāṃ śoṇite 'pi ca sarvaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             liṅgāny ālokya kartavyaṃ cikitsitam anantaram ||</l>
          <p xml:id="SS.6.45">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            raktapittapratiṣedho nāma (saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||45
            ||</p>

        <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.1"> athāto mūrcchāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.3"> kṣīṇasya bahudoṣasya viruddhāhārasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vegāghātādabhīghātāddhīnasattvasya vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.4"> karaṇāyataneṣūgrā bāhyeṣv ābhyantareṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             niviśante yadā doṣās tadā mūrcchanti mānavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.5"> hṛtpīḍā jṛmbhaṇaṃ glāniḥ saṃjñānāśo balasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             sarvāsāṃ pūrvarūpāṇi yathāsvaṃ tā vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.6"> saṃjñāvahāsu nāḍīṣu pihitāsvanilādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tamo 'bhyupaiti sahasā sukhaduḥkhavyapohakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.7"> sukhaduḥkhavyapohāc ca naraḥ patati kāṣṭhavat |
            <caesura/>
             moho mūrccheti tāṃ prāhuḥ ṣaḍvidhā sā prakīrtitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8"> vātādibhiḥ śoṇitena madyena ca viṣeṇa ca |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṭsvapyetāsu pittaṃ hi prabhutvenāvatiṣṭhate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.9"> apasmāroktaliṅgāni tāsām uktāni tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthivyambhastamorūpaṃ raktagandhaś ca tanmayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.10"> tasmād raktasya gandhena mūrcchanti bhuvi mānavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dravyasvabhāva ity eke sthitās tu viṣamadyayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.11"> guṇās tīvrataratvena sthitās tu viṣamadyayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ta eva tasmāj jāyeta mohastābhyāṃ yatheritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.11ef"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.12"> madyena vilapaṃś chete naṣṭavibhrāntamānasaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gātrāṇi vikṣipan bhūmau jarāṃ yāvan na yāti tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.13"> vepathusvapnatṛṣṇāḥ syuḥ stambhaś ca viṣamūrcchite |
            <caesura/>
             veditavyaṃ tīvrataraṃ yathāsvaṃ viṣalakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.14"> sekāvagāhau maṇayaḥ sahārāḥ śītāḥ pradehā vyajanānilāś ca |
            <caesura/>
             śītāni pānāni ca gandhavanti sarvāsu mūrcchāsvanivāritāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.15ab"> sitāpriyālekṣurasaplutāni drākṣāmadhūkasvarasānvitāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.15cd"> kharjūrakāśmaryarasaiḥ śṛtāni pānāni sarpīṃṣi ca jīvanāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.16"> siddhāni varge madhure payāṃsi sadāḍimā jāṅgalajā rasāś ca |
            <caesura/>
             tathā yavā lohitaśālayaś ca mūrcchāsu pathyāś ca sadā satīnāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.17"> bhujaṅgapuṣpaṃ maricānyuśīraṃ kolasya madhyaṃ ca pibet samāni |
            <caesura/>
             śītena toyena bisaṃ mṛṇālaṃ kṣaudreṇa kṛṣṇāṃ sitayā ca pathyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.18"> kuryāc ca nāsāvadanāvarodhaṃ kṣīraṃ pibed vāpy atha mānuṣīṇām |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchāṃ prasaktāṃ tu śirovirekairjayed abhīkṣṇaṃ vamanaiś ca tīkṣṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.19"> harītakīkvāthaśṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā dhātrīphalānāṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitādāḍimalājavanti śītāni nīlotpalapadmavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.20"> pibet kaṣāyāṇi ca gandhavanti pittajvaraṃ yāni śamaṃ nayanti |
            <caesura/>
             prabhūtadoṣas tamaso 'tirekāt saṃmūrcchito naiva vibudhyate yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.21"> saṃnyastasaṃjño bhṛśaduś cikitsyo jñeyas tadā buddhimatā manuṣyāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             yathā maloṣṭaṃ salile niṣiktaṃ samuddhered āśvavilīnam eva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.21a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.22ab"> tadvac cikitset tvarayā bhiṣak tam asvedanaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ prayātam
            | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.22cd"> tīkṣṇāñjanābhyañjanadhūmayogais tathā nakhābhyantarato trapātaiḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23ab"> vāditragītānunayair apūrvair vighaṭṭanair guptaphalāvagharṣaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23cd"> ābhiḥ kriyābhiś ca na labdhasaṃjñaḥ sānāhalālāśvasanaś ca
            varjyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23ef"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.24ab"> prabuddhasaṃjñaṃ vamanānulomyaistīkṣṇair viśuddhaṃ
            laghupathyabhuktam | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.24cdef"> phalatrikaiś citrakanāgarāḍhyais tathāśmajātāj jatunaḥ
            prayogaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkarair māsam upakrameta viśeṣato jīrṇaghṛtaṃ sa pāyyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.25"> yathāsvaṃ ca jvaraghnāni kaṣāyāṇyupayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             sarvamūrcchāparītānāṃ viṣajāyāṃ viṣāpaham ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            mūrcchāpratiṣedho nāma (aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||46 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="47" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.1"> athātaḥ pānātyayapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.3"> madyamuṣṇaṃ tathā tīkṣṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ viśadam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             rūkṣamāśukaraṃ caiva vyavāyi ca vikāśi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.4"> auṣṇyācchītopacāraṃ tattaikṣṇyāddhanti manogatim |
            <caesura/>
             viśatyavayavān saukṣmyādvaiśadyātkaphaśukranut || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.5"> mārutaṃ kopayed raukṣyādāśutvāccāśukarmakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             harṣadaṃ ca vyavāyitvād vikāśitvād visarpati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.6"> tadamlaṃ rasataḥ proktaṃ laghu rocanadīpanam |
            <caesura/>
             kecillavaṇavarjyāṃs tu rasānatrādiśanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.7"> snigdhais tadannairmāṃsaiś ca bhakṣyaiś ca saha sevitam |
            <caesura/>
             bhavedāyuḥprakarṣāya balāyopacayāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.8"> kāmyatā manasastuṣṭirdhairyaṃ tejo 'tivikramaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vidhivat sevyamāne tu madye sannihitā guṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.9"> tadevānannamajñena sevyamānamamātrayā |
            <caesura/>
             kayāgninā hy agnisamaṃ sametya kurute madam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.10"> madena karaṇānāṃ tu bhāvānyatve kṛte sati |
            <caesura/>
             nigūḍham api bhāvaṃ svaṃ prakāśīkurute 'vaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.11"> tryavasthaś ca mado jñeyaḥ pūrvo madhyo 'tha paś cimaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrve vīryaratiprītiharṣabhāṣyādivardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.12"> pralāpo madhyame moho yuktāyuktakriyās tathā |
            <caesura/>
             visaṃjñaḥ paś cime śete naṣṭakarmakriyāguṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13"> ślaiṣmikānalpapittāṃś ca snigdhānmātropasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pānaṃ na bādhate 'tyarthaṃ viparītāṃs tu bādhate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.14"> nirbhaktamekāntata eva madyaṃ niṣevyamāṇaṃ manujena nityam |
            <caesura/>
             utpādayet kaṣṭatamān vikārānāpādayec cāpi śarīrabhedam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.15"> kruddhena bhītena pipāsitena śokābhitaptena bubhukṣitena |
            <caesura/>
             vyāyāmabhārādhvaparikṣatena vegāvarodhābhihatena cāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.16"> atyamlabhakṣyāvatatodareṇa sājīrṇabhuktena tathābalena |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇābhitaptena ca sevyamānaṃ karoti madyaṃ vividhān vikārān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.17"> pānātyayaṃ paramadaṃ pānājīrṇam athāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             pānavibhramamugraṃ ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.18"> stambhāṅgamardhṛdayagrahatodakampāḥ pānātyaye 'nilakṛte śiraso
            rujaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             svedapralāpamukhaśoṣaṇadāhamūrcchāḥ pittātmake vadanalocanapītatā ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.19"> śleṣmātmake vamathuśītakaphaprasekāḥ sarvātmake bhavati
            sarvavikārasaṃpat |
            <caesura/>
             ūṣmāṇamaṅgagurutāṃ virasānanatvaṃ śleṣmādhikatvamaruciṃ malamūtrasaṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.20"> liṅgaṃ parasya tu madasya vadanti tajjñāstṛṣṇāṃ rujāṃ śirasi
            sandhiṣu cāpi bhedam |
            <caesura/>
             ādhmānamudgiraṇamamlaraso vidāho 'jīrṇasya pānajanitasya vadanti liṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.21"> jñeyāni tatra bhiṣajā suviniś citāni pittaprakopajanitāni ca
            kāraṇāni |
            <caesura/>
             hṛdgātratodavamathujvarakaṇṭhadhūmamūrcchākaphasravaṇamūrdharujo vidāhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.22"> dveṣaḥ surān navikṛteṣu ca teṣu teṣu taṃ pānavibhramam uśanty
            akhilena dhīrāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hīnottarauṣṭham atiśītam amandadāhaṃ tailaprabhāsyam atipānahataṃ (tailaprabhāsyam
            apipānahataṃ) vijahyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.23"> jihvauṣṭhadantam asitaṃ tv athavāpi nīlaṃ pīte ca yasya nayane
            rudhiraprame ca |
            <caesura/>
             hikkājvarau vamathuvepathupārśvaśūlāḥ kāsabhramāvapi ca pānahataṃ bhajante || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.24"> teṣāṃ nivāraṇam idaṃhi mayocyamānaṃ vyaktābhidhānamakhilena vidhiṃ
            nibodha |
            <caesura/>
             madyaṃ tu cukramaricārdrakadīpyakuṣṭhasauvarcalāyutamalaṃ pavanasya śāntyai || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.25"> pṛthvīkadīpyakamahauṣadhahiṅgubhir vā sauvarcalena ca yutaṃ
            vitaret sukhāya |
            <caesura/>
             āmrātakāmraphaladāḍimamātuluṅgaiḥ kuryāc chubhāny api ca ṣaḍavapānakāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.26"> seveta vā phalarasopahitān rasādīnānūpavargapiśitāny api
            gandhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             pittātmake madhuravargakaṣāyamiśraṃ madyaṃ hitaṃ samadhuśarkaramiṣṭagandham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.27"> pītvā ca madyam api cekṣurasapragāḍhaṃ niḥśeṣataḥ
            kṣaṇamavasthitamullikhec ca |
            <caesura/>
             lāvaiṇatittirirasāṃś ca pibedanamlān maudgān sukhāya saghṛtān sasitāṃś ca yūṣān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.28"> pānātyaye kaphakṛte kaphamullikhec ca madyena
            bimbividulodakasaṃyutena |
            <caesura/>
             seveta tiktakaṭukāṃś ca rasānudārān yūṣāṃś ca tiktakaṭukopahitān hitāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.29"> pathyaṃ yavānnavikṛtāni ca jāṅgalāni śleṣmaghnamanyadapi yac ca
            niratyayaṃ syāt |
            <caesura/>
             kuryāc ca sarvamatha sarvabhave vidhānaṃ ddvandvodbhave dvayamavekṣya yathāpradhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.30"> sāmānyamanyadapi yac ca samagramagryaṃ vakṣyāmi yac ca manaso
            madakṛt sukhaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             tvaṅgāgapuṣpamagadhailamadhūkadhānyaiḥ ślakṣṇairajājimaricaiś ca kṛtaṃ samāṃśaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.31"> pānaṃ kapittharasavāriparūṣakāḍhyaṃ pānātyayeṣu
            vidhivatsrutamambarānte |
            <caesura/>
             hrīverapadmaparipelavasaṃprayuktaiḥ puṣpairvilipya karavīrajalodbhavaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.32"> piṣṭaiḥ sapadmakayutair api sārivādyaiḥ sekaṃ jalaiś ca
            vitaredamalaiḥ suśītaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tvakpatracocamaricailabhujaṅgapuṣpaśleṣmātakaprasavavalkaguḍair upetam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.33"> drākṣāyutaṃ hṛtamalaṃ madirāmayārtais tatpānakaṃ śuci sugandhi
            narairniṣevyam |
            <caesura/>
             piṣṭvā pibec ca madhukaṃ kaṭurohiṇīṃ ca drākṣāṃ ca mūlamasakṛt trapuṣībhavaṃ yat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.34"> kārpāsinīmatha ca nāgabalāṃ ca tulyāṃ pītvā sukhī bhavati sādhu
            suvarcalāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kāśmaryadāruviḍadāḍimapippalīṣu drākṣānvitāsu kṛtamambuni pānakaṃ yat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.35"> tadbījapūrakarasāyutamāśu pītaṃ śāntiṃ parāṃ paramade tvacirāt
            karoti |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitāmadhukajīrakadhānyakṛṣṇāsvevaṃ kṛtaṃ trivṛtayā ca pibettathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.36"> sauvarcalāyutamudārarasaṃ phalāmlaṃ bhārgīśṛtena ca jalena hito
            'vasekaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.37"> ikṣvākudhāmārgavavṛkṣakāṇi kākāhvayodumbarikāś ca dugdhe |
            <caesura/>
             vipācya tasyāñjalinā vameddhi madyaṃ pibec cāhni gate tvajīrṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.38"> tvakpippalībhujagapuṣpaviḍair upetaṃ seveta hiṅgumaricailayutaṃ
            phalāmlām |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmbusaindhavayutāstvathavā viḍatvakcavyailahiṅgumagadhāphalamūlaśuṇṭhīḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.39"> hṛdyaiḥ khaḍair api ca bhojanamatra śastaṃ
            drākṣākapitthaphaladāḍimapānakaṃ yat |
            <caesura/>
             tat pānavibhramaharaṃ madhuśarkarāḍhyamāmrātakolarasapānakam eva cāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.40"> kharjūravetrakakarīraparūṣakeṣu drākṣātrivṛtsu ca kṛtaṃ sasitaṃ
            himaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             śrīparṇiyuktamathavā tu pibedimāni yaṣṭyāhvayotpalahimāmbuvimiśritāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.41"> kṣīripravālabisajīrakanāgapuṣpapatrailavālusitasārivapadmakāni |
            <caesura/>
             āmrātabhavyakaramardakapitthakolavṛkṣāmlavetraphalajīrakadāḍimāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.42"> seveta vā maricajīrakanāgapuṣpatvakpatraviśvacavikailayutān rasāṃś
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             sūkṣmāmbarasrutahimāṃca sugandhigandhān pānodbhavānnudati saptagadānaśeṣān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.43"> pañcendriyārthaviṣayā mṛdupānayogā hṛdyāḥ sukhāś ca manasaḥ
            satataṃ niṣevyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pānātyayeṣu vikaṭorunitambavatyaḥ pīnonnatastanabharānatamadhyadeśāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.44"> prauḍhāḥ striyo 'bhinavayauvanapīnagātryaḥ sevyāś ca
            pañcaviṣayātiśayasvabhāvāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.45"> pibedrasaṃ puṣpaphalodbhavaṃ vā sitāmadhūkatrisugandhiyuktam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃcūrṇya saṃyojya ca nāgapuṣpairajājikṛṣṇāmaricaiś ca tulyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.46"> varṣābhūyaṣṭyāhvamadhūkalākṣātvakkarbudārāṅkurajīrakāṇi |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ ca kṛṣṇāmatha keśaraṃ ca kṣīre samāloḍya pibet sukhepsuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.47"> bhavec ca madyena tu yena pātitaḥ prakāmapītena surāsavādinā |
            <caesura/>
             tad eva tasmai vidhivat pradāpayed viparyaye bhraṃśamavaśyamṛcchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.48"> yathā narendropahatasya kasyacidbhavet prasādastata eva nānyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhruvaṃ tathā madyahatasya dehino bhavet prasādastata eva nānyataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.49"> vicchinnamadyaḥ sahasā yo 'timadyaṃ viṣevate |
            <caesura/>
             tasya pānātyayoddiṣṭā vikārāḥ saṃbhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.50"> madyasyāgneyavāyavyau guṇāvambuvahāni(guṇāvambhovahāni) tu |
            <caesura/>
             srotāṃsi śoṣayeyātāṃ tena tṛṣṇopajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.51"> pāṭalotpalakandeṣu mudgaparṇyāṃ ca sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             piben māgadhikonmiśraṃ tatrāmbho himaśītalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.52"> sarpistailavasāmajjadadhibhṛṅgarasairyutam |
            <caesura/>
             kvāthena bilvayavayoḥ sarvagandhaiś ca peṣitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.53"> pakvam abhyañjane śreṣṭhaṃ seke kvāthaś ca śītalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rasavanti ca bhojyāni yathāsvam avacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.54"> pānakāni suśītāni hṛdyāni surabhīṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             tvacaṃ prāptas tu pānoṣmā pittaraktābhimūrcchitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dāhaṃ prakurute ghoraṃ pittavattatra bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.55"> śītaṃ vidhānamata ūrdhvamahaṃ pravakṣye
            dāhapraśāntikaramṛddhimatāṃ narāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tatrādito malayajena hitaḥ pradehaś candrāṃśuhāratuhinodakaśītalena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.56"> śītāmbuśītalataraiś ca śayānamenaṃ hārairmṛṇālavalayairabalāḥ
            spṛśeyuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhinnotpalojjvalahime śayane śayīta patreṣu vā sajalabinduṣu padminīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.57"> āsādayan pavanamāhṛtamaṅganābhiḥ kahlārapadmadalaśaivalasaṃcayeṣu
            |
            <caesura/>
             kāntairvanāntapavanaiḥ parimṛśyamānaḥ śaktaś caredbhavanakānanadīrghikāsu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.58"> dāhābhibhūtamathavā pariṣecayet tu
            lāmajjakāmburuhacandanatoyatoyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             visrāvitāṃ hṛtamalāṃ navavāripūrṇāṃ padmotpalākulajalāmadhivāsitāmbum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.59"> vāpīṃ bhajeta haricandanabhūṣitāṅgaḥ
            kāntākaraspṛśanakarkaśaromakūpaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatrainamamburuhapatrasamaiḥ spṛśantyaḥ śītaiḥ karoruvadanaiḥ kaṭhinaiḥ stanaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.60"> toyāvagāhakuśalā madhurasvabhāvāḥ saṃharṣayeyurabalāḥ sukalaiḥ
            pralāpaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhārāgṛhe pragalitodakadurdinābhe klāntaḥ śayīta salilānilaśītakukṣau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.61"> gandhodakaiḥ sakusumair upasiktabhūmau patrāmbucandanarasair
            upaliptakuḍye |
            <caesura/>
             jātyutpalapriyakakeśarapuṇḍarīkapunnāganāgakaravīrakṛtopacāre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.62"> tasmin gṛhe kamalareṇvaruṇe śayīta
            yatnāhṛtānilavikampitapuṣpadāmni |
            <caesura/>
             hemantavindhyahimavanmalayācalānāṃ śītāmbhasāṃ sakadalīharitadrumāṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.63"> udbhinnanīlanalināmburuhākarāṇāṃ candrodayasya ca kathāḥ
            śṛṇuyānmanojñāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mlānaṃ pratāntamanasaṃ manaso 'nukūlāḥ pīnastanorujaghanā haricandanāṅgyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.64"> tā enamārdravasanāḥ saha saṃviśeyuḥ śliṣṭvāvalāḥ
            śithilamekhalahārayaṣṭyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.65"> harṣayeyurnaraṃ nāryaḥ svaguṇai rahasi sthitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāḥ śaityāc chamayeyuś ca pittapānātyayāntaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.66"> tṛḍdāharaktapitteṣu kāryo 'yaṃ bheṣajakramaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sāmānyato viśeṣaṃ tu śṛṇu dāheṣv aśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.67"> kṛtsnadehānugaṃ raktamudriktaṃ dahati hy ati |
            <caesura/>
             saṃcūṣyate dahyate ca tāmrābhastāmralocanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.68"> lohagandhāṅgavadano vahninevāvakīryate |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vilaṅghya vidhānena saṃsṛṣṭāhāram ācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.69"> apraśāmyati dāhe ca rasais tṛptasya jāṅgalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śākhāśrayā yathānyāyaṃ rohiṇīrvyadhayet sirāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.70"> pittajvarasamaḥ pittāt sa cāpy asya vidhir hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇānirodhād abdhātau kṣīṇe tejaḥ samuddhatam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.71"> sabāhyābhyantaraṃ dehaṃ dahed vai mandacetasaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃśuṣkagalatālvoṣṭho jihvāṃ niṣkṛṣya ceṣṭate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.72"> tatropaśamayet tejas tv abdhātuṃ ca vivardhayet |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayet kāmam ambhaś ca śarkarāḍhyaṃ payo 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.73"> śītam ikṣurasaṃ manthaṃ vitarec ceritaṃ vidhim |
            <caesura/>
             asṛjā pūrṇakoṣṭhasya dāho bhavati duḥsahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.74"> vidhiḥ sadyovraṇīyoktas tasya lakṣaṇam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             dhātukṣayokto yo dāhas tena mūrcchātṛṣānvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.75"> kṣāmasvaraḥ kriyāhīno bhṛśaṃ sīdati pīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktapittavidhis tasya hitaḥ snigdho 'nilāpahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.76"> kṣatajenāśnataś cānyaḥ śocato vāpy anekadhā |
            <caesura/>
             tenāntardahyate 'tyarthaṃ tṛṣṇāmūrcchāpralāpavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.77"> tamiṣṭaviṣayopetaṃ suhṛdbhir abhisaṃvṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīramāṃsarasāhāraṃ vidhinoktena sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.78"> marmābhighātajo 'py asti sa cāsādhyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarva eva ca varjyāḥ syuḥ śītagātreṣu dehiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.79"> (evaṃvidho bhaved yas tu madirāmayapīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ) praśāntopadrave cāpi śodhanaṃ prāptam ācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.80"> sajīrakāṇyārdrakaśṛṅgaverasauvarcalāny ardhajalaplutāni |
            <caesura/>
             madyāni hṛdyānyatha gandhavanti pītāni sadyaḥ śamayanti tṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.81"> jalaplutaś candanabhūṣitāṅgaḥ sragvī sabhaktāṃ piśitopadaṃśām |
            <caesura/>
             piben surāṃ naiva labheta rogān manonuvighnaṃ ca madaṃ na yāti ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            madātyayapratiṣedho nāma (navamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||47
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="48" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.1"> athātastṛṣṇāpratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.3"> satataṃ yaḥ pibedvāri na tṛptimadhigacchati |
            <caesura/>
             punaḥ kāṅkṣati toyaṃ ca taṃ tṛṣṇārditam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.4"> sakṣobhaśokaśramamadyapānādrūkṣāmlaśuṣkoṣṇakaṭūpayogāt |
            <caesura/>
             dhātukṣayāllaṅghanasūryatāpāt pittaṃ ca vātaś ca bhṛśaṃ pravṛddhau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.5"> srotāṃsi saṃdūṣayataḥ sametau yānyambuvāhīni śarīriṇāṃ hi |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsvapāṃvāhiṣu dūṣiteṣu jāyeta tṛṣṇātibalā tatas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.6"> tisraḥ smṛtāstāḥ kṣatajā caturthī kṣayāt tathānyām asamudbhavā ca |
            <caesura/>
             syāt saptamī bhaktanimittajā tu nibodha liṅgāny anupūrvaśas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.7"> tālvoṣṭhakaṇṭhāsyaviśoṣadāhāḥ saṃtāpamohabhramavipralāpāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti tāsām utpattikāleṣu viśeṣatas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.8"> śuṣkāsyatā mārutasaṃbhavāyāṃ todas tathā śaṅkhaśiraḥsu cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             srotonirodho virasaṃ ca vaktraṃ śītabhir adbhiś ca vivṛddhim eti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.9"> mūrcchāpralāpārucivaktraśoṣāḥ pītekṣaṇatvaṃ pratataś ca dāhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītābhikāṅkṣā mukhatiktatā ca pittātmikāyāṃ paridhūpanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.10"> kaphāvṛtābhyāmanilānalābhyāṃ kapho 'pi śuṣkaḥ prakaroti tṛṣṇām |
            <caesura/>
             nidrā gurutvaṃ madhurāsyatā ca tayārditaḥ śuṣyati cātimātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.11"> kaṇṭhopalepo mukhapicchilatvaṃ śītajvaraś chardirarocakaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphātmikāyāṃ gurugātratā ca śākhāsu śophastvavipāka eva |
            <caesura/>
             etāni rūpāṇi bhavanti tasyāṃ tayārditaḥ kāṅkṣati nāti cāmbhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.12"> kṣatasya rukśoṇitanirgamābhyāṃ tṛṣṇā caturthī kṣatajā matā tu |
            <caesura/>
             tayābhibhūtasya niśādināni gacchanti duḥkhaṃ pibato 'pi toyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.13"> rasakṣayādyā kṣayajā matā sā tayārditaḥ śuṣyati dahyate ca |
            <caesura/>
             atyarthamākāṅkṣati cāpi toyaṃ tāṃ sannipātād itikecidāhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.14"> rasakṣayoktāni ca lakṣaṇāni tasyāmaśeṣeṇa bhiṣagvyavasyet |
            <caesura/>
             tridoṣaliṅgāmasamudbhavā ca hṛcchūlaniṣṭhīvanasādayuktā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.15"> snigdhaṃ tathāmlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca bhuktaṃ gurvannamevātitṛṣāṃ karoti |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇaṃ vicittaṃ badhiraṃ tṛṣārtaṃ vivarjayennirgatajihvamāśu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.16"> tṛṣṇābhivṛddhāvudare ca pūrṇe taṃ vāmayenmāgadhikodakena |
            <caesura/>
             vilobhanaṃ cātra hitaṃ vidheyaṃ syāddāḍimāmrātakamātuluṅgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.17"> tisraḥ prayogairiha sannivāryāḥ śītaiś ca samyag rasavīryajātaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gaṇḍūṣamamlairvirase ca vaktre kuryāc chubhairāmalakasya cūrṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.18"> suvarṇarūpyādibhir agnitaptairloṣṭaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā sikatādibhir vā |
            <caesura/>
             jalaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ śamayet tu tṛṣṇāṃ saśarkaraṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.19"> pañcāṅgikāḥ pañcagaṇā ya uktāsteṣv ambu siddhaṃ prathame gaṇe vā |
            <caesura/>
             pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ manujo 'cireṇa tṛṣo vimucyeta hi vātajāyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.20"> pittaghnavargais tu kṛtaḥ kaṣāyaḥ saśarkaraḥ kṣaudrayutaḥ suśītaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             pītastṛṣāṃ pittakṛtāṃ nihanti kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ vāpy atha jīvanīyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.21"> bilvāḍhakīkanyakapañcamūlīdarbheṣu siddhaṃ kaphajāṃ nihanti |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ bhavec chardanam eva cātra taptena nimbaprasavodakena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.22"> sarvāsu tṛṣṇāsvathavāpi paittaṃ kuryād vidhiṃ tena hi tā na santi
            |
            <caesura/>
             paryāgatodumbarajo rasas tu saśarkaratatkvathitodakaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.23"> vargasya siddhasya ca sārivādeḥ pātavyamambhaḥ śiśiraṃ tṛṣārtaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaśeruśṛṅgāṭakapadmamocabisekṣusiddhaṃ vāṃ nihanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.24"> lājotpalośīrakucandanāni dattvā pravāte niśi vāsayet tu |
            <caesura/>
             taduttamaṃ toyamudāragandhi sitāyutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ vadanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.25"> drākṣāpragāḍhaṃ ca hitāya vaidyas tṛṣṇārditebhyo vitaren narebhyaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             sasārivādau tṛṇapañcamūle tathotpalādau prathame gaṇe ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.26"> kuryāt kaṣāyaṃ ca yatheritena madhūkapuṣpādiṣu cāpareṣu |
            <caesura/>
             rājādanakṣīrikapītaneṣu ṣaṭ pānakānyatra hitāni ca syuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.27"> satuṇḍikerāṇyathavā pibet tu piṣṭāni kārpāsasamudbhavāni |
            <caesura/>
             kṣatodbhavāṃ rugvinivāraṇena jayed rasānāmasṛjaś ca pānaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.28"> kṣayotthitāṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ nihanyānmāṃsodakaṃ vā madhukodakaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             āmodbhavāṃ bilvavacāyutais tu jayet kaṣāyairatha dīpanīyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.29"> āmrātabhallātabalāyutāni pibet kaṣāyāṇyatha dīpanāni |
            <caesura/>
             gurvannajātāṃ vamanairjayec ca kṣayādṛte sarvakṛtāṃ ca tṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.30"> śramodbhavāṃ māṃsaraso nihanti guḍodakaṃ vāpy athavāpi manthaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhaktoparodhāttṛṣito yavāgūmuṣṇāṃ piben manthamatho himaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.31"> yā snehapītasya bhavec ca tṛṣṇā tatroṣṇamambhaḥ prapiben manuṣyaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             madyodbhavāmardhajalaṃ nihanti madyaṃ tṛṣāṃ yāpi ca madyapasya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.32"> tṛṣṇodbhavāṃ hanti jalaṃ suśītaṃ saśarkaraṃ sekṣurasaṃ tathāmbhaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             svaiḥ svaiḥ kaṣāyairvamanāni tāsāṃ tathā jvaroktāni ca pācanāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.33"> lepāvagāhau pariṣecanāni kuryāt tathā śītagṛhāṇi cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             saṃśodhanaṃ kṣīrarasau ghṛtāni sarvāsu lehānmadhurān himāṃś ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre (daśamo
            'dhyāyaḥ āditaḥ) aṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||48 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="49" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.1"> athātaś chardipratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.3"> atidravairatisnigdhairahṛdyairlavaṇairati |
            <caesura/>
             akāle cātimātraiś ca tathāsātmyaiś ca bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.4"> śramāt kṣayāt tathodvegād ajīrṇāt kṛmidoṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nāryāś cāpannasattvāyās tathātidrutam aśnataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.5"> atyantāmaparītasya chardervai saṃbhavo dhruvam |
            <caesura/>
             (bībhatsairhetubhiś cānyairdrutamutkleśito balāt ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.6"> chādayannānanaṃ vegairardayannaṅgabhañjanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nirucyate chardir iti doṣo vaktrād viniścaran || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.7"> doṣānudīrayan vṛddhānudāno vyānasaṅgataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ūrdhvamāgacchati bhṛśaṃ viruddhāhārasevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.8"> praseko hṛdayotkleśo bhaktasyānabhinandanam |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvarūpaṃ mataṃ chardyā yathāsvaṃ ca vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.9"> pracchardayet phenilamalpamalpaṃ śūlārdito 'bhyarditapārśvapṛṣṭhaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             śrāntaḥ saghoṣaṃ bahuśaḥ kaṣāyaṃ jīrṇe 'dhikaṃ sānilajā vamis tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.10"> yo 'mlaṃ bhṛśaṃ vā kaṭutiktavaktraḥ pītaṃ saraktaṃ haritaṃ vamedvā
            |
            <caesura/>
             sadāhacoṣajvaravaktraśoṣo mūrcchānvitaḥ pittanimittajā sā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.11"> yo hṛṣṭaromā madhuraṃ prabhūtaṃ śuklaṃ himaṃ sāndrakaphānuviddham
            |
            <caesura/>
             abhaktaruggauravasādayukto vamedvamī sā kaphakopajā syāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.12"> sarvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti yasyāṃ sā sarvadoṣaprabhavā matā tu |
            <caesura/>
             bībhatsajā dauhṛdajāmajā ca sātmyaprakopāt kṛmijā ca yā hi |
            <caesura/>
             sā pañcamī tāṃ ca vibhāvayet tu doṣocchrayeṇaiva yathoktamādau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.13"> śūlahṛllāsabahulā kṛmijā ca viśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmihṛdrogatulyena lakṣaṇena ca lakṣitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.14"> kṣīṇasyopadravairyuktāṃ sāsṛkpūyāṃ sacandrikām |
            <caesura/>
             chardiṃ prasaktāṃ kuśalo nārabheta cikitsitum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.15"> āmāśayotkleśabhavā hi sarvāstasmād dhitaṃ laṅghanam eva tāsu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.16"> vamīṣu bahudoṣāsu chardanaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             virecanaṃ vā kurvīta yathādoṣocchrayaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.17"> saṃsargaś cānupūrveṇa yathāsvaṃ bheṣajāyutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             laghūni pariśuṣkāṇi sātmyānyannāni cācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.18"> yathāsvaṃ ca kaṣāyāṇi jvaraghnāni prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             hanyāt kṣīraghṛtaṃ pītaṃ chardiṃ pavanasaṃbhavām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.19"> sasaindhavaṃ pibet sarpirvātacchardinivāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             mudgāmalakayūṣo vā sasarpiṣkaḥ sasaindhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yavāgūṃ madhumiśrāṃ vā pañcamūlīkṛtāṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.20"> pibedvā vyaktasindhūtthaṃ phalāmlaṃ vaiṣkiraṃ rasam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇalavaṇaṃ cātra hitaṃ snehavirecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.21"> pittopaśamanīyāni pākyāni śiśirāṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyāṇyupayuktāni ghnanti pittakṛtāṃ vamīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.22"> śodhanaṃ madhuraiś cātra drākṣārasasam āyutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             balavatyāṃ praśaṃsanti sarpis tailvakam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.23"> āragvadhādiniryūhaṃ daśāṅgayogam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayetātha sakṣaudraṃ kaphajāyāṃ cikitsakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.24"> kṛtaṃ guḍūcyā vidhivat kaṣāyaṃ himasaṃjñitam |
            <caesura/>
             tisṛṣv api bhavet pathyaṃ mākṣikeṇa samanvitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.25"> bībhatsajāṃ hṛdyatamairdauhṛdīṃ kāṅkṣitaiḥ phalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             laṅghanairvamanaiś cāmāṃ sātmyaiḥ sātmyaprakopajām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.26"> kṛmihṛdrogavac cāpi kṛmijāṃ sādhayed vamīm |
            <caesura/>
             vitarec ca yathādoṣaṃ śastaṃ vidhimanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.27"> dadhittharasasṃsaktāṃ pippalīṃ mākṣikānvitām |
