            <caesura/>
             muhurmuhurnaro līḍhvā chardibhyaḥ pravimucyate(pratimucyate) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.28"> samākṣikā madhurasā pītā vā taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ vā madhuyutaṃ tisṛṇām api bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.29"> svayaṅguptāṃ sayaṣṭyāhvāṃ taṇḍulāmbumadhudravām |
            <caesura/>
             pibed yavāgūm athavā siddhāṃ patraiḥ karañjajaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.30"> yuktāmlalavaṇāḥ piṣṭāḥ kustumburyo 'thavā hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyutaṃ khādet kapitthaṃ tryūṣaṇena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.31"> sitācandanamadhvāktaṃ lihyād vā makṣikāśakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             pibet payo 'gnitaptaṃ ca nirvāpya gṛhagodhikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.32"> sarpiḥkṣaudrayutān vāpi lājaśaktūn pibet tathā |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥkṣaudrasitopetāṃ māgadhīṃ vā lihet tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.33"> dhātrīrase candanaṃ vā ghṛṣṭaṃ mudgadalāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             kolāmalakamajjānaṃ lihyādvā trisugandhikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.34"> sakṣaudrāṃ śālilājānāṃ yavagūṃ vā piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ghreyāṇyupaharec cāpi manoghrāṇasukhāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.35"> jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni śubhāni pānakāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             bhojanāni vicitrāṇi kuryāt sarvāsvatandritaḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            chardipratiṣedho nāma (ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||49 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="50" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.1"> athāto hikkāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.3"> vidāhiguruviṣṭambhir ūkṣābhiṣyandibhojanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītapānāsanasthānarajodhūmānilānalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.4"> vyāyāmakarmabhārādhvavegāghātāpatarpaṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āmadoṣābhighātastrīkṣayadoṣaprapīḍanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.5"> viṣamāśanādhyanaśanais tathā samaśanair api |
            <caesura/>
             hikkā śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca nṛṇāṃ samupajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.6"> muhurmuhurvāyurudeti sasvano yakṛtplihāntrāṇi mukhādivākṣipan |
            <caesura/>
             sa ghoṣavānāśu hinastyasūn yatastatas tu hikketi bhiṣagbhir ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.7"> annajāṃ yamalāṃ kṣudrāṃ gambhīrāṃ mahatīṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             vāyuḥ kaphenānugataḥ pañca hikkāḥ karoti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.8"> mukhaṃ kaṣāyamaratirgauravaṃ kaṇṭhavakṣasoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvarūpāṇi hikkānāmāṭopo jaṭharasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.9"> tvaramāṇasya cāhāraṃ bhuñjānasyāthavā ghanam |
            <caesura/>
             vāyurannairavastīrṇaḥ kaṭukairardito bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.10"> hikkayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā tāṃ vidyādannajāṃ bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             cireṇa yamalairvegairyā hikkā saṃpravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.11"> kampayantī śirogrīvaṃ yamalāṃ tāṃ vinirdiśet |
            <caesura/>
             vikṛṣṭakālairyā vegairmandaiḥ samabhivartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.12"> kṣudrikā nāma sā hikkā jatrumūlāt pradhāvitā |
            <caesura/>
             nābhipravṛttā yā hikkā ghorā gambhīranādinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.13"> śuṣkauṣṭhakaṇṭhajihvāsyaśvāsapārśvarujākarī |
            <caesura/>
             anekopadravayutā gambhīrā nāma sā smṛtā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.14"> marmāṇyāpīḍayantīva satataṃ yā pravartate |
            <caesura/>
             dehamāyamya vegena ghoṣayatyatitṛṣyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mahāhikketi sā jñeyā sarvagātraprakampinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.15"> āyamyate hikkato 'ṅgāni yasya dṛṣṭiś cordhvaṃ tāmyate yasya gāḍham
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇo 'nnadviṭ kāsate yaś ca hikkī tau dvāvantyau varjayed dhikkamānau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.16"> prāṇāyāmodvejanatrāsanāni sūcītodaiḥ saṃbhramaś cātra śastaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭyāhvaṃ vā mākṣikeṇāvapīḍe pippalyo vā śarkarācūrṇayuktāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.17"> sarpiḥ koṣṇaṃ kṣīramikṣo raso vā nātikṣīṇe chardanaṃ śāntihetoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nārīpayaḥpiṣṭamaśuklacandanaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sasaindhavaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.18"> cūrṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavamambhasāthavā nihanti hikkāṃ ca hitaṃ ca
            nasyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yuñjyāddhūmaṃ śālaniryāsajātaṃ naipālaṃ vā goviṣāṇodbhavaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.19"> sarpiḥsnigdhaiś carmabālaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā hikkāsthāne svedanaṃ cāpi
            kāryam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudropetaṃ gairikaṃ kāñcanāhvaṃ lihyādbhasma grāmyasattvāsthijaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.20"> tadvacchvāvinmeṣagośalyakānāṃ(gośallakānāṃ)
            romāṇyantardhūmadagdhāni cātra |
            <caesura/>
             madhvājyāktaṃ barhipatraprasūtamevaṃ bhasmaudumbaraṃ tailvakaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.21"> svarjikṣāraṃ bījapūrādrasena kṣaudropetaṃ hanti līḍhvāśu hikkām |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥsnigdhā ghnanti hikkāṃ yavāgvaḥ koṣṇagrāsāḥ pāyaso vā sukhoṣṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.22"> śuṇṭhītoye sādhitaṃ kṣīramājaṃ tadvat pītaṃ śarkarāsaṃyutaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             ātṛptervā sevyamānaṃ nihantyād ghrātaṃ hikkāmāśu mūtraṃ tvajāvyoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.23"> sapūtikīṭaṃ laśunogragandhāhiṅgvabjamācūrṇya subhāvitaṃ tat |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudraṃ sitāṃ vāraṇakeśaraṃ ca pibedrasenekṣumadhūkajena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.24"> pibet palaṃ vā lavaṇottamasya dvābhyāṃ palābhyāṃ haviṣaḥ samagram
            |
            <caesura/>
             harītakīṃ koṣṇajalānupānāṃ pibed ghṛtaṃ kṣāramadhūpapannam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.25"> rasaṃ kapitthānmadhupippalībhyāṃ śuktipramāṇaṃ prapibet sukhāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.26"> kṛṣṇāṃ sitāṃ cāmalakaṃ ca līḍhaṃ saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhunāthavāpi |
            <caesura/>
             kolāsthimajjāñjanalājacūrṇaṃ hikkā nihanyānmadhunāvalīḍham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.27"> pāṭalāyāḥ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ gairikaṃ kaṭurohiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             kharjūramadhyaṃ māgadhyaḥ kāśīśaṃ dadhināma ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.28"> catvāra ete yogāḥ syuḥ pratipādapradarśitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhudvitīyāḥ kartavyāste hikkāsu vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.29"> kapotapārāvatalāvaśaka(lla)śvadaṃṣṭragodhāvṛṣadaṃśajān rasān |
            <caesura/>
             pibet phalāmlānahimān sasaindhavān snigdhāṃs tathaiva rṣyamṛgadvijodbhavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.30"> virecanaṃ pathyatamaṃ sasaindhavaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca
            sitopalāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sadāgatāvūrdhvagate 'nuvāsanaṃ vadanti kecic ca hitāya hikkinām ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            hikkāpratiṣedho nāma (dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||50 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="51" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.1"> athātaḥ śvāsapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.3"> yair eva kāraṇairhikkā bahubhiḥ saṃpravartate |
            <caesura/>
             tair eva kāraṇaiḥ śvāso ghoro bhavati dehinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.4"> vihāya prakṛtiṃ vāyuḥ prāṇo 'tha kaphasaṃyutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śvāsayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā taṃ śvāsaṃ paricakṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.5"> kṣudrakastamakaś chinno mahānūrdhvaś ca pañcadhā |
            <caesura/>
             bhidyate sa mahāvyādhiḥ śvāsa eko viśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.6"> prāgrūpaṃ tasya hṛtpīḍā bhaktadveṣo 'ratiḥ parā |
            <caesura/>
             ānāhaḥ pārśvayoḥ śūlaṃ vairasyaṃ vadanasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.7"> kiñcidārabhamāṇasya yasya śvāsaḥ pravartate |
            <caesura/>
             niṣaṇṇasyaiti śāntiṃ ca sa kṣudra iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.8"> tṛṭsvedavamathuprāyaḥ kaṇṭhaghurghurikānvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣāddurdine tāmyec chvāsaḥ sa tamako mataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.9"> ghoṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ sakāsaḥ sakapho naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yaḥ śvasity abalo 'nnadviṭ suptas tamakapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.10"> sa śāmyati kaphe hīne svapataś ca vidhardhate |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchājvarābhibhūtasya jñeyaḥ pratamakas tu saḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.11"> ādhmāto dahyamānena bastinā sarujaṃ naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaprāṇena vicchinnaṃ śvasyācchinnaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.12"> niḥsaṃjñaḥ pārśvaśūlārtaḥ śuṣkakaṇṭho 'tighoṣavān |
            <caesura/>
             saṃrabdhanetrastvāyamya yaḥ śvasyāt sa mahān smṛtaḥ | </l>
          <l/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.13"> marmasv āyamyamāneṣu śvasan mūḍho muhuś ca yaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ūrdhvaprekṣī hataravas tam ūrdhvaśvāsam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.14"> kṣudraḥ sādhyatamas teṣāṃ tamakaḥ kṛcchra ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             trayaḥ śvāsā na sidhyanti tamako durbalasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.15"> snehabastiṃ vinā kecidūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdu rāṇavatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvāsināmādiśanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.16"> śvāse kāse ca hikkāyāṃ hṛdroge cāpi pūjitam |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaṃ purāṇaṃ saṃsiddhamabhayāviḍarāmaṭhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.17"> sauvarcalābhayābilvaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vānavaṃ ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ vā prathame gaṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.18"> sapañcalavaṇaṃ sarpiḥ śvāsakāsau vyapohati |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsrāviḍaṅgapūtīkatriphalāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.19"> dvikṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ sarpiś caturguṇajalāplutam |
            <caesura/>
             kolamātraiḥ pibettaddhi śvāsakāsau vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.20"> arśāṃsyarocakaṃ gulmaṃ śakṛdbhedaṃ kṣayaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtsne vṛṣakaṣāye vā pacet sarpiś caturguṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.21"> tanmūlakusumāvāpaṃ śītaṃ kṣaudreṇa yojayet |
            <caesura/>
             śṛṅgīmadhūlikābhārgīśuṇṭhītārkṣyasitāmbudaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.22"> saharidraiḥ sayaṣṭyāhvaiḥ samairāvāpya yogataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaprasthaṃ paceddhīmān śītatoye caturguṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.23"> śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ tathā hikkāṃ sarpiretanniyacchati |
            <caesura/>
             suvahā kālikā bhargī śukākhyā naiculaṃ phalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.24"> kākādanī śṛṅgaveraṃ varṣabhūrbṛhatīdvayam |
            <caesura/>
             kolamātrairghṛtaprasthaṃ pacedebhir jaladvikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.25"> kaṭūṣṇaṃ pītam etad dhi śvāsāmayavināśanam |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalayavakṣārakaṭukāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.26"> vacābhayāviḍaṅgaiś ca sādhitaṃ śvāsaśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             gopavally udake siddhaṃ syād anyad dviguṇe ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.27"> pañcaitāni havīṃṣyāhurbhiṣajaḥ śvāsakāsayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tālīśatāmalakyugrājīvantīkuṣṭhasaindhavaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.28"> bilvapuṣkarabhūtīkasauvarcalakaṇāgnibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pathyā tejovatī yuktaiḥ sarpirjalacaturguṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.29"> hiṅgupādayutaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaśvāsaharaṃ param |
            <caesura/>
             vāsāghṛtaṃ ṣaṭpalaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ cātra hitaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.30"> tailaṃ daśaguṇe siddhaṃ bhṛṅgarājarase śubhe |
            <caesura/>
             sevyamānaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śvāsakāsau vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.31"> phalāmlā viṣkirarasāḥ snigdhāḥ pravyaktasaindhavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṇādīnāṃ śirobhir vā kaulatthā vā susaṃskṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.32"> hanyuḥ śvāsaṃ ca kāsaṃ ca saṃskṛtāni payāṃsi ca |
            <caesura/>
             timirasya ca bījāni karkaṭākhyā ca cūrṇitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.33"> durālabhātha pippalyaḥ kaṭukākhyā harītakī |
            <caesura/>
             śvāvinmayūraromāṇi kolā māgadhikākaṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.34"> bhārgītvak śṛṅgaveraṃ ca śarkarā śallakāṅgajam |
            <caesura/>
             nṛttakauṇḍakabījāni cūrṇitāni tu kevalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.35"> pañca ślokārdhikāstvete lehā ye samyag īritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ te lehyāḥ kāsaśvāsārditairnaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.36"> saptacchadasya puṣpāṇi pippalīś cāpi mastunā |
            <caesura/>
             pibet saṃcūrṇya madhunā dhānāś cāpy atha bhakṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.37"> arkāṅkurairbhāvitānāṃ yavānāṃ sādhvanekaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ vā pibedeṣāṃ sakṣaudraṃ śvāsapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.38"> śirīṣakadalīkundapuṣpaṃ māgadhikāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyutaṃ pītvā jayec chvāsānaśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.39"> kolamajjāṃ tālamūlamṛṣyacarmamasīm api |
            <caesura/>
             lihyāt kṣaudreṇa bhārgīṃ vā sarpirmadhusamāyutām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.40"> nīcaiḥkadambabījaṃ vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ harītakīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ karkaṭākhyāṃ durālabhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.41"> sarpirmadhubhyāṃ vilihan hanti śvāsān sudāruṇān |
            <caesura/>
             haridrāṃ maricaṃ drākṣāṃ guḍaṃ rāsnāṃ kaṇāṃ śaṭīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.42"> lihyāttailena tulyāni śvāsārto hitabhojanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gavāṃ purīṣasvarasaṃ madhusarpiḥkaṇāyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.43"> lihyācchvāsseṣu kāseṣu vājināṃ vā śakṛdrasam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṇḍurogeṣu śotheṣu ye yogāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.44"> śvāsakāsāpahāste 'pi kāsaghnā ye ca kīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhārgītvak tryūṣaṇaṃ tailaṃ haridrāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.45"> pippalīṃ maricaṃ caṇḍāṃ gośakṛdrasam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             talakoṭasya bījeṣu pacedutkārikāṃ śubhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.46"> sevyamānā nihantyeṣā śvāsānāśu sudustarān |
            <caesura/>
             purāṇasarpiḥ pippalyaḥ kaulatthā jāṅgalā rasāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.47"> surā sauvīrakaṃ hiṅgu mātuluṅgaraso madhu |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāmalakabilvāni śastāni śvāsihikkinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.48"> śvāsahikkāparigataṃ snigdhaiḥ svedair upācaret |
            <caesura/>
             āktaṃ lavaṇatailābhyāṃ tairasya grathitaḥ kaphaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.49"> khastho vilayanaṃ yāti mārutaś ca praśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             svinnaṃ jñātvā tataś caiva bhojayitvā rasaudanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.50"> vātaśleṣmavibandhe vā bhiṣag dhūmaṃ prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             manaḥśilādevadāruharidrācchadanāmiṣaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.51"> lākṣorubūkamūlaiś ca kṛtvā vartīr vidhānataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiryavamadhūcchiṣṭaśālaniryāsajaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.52"> śṛṅgabālakhurasnāyutvak samastaṃ gavām api |
            <caesura/>
             turuṣkaśallakīnāṃ ca gugguloḥ padmakasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.53"> ete sarve sasarpiṣkā dhūmāḥ kāryā vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             balīyasi kaphagraste vamanaṃ savirecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.54"> durbale caiva rūkṣe ca tarpaṇaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             jāṅgalorabhrajairmāṃsairānūpair vā susaṃskṛtaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.55"> nidigdhikāṃ cāmalakapramāṇāṃ hiṅgvardhayuktāṃ madhunā suyuktām |
            <caesura/>
             lihan naraḥ śvāsanipīḍito hi śvāsaṃ jayaty eva balāttryaheṇa || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.56"> yathāgniriddhaḥ pavanānuviddho vajraṃ yathā vā surarājamuktam |
            <caesura/>
             rogāstathaite khalu durnivārāḥ śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca vilambikā ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            hikkāśvāsapratiṣedho nāma (tryodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||51
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="52" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.1"> athātaḥ kāsapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.3"> uktā ye hetavo nṝṇāṃ rogayoḥ śvāsahikkayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kāsasyāpi ca vijñeyāsta evotpattihetavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.4"> dhūmopaghātādrajasas tathaiva vyāyāmarūkṣānnaniṣevaṇāc ca |
            <caesura/>
             vimārgagatvād api bhojanasya vegāvarodhāt kṣavathos tathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.5"> prāṇo hyudānānugataḥ praduṣṭaḥ saṃbhinnakāṃsyasvanatulyaghoṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nireti vaktrāt sahasā sadoṣaḥ kāsaḥ sa vidvadbhir udāhṛtas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.6"> sa vātapittaprabhavaḥ kaphāc ca kṣatāttathānyaḥ kṣayajo 'paraś ca |
            <caesura/>
             pañcaprakāraḥ kathito bhiṣagbhir vivardhito yakṣmavikārakṛt syāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.7"> bhaviṣyatas tasya tu kaṇṭhakaṇḍūrbhojyoparodho galatālulepaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svaśabdavaiṣamyamarocako 'gnisādaś ca liṅgāni bhavantyamūni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.8"> hṛcchaṅkhamūrdhodarapārśvaśūlī kṣāmānanaḥ kṣīṇabalasvaraujāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prasaktamantaḥkaphamīraṇena kāset tu śuṣkaṃ svarabhedayuktaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.9"> urovidāhajvaravaktraśoṣairabhyarditastiktamukhastṛṣārtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pītāni vamet kaṭūni kāset sa pāṇḍuḥ paridahyamānaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.10"> pralipyamānena(vilipyamānena) mukhena sīdan śirorujārtaḥ
            kaphapūrṇadehaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             abhaktaruggauravasādayuktaḥ kāseta nā sāndrakaphaṃ kaphena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.11"> vakṣo 'timātraṃ vihataṃ tu yasya vyāyāmabhārādhyayanābhighātaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśliṣṭavakṣāḥ sa naraḥ saraktaṃ ṣṭhīvatyabhīkṣṇaṃ kṣatajaṃ tamūhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.12"> sa gātraśūlajvaradāhamohān prāṇakṣayaṃ copalabheta kāsī |
            <caesura/>
             śuṣyan viniṣṭhīvati durbalas tu prakṣīṇamāṃso rudhiraṃ sapūyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.13"> sasarvaliṅgaṃ bhṛśaduś cikitsyaṃ cikitsitajñāḥ kṣayajaṃ vadanti |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddhatvamāsādya bhavet tu yo vai yāpyaṃ tamāhurbhiṣajas tu kāsam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.14"> śṛṅgīvacākaṭphalakattṛṇābdadhānyābhayābhārgyamarāhvaviśvam |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmbunā hiṅguyutaṃ tu pītvā baddhāsyamapyāśu jahāti kāsam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.15"> phalatrikavyoṣaviḍaṅgaśṛṅgīrāsnāvacāpadmakadevakāṣṭhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lehaḥ samaiḥ kṣaudrasitāghṛtāktaḥ kāsaṃ nihanyādacirādudīrṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.16"> pathyāṃ sitāmāmalakāni lājāṃ samāgadhīṃ cāpi vicūrṇya śuṇṭhīm |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ vilihīta kāsī sasaindhavāṃ voṣṇajalena kṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.17"> khādedguḍaṃ nāgarapippalībhyāṃ drākṣāṃ ca sarpirmadhunāvalihyāt |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ sitāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca tulyāṃ saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhukaṃ tugāṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.18"> lihyād ghṛtakṣaudrayutāṃ samāṃśāṃ sitopalāṃ vā maricāṃśayuktām |
            <caesura/>
             dhātrīkaṇāviśvasitopalāś ca saṃcūrṇya maṇḍena pibec ca dadhnaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.19"> hareṇukāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca tulyāṃ dadhnā pibet kāsagadābhibhūtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ubhe haridre suradāruśuṇṭhīṃ gāyatrisāraṃ ca pibet samāṃśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.20"> bastasya mūtreṇa sukhāmbunā vā dantīṃ dravantīṃ ca satilvakākhyām
            |
            <caesura/>
             bhṛṣṭāni sarpīṃṣyatha bādarāṇi khādet palāśāni sasaindhavāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.21"> kolapramāṇaṃ prapibeddhi hiṅgu sauvīrakeṇāmlarasena vāpi |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudreṇa lihyānmaricāni vāpi bhārgīvacāhiṅgukṛtā ca vartiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.22"> dhūme praśastā ghṛtasaṃprayuktā veṇutvagelālavaṇaiḥ kṛtā vā |
            <caesura/>
             musteṅgudītvaṅmadhukāhvamāṃsīmanaḥśilālaiś chagalāmbupiṣṭaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.23"> vidhāya vartīś ca payo 'nupānaṃ dhūmaṃ pibedvātabalāsakāsī |
            <caesura/>
             pibec ca sīdhuṃ maricānvitaṃ vā tenāśu kāsaṃ jayati prasahya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.24"> drākṣāmbumañjiṣṭhapurāhvayābhiḥ kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktam |
            <caesura/>
             nidigdhikānāgarapippalībhiḥ khādec ca mudgānmadhunā susiddhān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.25"> utkārikāṃ sarpiṣi nāgarāḍhyāṃ paktvā samūlaistruṭikolapatraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ebhir niṣeveta kṛtāṃ ca peyāṃ tanvīṃ suśītāṃ madhunā vimiśrām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.26"> yat plīhni sarpirvihitaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ tadvātakāsaṃ jayati prasahya |
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhādikṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā rasena vā vāsakajena pakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.27"> virecanaṃ snaihikamatra coktamāsthāpanaṃ cāpy anuvāsanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             dhūmaṃ pibet snaihikamapramattaḥ pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ ghṛtam eva cātra || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.28"> hitā yavāgvaś ca raseṣu siddhāḥ payāṃsi lehāḥ saghṛtās tathaiva |
            <caesura/>
             pracchardanaṃ kāyaśirovirekās tathaiva dhūmāḥ kavalagrahāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.29"> uṣṇāś ca lehāḥ kaṭukā nihanyuḥ kaphaṃ viśeṣeṇa viśoṣaṇaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭutrikaṃ cāpi vadanti pathyaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṛmighnasvarase vipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.30"> nirguṇḍipatrasvarase ca pakvaṃ sarpiḥ kaphotthaṃ vinihanti kāsam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhāviḍavyoṣaviḍaṅgasindhutrikaṇṭarāsnāhutabhugbalābhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.31"> śṛṅgīvacāmbhodharadevadārudurālabhābhārgyabhayaśaṭībhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             samyag vipakvaṃ dviguṇena sarpirnidigdhikāyāḥ svarasena caitat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.32"> śvāsāgnisādasvarabhedabhinnānnihantyudīrṇānapi pañca kāsān |
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhotpalasārivādīn niṣkvāthya vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.33"> ghṛtaṃ pacedikṣurasāmbudugdhaiḥ kākolivarge ca saśarkaraṃ tat |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ pibet pittakṛte ca kāse ratiprasūte kṣataje ca kāse || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.34"> kharjūrabhārgīmagadhāpriyālamadhūlikailāmalakaiḥ samāṃśaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ sitākṣaudraghṛtaprāgāḍhaṃ trīn hanti kāsānupayujyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.35"> raktāharidrāñjanavahnipāṭhāmūrvopakulyā vilihet samāṃśāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudreṇa kāse kṣataje kṣayotthe pibed ghṛtaṃ cekṣurase vipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.36"> cūrṇaṃ pibed āmalakasya vāpi kṣīreṇa pakvaṃ saghṛtaṃ hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇāni godhūmayavodbhavāni kākolivargaś ca kṛtaḥ susūkṣmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.37"> kāseṣu peyastriṣu kāsavadbhiḥ kṣīreṇa sakṣaudraghṛtena vāpi |
            <caesura/>
             guḍodakaṃ vā kvathitaṃ pibeddhi kṣaudreṇa śītaṃ maricopadaṃśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.38"> prasthatrayeṇāmalakīrasasya śuddhasya dattvārdhatulāṃ guḍasya |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇīkṛtairgranthikacavyajīravyoṣebhakṛṣṇāhapuṣājamodaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.39"> viḍaṅgasindhutriphalāyavānīpāṭhāgnidhānyaiś ca picupramāṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dattvā trivṛccūrṇapalāni cāṣṭāvaṣṭau ca tailasya pacedyathāvat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.40"> taṃ bhakṣayed akṣaphalapramāṇaṃ yatheṣṭaceṣṭastrisugandhiyuktam |
            <caesura/>
             anena sarve grahaṇīvikārāḥ saśvāsakāsasvarabhedaśothāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.41"> śāmyanti cāyaṃ ciramantaragnerhatasya puṃstvasya ca vṛddhihetuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             strīṇāṃ ca vandhyāmayanāśanaḥ syāt kalyāṇako nāma guḍaḥ pratītaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.42"> dvipañcamūlebhakaṇātmaguptābhārgīśaṭīpuṣkaramūlaviśvān |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhāmṛtāgranthikaśaṅkhapuṣpīrāsnāgnyapāmārgabalāyavāsān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.43"> dvipālikān nyasya yavāḍhakaṃ ca harītakīnāṃ ca śataṃ gurūṇām |
            <caesura/>
             droṇe jalasyāḍhakasaṃyute ca kvāthe kṛte pūtacaturthabhāge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.44"> pacettulāṃ śuddhaguḍasya dattvā pṛthak ca tailāt kuḍavaṃ ghṛtāc ca
            |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ ca tāvan magadhodbhavāyā deyaṃ ca tasmin madhu siddhaśīte || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.45"> rasāyanāt karṣamato vilihyāddve cābhaye nityam athāśu hanyāt |
            <caesura/>
             tad rājayakṣmagrahaṇīpradoṣaśophāgnimāndyasvarabhedakāsān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.46"> pāṇḍvāmayaśvāsaśirovikārān hṛdrogahikkāviṣam ajvarāṃś ca |
            <caesura/>
             medhābalotsāham atipradaṃ ca cakāra caitad bhagavān agastyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.47"> kulīraśuktīcaṭakaiṇalāvānniṣkvāthya vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam |
            <caesura/>
             pacedghṛtaṃ tat tu niṣevyamāṇaṃ hanyāt kṣatotthaṃ kṣayajaṃ ca kāsam ||
            śatāvarīnāgabalāvipakvaṃ ghṛtaṃ vidheyaṃ ca hitāya kāsinām | </l>
          <l/>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            kāsapratiṣedho nāma (caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||52 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="53" type="adhyāya">
          <head>tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.1"> athātaḥ svarabhedapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.3"> atyuc cabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanātigītaśītādibhiḥ prakupitāḥ pavanādayas
            tu |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.4"> vātena kṛṣṇanayanānanamūtravarcā bhinnaṃ śanair vadati gadgadavat
            svaraṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pītavadanākṣipurīṣamūtro brūyād galena paridāhasamanvitena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.5"> kṛcchrāt kaphena satataṃ kapharuddhakaṇṭho mandaṃ śanairvadati cāpi
            divā viśeṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpadavyaktatā ca vacasastamasādhyam āhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.6"> dhūpyeta vāk kṣayakṛte kṣayamāpnuyāc ca vāgeṣa cāpi(vāpi) hatavāk
            parivarjanīyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             antargalaṃ svaramalakṣyapadaṃ cireṇa medaś cayādvadati digdhagalauṣṭhatāluḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.7"> kṣīṇasya vṛddhasya kṛśasya cāpi cirotthito yaś ca sahopajātaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             medasvinaḥ sarvasamudbhavaś ca svarāmayo yo na sa siddhimeti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.8"> snigdhān svarāturanarānapakṛṣṭadoṣān nyāyena tān
            vamanarecanabastibhiś ca |
            <caesura/>
             nasyāvapīḍamukhadhāvanadhūmalehaiḥ saṃpādayec ca vividhaiḥ kavalagrahaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.9ab"> yaḥ śvāsakāsavidhir ādita eva coktas taṃ cāpy aśeṣam avatārayituṃ
            yateta | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.9cd"> vaiśeṣikaṃ ca vidhim ūrdhvam ato vadāmi taṃ vai svarāturahitaṃ
            nikhilaṃ nibodha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.10"> svaropaghāte 'nilaje bhuktopari ghṛtaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             kāsamardakavātārkamārkavasvarase śṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.11"> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ hanty anilaṃ siddham ārtagale rase |
            <caesura/>
             yavakṣārājamodābhyāṃ citrakāmalakeṣu vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.12"> devadārvagnikābhyāṃ vā siddhāmājaṃ samākṣikam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhodakānupāno vā sasarpiṣko guḍaudanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.13"> kṣīrānupānaṃ pitte tu pibet sarpiratandritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aśnīyāc ca sasarpiṣkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukapāyasam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.14"> lihyānmadhurakāṇāṃ vā cūrṇaṃ madhughṛtāplutam |
            <caesura/>
             śatāvarīcūrṇayogaṃ balācūrṇam athāpi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.15"> pibet kaṭūni mūtreṇa kaphaje svarasaṃkṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             lihyādvā madhutailābhyāṃ bhuktvā khādet kaṭūni vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.16"> svaropaghāte medoje kaphavadvidhiriṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaje kṣayaje cāpi pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.16a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.17"> śarkarāmadhumiśrāṇi śṛtāni madhuraiḥ saha |
            <caesura/>
             pibet payāṃsi yasyoc cairvadato 'bhihataḥ svaraḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            chardipratiṣedho nāma (pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||53 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="54" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catuḥpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.1"> athātaḥ kṛmirogapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.3"> ajīrṇādhyaśanāsātmyaviruddhamalināśanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             avyāyāmadivāsvapnagurvatisnigdhaśītalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.3a"/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.3b"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.4"> māṣapiṣṭānnavidalabisaśālūkaserukaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             parṇaśākasurāśuktad adhikṣīraguḍekṣubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.5"> palalānūpapiśitapiṇyākapṛthukādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svādvamladravapānaiś ca śleṣmā pittaṃ ca kupyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.6"> kṛmīn bahuvidhākārān karoti vividhāśrayān |
            <caesura/>
             āmapakvāśaye teṣāṃ kaphaviḍjanmanāṃ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhamanyāṃ raktajānāṃ ca prasavaḥ prāyaśaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.7"> viṃśateḥ kṛmijātīnāṃ trividhaḥ saṃbhavaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             purīṣakapharaktāni tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.8"> ajavā vijavāḥ kipyāś cipyā gaṇḍūpadās tathā |
            <caesura/>
             cūravo dvimukhāś caiva jñeyāḥ sapta purīṣajāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.9"> śvetāḥ sūkṣmāstudantyete gudaṃ pratisaranti ca |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāmevāpare pucchaiḥ pṛthavaś ca bhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.10"> śūlāgnimāndyapāṇḍutvaviṣṭambhabalasaṃkṣayāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prasekārucihṛdrogaviḍbhedās tu purīṣajaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.11"> raktā gaṇḍūpadā dīrghā gudakaṇḍūnipātinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śūlāṭopaśakṛdbhedapaktināśakarāś ca te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.12"> darbhapuṣpā mahāpuṣpāḥ pralūnāś cipiṭās tathā |
            <caesura/>
             pipīlikā dāruṇāś ca kaphakopasamudbhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.13"> romaśā romamūrdhānaḥ sapucchāḥ śyāvamaṇḍalāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rūḍhadhānyāṅkurākārāḥ śuklāste tanavas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.14"> majjādā netraleḍhārastāluśrotrabhujas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śirohṛdrogavamathupratiśyāyakarāś ca te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.15"> keśaromanakhādāś ca dantādāḥ kikkiśās tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhajāḥ saparīsarpā jñeyāḥ śoṇitasaṃbhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.16"> te saraktāś ca kṛṣṇāś ca snigdhāś ca pṛthavas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             raktādhiṣṭhānajān prāyo vikārān janayanti te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.17"> māṣapiṣṭānnavidalaparṇaśākaiḥ purīṣajāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsamāṣaguḍakṣīradadhitailaiḥ kaphodbhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.18"> viruddhājīrṇaśākādyaiḥ śoṇitotthā bhavanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             jvaro vivarṇatā śūlaṃ hṛdrogaḥ sadanaṃ bhramaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.19"> bhaktadveṣo 'tisāraś ca saṃjātakṛmilakṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             dṛśyāstrayodaśādyās tu kṛmīṇāṃ parikīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.20"> keśādādyāstvadṛśyāste dvāvādyau parivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             eṣāmanyatamaṃ jñātvā jighāṃsuḥ snigdhamāturam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.21"> surasādivipakvena sarpiṣā vāntamāditaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             virecayettīkṣṇatarairyogairāsthāpayec ca tam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.22"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ surasādergaṇasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgasnehayuktena kvāthena lavaṇena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.23"> pratyāgate nirūhe tu naraṃ snātaṃ sukhāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             yuñjyāt kṛmighnairaśanais tataḥ śīghraṃ bhiṣagvaraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.23a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.24"> snehenoktena cainaṃ tu yojayet snehabastinā |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ śirīṣakiṇihīrasaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.25"> kevūkasvarasaṃ vāpi pūrvavattīkṣṇabhojanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             palāśabījasvarasaṃ kalkaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.26"> pāribhadrakapatrāṇāṃ kṣaudreṇa svarasaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             pattūrasvarasaṃ vāpi pibedvā surasādijam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.26a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.27"> lihyādaśvaśakṛccūrṇaṃ vaiḍaṅgaṃ vā samākṣikam |
            <caesura/>
             patrairmūṣikaparṇyā vā supiṣṭaiḥ piṣṭamiśritaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.28"> khādet pūpalikāḥ pakvā dhānyāmlaṃ ca pibedanu |
            <caesura/>
             surasādigaṇe pakvaṃ tailaṃ vā pānamiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.29"> viḍaṅgacūrṇayuktair vā piṣṭairbhakṣyāṃs tu kārayet |
            <caesura/>
             tatkaṣāyaprapītānāṃ tilānāṃ sneham eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.30"> śvāvidhaḥ śakṛtaś cūrṇaṃ saptakṛtvaḥ subhāvitam |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgānāṃ kaṣāyeṇa traiphalena tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.31"> kṣaudreṇa līḍhvānupibedrasamāmalakodbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             akṣābhayārasaṃ vāpi vidhireṣo 'yasām api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.32"> pūtīkasvarasaṃ vāpi pibedvā madhunā saha |
            <caesura/>
             pibedvā pippalīmūlamajāmūtreṇa saṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.33"> saptarātraṃ pibed ghṛṣṭaṃ trapu vā dadhimastunā |
            <caesura/>
             purīṣajān kaphotthāṃś ca hanyādevaṃ kṛmīn bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.34"> śirohṛdghrāṇakarṇākṣisaṃśritāṃś ca pṛthagvidhān |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣeṇāñjanairnasyairavapīḍaiś ca sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.35"> śakṛdrasaṃ turaṅgasya suśuṣkaṃ bhāvayed ati |
            <caesura/>
             niṣkvāthena viḍaṅgānāṃ cūrṇaṃ pradhamanaṃ tu tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.36"> ayaś cūrṇānyanenaiva vidhinā yojayed bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             sakāṃsyanīlaṃ tailaṃ ca nasyaṃ syātsurasādike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.37"> indraluptavidhiś cāpi vidheyo romabhojiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             dantādānāṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ vidhānaṃ mukharogikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.38"> raktajānāṃ pratīkāraṃ kuryāt kuṣṭhacikitsite |
            <caesura/>
             surasādiṃ tu sarveṣu sarvathauvopayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.39"> pravyaktatikatakaṭukaṃ bhojanaṃ ca hitaṃ bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             kulatthakṣārasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ kṣārapānaṃ ca pūjitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.54.40"> kṣīrāṇi māṃsāni ghṛtāni caiva dadhīni śākāni ca parṇavanti |
            <caesura/>
             samāsato 'mlānmadhurān himāṃś ca kṛmīn jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            kṛmipratiṣedho nāma (ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) catuḥpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||54 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="55" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.1"> athāta udāvartapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.3"> adhaś cordhvaṃ ca bhāvānāṃ pravṛttānāṃ svabhāvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             na vegān dhārayet prājño vātādīnāṃ jijīviṣuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.4"> vātaviṇmūtrajṛmbhāśrukṣavodgāravamīndriyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vyāhanyamānair uditair udāvarto nirucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.5"> kṣuttṛṣṇāśvāsanidrāṇām udāvarto vidhāraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             tasyābhidhāsye vyāsena lakṣaṇaṃ ca cikitsitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.6"> trayodaśavidhaś cāsau bhinna etais tu kāraṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apathyabhojanāc cāpi vakṣyate ca tathāparaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.7"> ādhmānaśūlau hṛdayoparodhaṃ śirorujaṃ śvāsamatīva hikkām |
            <caesura/>
             kāsapratiśyāyagalagrahāṃś ca balāsapittaprasaraṃ ca ghoram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.8"> kuryād apāno 'bhihataḥ svamārge hanyāt purīṣaṃ mukhataḥ kṣiped vā |
            <caesura/>
             āṭopaśūlau parikartanaṃ ca saṅgaḥ purīṣasya tathordhvavātaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.9"> purīṣamāsyād api vā nireti purīṣavege 'bhihate narasya |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrasya vege 'bhihate naras tu kṛcchreṇa mūtraṃ kurute 'lpam alpam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.10"> meḍhre gude vaṅkṣaṇabastimuṣkanābhipradeśeṣv athavā+api mūrdhni |
            <caesura/>
             ānaddhabastiś ca bhavanti tīvrāḥ śūlāś ca śūlair iva bhinnamūrteḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.11"> manyāgalastambhaśirovikārā jṛmbhopaghātāt pavanātmakāḥ syuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrotrānanaghrāṇavilocanotthā bhavanti tīvrāś ca tathā vikārāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.12"> ānandajaṃ śokasamudbhavaṃ vā netrodakaṃ prāptam amuñcato hi |
            <caesura/>
             śirogurutvaṃ nayanāmayāś ca bhavanti tīvrāḥ saha pīnasena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.13"> bhavanti gāḍhaṃ kṣavathor vighātāc chirokṣināsāśravaṇeṣu rogāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhāsyapūrṇatvam atīva todaḥ kūjaś ca vāyor uta vā pravṛttiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.14"> udgāravege 'bhihate bhavanti ghorā vikārāḥ pavanaprasūtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             charder vighātena bhavec ca kuṣṭhaṃ yenaiva doṣeṇa vidagdham annam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.15"> mūtrāśaye pāyuni muṣkayoś ca śopho rujo mūtravinigrahaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             śukrāśmarī tatsravaṇaṃ bhaved vā te te vikārā vihate tu śukre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.16"> tandrāṅgamardārucivibhramāḥ syuḥ kṣudho 'bhighātāt kṛśatā ca
            dṛṣṭeḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhāsyaśoṣaḥ śravaṇāvarodhastṛṣṇābhighātāddhṛdaye vyathā ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.17"> śrāntasya niḥśvāsavinigraheṇa hṛdrogamohāv athavāpi gulmaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbhāṅgamardo 'ṅgaśirokṣijāḍyaṃ nidrābhighātād athavāpi tandrā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.18"> tṛṣṇārditaṃ parikliṣṭaṃ kṣīṇaṃ śūlair abhidrutam |
            <caesura/>
             śakṛdvamantaṃ matimān udāvartinam utsṛjet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.19"> sarveṣv eteṣu vidhivad udāvarteṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāyoḥ kriyā vidhātavyāḥ svamārgapratipattaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.20"> sāmānyataḥ pṛthaktvena kriyāṃ bhūyo nibodha me |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ mārutaje snigdhasvinne viśiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.21"> purīṣaje tu kartavyo vidhir ānāhiko bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalāḍhyāṃ madirāṃ mūtre tv abhihate pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.22"> elāṃ vāpy atha madyena kṣīraṃ vāpi piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhātrīphalānāṃ svarasaṃ sajalaṃ vā pibet tryaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.23"> rasamaśvapurīṣasya gardabhasyāthavā pibet |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsopadaṃśaṃ madhu vā pibedvā sīdhu gauḍikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.24"> bhadradāru ghanaṃ mūrvā haridrā madhukaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kolapramāṇāni pibedāntarikṣeṇa vāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.25"> duḥsparśāsvarasaṃ vāpi kaṣāyaṃ kuṅkumasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             ervārubījaṃ toyena pibed vā lavaṇīkṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.26"> pañcamūlīśṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ drākṣārasam athāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             yogāṃś ca vitared atra pūrvoktān aśmarībhidaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.27"> mūtrakṛcchrakramaṃ cāpi kuryān niravaśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhūyo vakṣyāmi yogān yān mūtrāghātopaśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.28"> snehaiḥ svedair udāvartaṃ jṛmbhājaṃ samupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             aśrumokṣo 'śruje kāryaḥ snigdhasvinnasya dehinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.29"> tīkṣṇāñjanāvapīḍābhyāṃ tīkṣṇagandhopaśiṅghanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vartiprayogair athavā kṣavasaktiṃ pravartayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.30"> (tīkṣṇaiṣadhapradhamanair athavād ity araśmibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ) udgāraje kramopetaṃ snaihikaṃ dhūmam ācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.31"> surāṃ sauvarcalavatīṃ bījapūrarasānvitām |
            <caesura/>
             chardyāghātaṃ yathādoṣaṃ samyak snehādibhir jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.32"> sakṣāralavaṇopetamabhyaṅgaṃ cātra dāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             bastiśuddhikarāvāpaṃ caturguṇajalaṃ payaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.33"> āvārināśāt kvathitaṃ pītavantaṃ prakāmataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ramayeyuḥ priyā nāryaḥ śukrodāvartinaṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.34"> kṣudvighāte hitaṃ snigdham uṣṇam alpaṃ ca bhojanam |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇāghāte piben manthaṃ yavāgūṃ vāpi śītalām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.35"> bhojyo rasena viśrāntaḥ śramaśvāsāturo naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nidrāghāte pibet kṣīraṃ svapyācceṣṭakathā naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.36"> ādhmānādyeṣu rogeṣu yathāsvaṃ prayateta hi |
            <caesura/>
             yac ca yatra bhavet prāptaṃ tac ca tasmin prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.37"> vāyuḥ koṣṭhānugo rūkṣaiḥ kaṣāyakaṭutiktakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhojanaiḥ kupitaḥ sadya udāvartaṃ karoti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.38"> vātamūtrapurīṣāsṛkkaphamedovahāni vai |
            <caesura/>
             srotāṃsy udāvartayati purīṣaṃ cātivartayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.39"> tato hṛdbastiśūlārto gauravārucipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi kṛcchreṇa kurute naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.40"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyadāhamohavamijvarān |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇāhikkāśirorogamanaḥśravaṇavibhramān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.41"> labhate ca bahūn anyān vikārān vātakopajān |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ tailalavaṇābhyaktaṃ snigdhaṃ svinnaṃ nirūhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.42"> doṣato bhinnavarcaskaṃ bhuktaṃ cāpy anuvāsayet |
            <caesura/>
             na cec chāntiṃ vrajaty evam udāvartaḥ sudāruṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.43"> athainaṃ bahuśaḥ svinnaṃ yuñjyāt snehavirecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayeta trivṛtpīluyavānīramlapācanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.44"> hiṅgukuṣṭhavacāsvarjiviḍaṅgaṃ vā dviruttaram |
            <caesura/>
             yogāv etāv udāvartaṃ śūlaṃ cānilajaṃ hataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.45"> devadārvagnikau kuṣṭhaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ pathyāṃ palaṅkaṣām |
            <caesura/>
             pauṣkarāṇi ca mūlāni toyasyardhāḍhake pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.46"> pādāvaśiṣṭaṃ tat pītam udāvartam apohati |
            <caesura/>
             mūlakaṃ śuṣkam ārdraṃ ca varṣābhūḥ pañcamūlakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.47"> ārevataphalaṃ cāpsu paktvā tena ghṛtaṃ pacet |
            <caesura/>
             tat pīyamānaṃ śāsty ugram udāvartam aśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.48"> vacām ativiṣāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ yavakṣāraṃ harītakīm |
            <caesura/>
             kṛṣṇāṃ nirdahanīṃ cāpi pibed uṣṇena vāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.49"> ikṣvākumūlaṃ madanaṃ viśalyātiviṣe vacām |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaṃ kiṇvāgnikau caiva pibet tulyāni pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.50"> mūtreṇa devadārvagnitriphalābṛhatīḥ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             yavaprasthaṃ phalaiḥ sārdhaṃ kaṇṭakāryā jalāḍhake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.51"> paktvārdhaprasthaśeṣaṃ tu pibed dhiṅgusamanvitam |
            <caesura/>
             madanālābubījāni pippalīṃ sanidigdhikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.52"> saṃcūrṇya pradhamennāḍyā viśaty etad yathā gudam |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ nikumbhakampillaśyāmekṣvākvagnikodbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.53"> kṛtavedhanamāgadhyor lavaṇānāṃ ca sādhayet |
            <caesura/>
             gavāṃ mūtreṇa tā vartīḥ kārayet tu gudānugāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sadyaḥ śarmakarāv etau yogāv amṛtasaṃmatau ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            udāvartapratiṣedho nāma (saptadaśo+ādhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||55
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="56" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṭpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.1"> athāto visūcikāpratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.3"> ajīrṇam āmaṃ viṣṭabdhaṃ vidagdhaṃ ca yad īritam |
            <caesura/>
             visūcyalasakau tasmād bhavec cāpi vilambikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.4"> sūcībhir iva gātrāṇi tudan saṃtiṣṭhate 'nilaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yasyājīrṇena sā vaidyair ucyate ti visūcikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.5"> na tāṃ parimitāhārā labhante viditāgamāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūḍhās tām ajitātmāno labhante kaluṣāśayāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.6"> mūrcchātisārau vamathuḥ pipāsā śūlaṃ bhramodveṣṭanajṛmbhadāhāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vaivarṇyakampau hṛdaye rujaś ca bhavanti tasyāṃ śirasaś ca bhedaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.7"> kukṣir ānahyate 'tyarthaṃ pratāmyati vikūjati |
            <caesura/>
             niruddho mārutaś cāpi kukṣau viparidhāvati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.8"> vātavarconirodhaś ca kukṣau yasya bhṛśaṃ bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             tasyālasakam ācaṣṭe tṛṣṇodgārāv arodhakau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.9"> duṣṭaṃ tu bhuktaṃ kaphamārutābhyāṃ pravartate nordhvam adhaś ca
            yasya |
            <caesura/>
             vilambikāṃ tāṃ bhṛśaduścikitsyām ācakṣate śāstravidaḥ purāṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.10"> yatrasthamāmaṃ virujet tam eva deśaṃ viśeṣeṇa vikārajātaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣeṇa yenāvatataṃ svaliṅgais taṃ lakṣayed āmasamudbhavaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.11"> yaḥ śyāvadantauṣṭhanakho 'lpasaṃjñaś chardyardito
            'bhyantarayātanetraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣāmasvaraḥ sarvavimuktasandhir yāyān naraḥ so 'punar āgamāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.12"> sādhyāsu pārṣṇyor dahanaṃ praśastam agnipratāpo vamanaṃ ca tīkṣṇam
            |
            <caesura/>
             pakve tato 'nne tu vilaṅghanaṃ syāt saṃpācanaṃ cāpi virecanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.13"> viśuddhadehasya hi sadya eva mūrcchātisārādir upaiti śāntim |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ cāpi vadanti pathyaṃ sarvāsu yogānaparān nibodha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.14"> pathyāvacāhiṅgukaliṅgagṛñjasauvarcalaiḥ sātiviṣaiś ca cūrṇam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhāmbupītaṃ vinihantyajīrṇaṃ śūlaṃ visūcīmaruciṃ ca sadyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.15"> kṣārāgadaṃ vā lavaṇaṃ viṣaṃ vā guḍapragāḍhān atha sarṣapān vā |
            <caesura/>
             amlena vā saindhavahiṅguyuktau sabījapūrṇau saghṛtau trivargau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.16"> kaṭutrikaṃ vā lavaṇair upetaṃ pibet snuhīkṣīravimiśritaṃ tu |
            <caesura/>
             kalyāṇakaṃ vā lavaṇaṃ pibet tu yad uktam ādāv anilāmayeṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.17"> kṛṣṇājamodakṣavakāṇi vāpi tulyau pibed vā magadhānikumbhau |
            <caesura/>
             dantīyuta vā magadhodbhavānāṃ kalkaṃ pibet koṣavatīrasena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.18"> uṣṇābhir adbhir magadhodbhavānāṃ kalkaṃ piben nāgarakalkayuktam |
            <caesura/>
             vyoṣaṃ karañjasya phalaṃ haridre mūlaṃ samaṃ cāpy atha mātuluṅgyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.19"> chāyāviśuṣkā guṭikāḥ kṛtās tā hanyur visūcīṃ nayanāñjanena |
            <caesura/>
             suvāmitaṃ sādhuvirecitaṃ vā sulaṅghataṃ vā manujaṃ viditvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.20"> peyādibhir dīpanapācanīyaiḥ samyakkṣudhārtaṃ samupakrameta |
            <caesura/>
             āmaṃ śakṛd vā nicitaṃ krameṇa bhūyo vibaddhaṃ viguṇānilena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.21"> pravartamānaṃ na yathāsvamenaṃ vikāram ānāham udāharanti ||
            <caesura/>
             tasmin bhavantyāmasamudbhave tu tṛṣṇāpratiśyāyaśirovidāhāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.22"> āmāśaye śūlam atho gurutvaṃ hṛllāsa udgāravighātanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             stambhaḥ kaṭīpṛṣṭhapurīṣamūtre śūlo 'tha mūrcchā sa śakṛd vamec ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.23"> śvāsaś ca pakvāśayaje bhavanti liṅgāni cātrālasakodbhavāni |
            <caesura/>
             āmodbhave vāntam upakrameta saṃsargabhaktakramadīpanīyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.24"> athetaraṃ yo na śakṛd vamet tam āmaṃ jayet svedanapācanaiś ca |
            <caesura/>
             visūcikāyāṃ parikīrtitāni dravyāṇi vairecanikāni yāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.25"> tānyeva vartīr viraced vicūrṇya mahiṣyajāvībhagavāṃ tu mūtraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svinnasya pāyau viniveśya tāś ca cūrṇāni caiṣāṃ pradhamet tu nāḍyā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.26"> mūtreṣu saṃsādhya yathāvidhānaṃ dravyāṇi yāny ūrdhvam adhaś ca
            yānti |
            <caesura/>
             kvāthena tenāśu nirūhayec ca mūtrārdhayuktena samākṣikeṇa || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.27"> tribhaṇḍiyuktaṃ lavaṇaprakuñcaṃ dattvā viriktakramam ācarec ca |
            <caesura/>
             eṣv eva tailena ca sādhitena prāptaṃ yadi syād anuvāsayec ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre kāyacikitsātantre visūcikāpratiṣedho
            nāma (aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ṣaṭpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||56 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="57" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.1"> athāto 'rocakapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.3"> doṣaiḥ pṛthak saha ca cittaviparyayāc ca bhaktāyaneṣu hṛdi cāvatate
            pragāḍham |
            <caesura/>
             nānne rucir bhavati taṃ bhiṣajo vikāraṃ bhaktopaghātam iha pañcavidhaṃ vadanti || | </l>
          <l/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.4"> hṛcchūlapīḍanayutaṃ virasānanatvaṃ vātātmake bhavati liṅgamarocake
            tu |
            <caesura/>
             hṛddāhacoṣabahutā mukhatiktatā ca mūrcchā satṛḍ bhavati pittakṛte tathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.5"> kaṇḍūgutvakaphasaṃsravasādatandrāḥ śleṣmātmake madhuramāsyamarocake
            tu |
            <caesura/>
             sarvātmake pavanapittakaphā bahūni rūpāṇyathāsya hṛdaye samudīrayanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.6"> saṃrāgaśokabhayaviplutacetasas tu cintākṛto bhavati so
            'śucidarśanāc ca |
            <caesura/>
             vāte vacāmbuvamanaṃ kṛtavān pibec ca snehaiḥ surābhir athavoṣṇajalena cūrṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.7"> kṛṣṇāviḍaṅgayavabhasmahareṇubhārgīrāsnailahiṅgulavaṇottamanāgarāṇām
            |
            <caesura/>
             pitte guḍāmbumadhurair vamanaṃ praśastaṃ snehaḥ sasaindhavasitāmadhusarpiriṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.8"> nimbāmbuvāmitavataḥ kaphaje 'nupānaṃ rājadrumāmbu madhunā tu
            sadīpyakaṃ syāt |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ yad uktam athavānilaje tad eva sarvaiś ca sarvakṛtam evam upakrameta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.9">
            drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāmalakendravṛkṣaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bījaiḥ karañjanṛpavṛkṣabhavaiś ca piṣṭair lehaṃ pacet surabhimūtrayutaṃ yathāvat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.10"> mustāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ rajanīdvayaṃ ca bhārgīṃ ca kuṣṭhamatha
            nirdahanīṃ ca piṣṭvā |
            <caesura/>
             mūtre 'vije dviradamūtrayute paced vā pāṭhāṃ tugāmativiṣāṃ rajanīṃ ca mukhyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.11"> maṇḍūkimarkamamṛtāṃ ca salāṅgalākhyāṃ mūtre pacet tu mahiṣasya
            vidhānavidvā |
            <caesura/>
             etān na santi caturo lihatas tu lehān gulmāruciśvasanakaṇṭhahṛdāmayāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.12"> sātmyān svadeśaracitān vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyān pānāni
            mūlaphalaṣāḍavarāgayogān |
            <caesura/>
             adyādrasāṃś ca vividhān vividhaiḥ prakārair bhuñjīta cāpi laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.13"> āsthāpanaṃ vidhivadatra virecanaṃ ca kuryān mṛdūni śirasaś ca
            virecanāni |
            <caesura/>
             trīṇy ūṣaṇāni rajanītriphalāyutāni cūrṇīkṛtāni yavaśūkavimiśritāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.14"> kṣaudrāyutāni vitaren mukhabodhanārtham anyāni tiktakaṭukāni ca
            bheṣajāni |
            <caesura/>
             mustādirājataruvargadaśāṅgasiddhaiḥ kvāthair jayen madhuyutair vividhaiś ca lehaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15"> mūtrāsavairguḍakṛtaiś ca tathā tvariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca
            madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             syādeṣa eva kaphavātahate vidhiś ca śāntiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16"> icchābhighātabhayaśokahate 'ntaragnau bhāvān bhavāya vitaret khalu
            śakyarūpān |
            <caesura/>
             artheṣu cāpy apaciteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaiḥ śrutiśatairanumānayettam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.17"> dainyaṃ gate manasi bodhanamatra śastaṃ yadyat priyaṃ
            tadupasevyamarocake tu ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            'rocakapratiṣedho nāma (ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||57
            ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="58" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭāpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.1"> athāto mūtrāghātapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.i"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.ii"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.3"> vātakuṇḍalikāṣṭhīlā vātabastis tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrātītaḥ sajaṭharo mūtrotsaṅgaḥ kṣayas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.4"> mūtragranthir mūtraśukramuṣṇavātas tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mūtraukasādau dvau cāpi rogā dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.5"> raukṣyād vegavighātād vā vāyur antaram āśirtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtraṃ carati saṃgṛhya viguṇaḥ kuṇḍalīkṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.6"> sṛjed alpālpamathavā sarujaskaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātakuṇḍalikāṃ taṃ tu vyādhiṃ vidyāt sudāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.7"> śakṛnmārgasya basteś ca cāyur antaram āśritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aṣṭhīlāvadghanaṃ granthiṃ karoty acalam unnatam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.8"> viṇmūtranilasaṅgaś ca tatrādhmānaṃ ca jāyate |
            <caesura/>
             vedanā ca parā bastau vātāṣṭhīleti tāṃ viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.9"> vegaṃ vidhārayed yas tu mūtrasyākuśalo naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             niruṇaddhi mukhaṃ tasya baster bastigato 'nilaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.10"> mūtrasaṅgo bhavet tena bastikukṣinipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātabastiḥ sa vijñeyo vyādhiḥ kṛcchraprasādhanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.11"> vegaṃ sandhārya mūtrasya yo bhūyaḥ sraṣṭum icchati |
            <caesura/>
             tasya nābhyeti yadi vā kathañ cit saṃpravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.12"> pravāhato mandarujam alpam alpaṃ punaḥ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrātītaṃ tu taṃ vidyān mūtravegavighātajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.13"> mūtrasya vihate vege tadudāvartahetunā |
            <caesura/>
             apānaḥ kupito vāyur udaraṃ pūrayed bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.14"> nābher adhastād ādhmānaṃ janayet tīvravedanam |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ mūtrajaṭharaṃ vidyād adhaḥsrotonirodhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.15"> bastau vāpy athavā nāle maṇau vā yasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtraṃ pravṛttaṃ sajjeta saraktaṃ vā pravāhataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.16"> sravec chanair alpam alpaṃ sarujaṃ vātha nīrujam |
            <caesura/>
             viguṇānilajo vyādhiḥ sa mūtrotsaṅgasaṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.17"> rūkṣasya klāntadehasya bastisthau pittamārutau |
            <caesura/>
             sadāhavedanaṃ kṛcchraṃ kuryāt āṃ mūtrasaṃkṣayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.18"> abhyantare bastimukhe vṛtto 'lpaḥ sthira eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             vedanāvānati sadā mūtramārganirodhanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.19"> jāyate sahasā yasya granthir aśmarilakṣaṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa mūtragranthir ity evam ucyate vedanādibhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.20"> pratyupasthitamūtras tu maithunaṃ yo 'bhinandati |
            <caesura/>
             tasya mūtrayutaṃ retaḥ sahasā saṃpravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.21"> purastād vāpi mūtrasya paścād vāpi kadācana |
            <caesura/>
             bhasmodakapratīkāśaṃ mūtraśukraṃ tad ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.22"> vyāyāmādhvātapaiḥ pittaṃ bastiṃ prāpyānilāvṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             bastiṃ meḍhraṃ gudaṃ caiva pradahan srāvayed adhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.23"> mūtraṃ hāridramathavā saraktaṃ raktam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             kṛcchrāt pravartate jantor uṣṇavātaṃ vadanti tam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.24"> viśadaṃ pītakaṃ mūtraṃ sadāhaṃ bahalaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śuṣkaṃ bhavati yac cāpi rocanācūrṇasannibham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.25"> mūtraukasādaṃ taṃ vidyād rogaṃ pittakṛtaṃ budhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             picchilaṃ saṃhataṃ śvetaṃ tathā kṛcchrapravartanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.26"> śuṣkaṃ bhavati yaccāpi śaṅkhacūrṇaprapāṇḍuram |
            <caesura/>
             mūtraukasāhaṃ taṃ vidyād āmayaṃ dvādaśaṃ kaphāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.27"> kaṣāyakalkasarpiṃṣi bhakṣyān lehān payāṃsi ca |
            <caesura/>
             kṣāramadyāsavasvedān(kṣāramadhvāsavasvedān) bastīṃś cottarasaṃjñitān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.28"> vidadhyān matimāṃs tatra vidhiṃ cāśmarināśanam |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrodāvartayogāṃś ca kārtsnyenātra prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.29"> kalkam ervārubījānām akṣamātraṃ sasaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             dhānyāmlayuktaṃ pītvaiva mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.30"> surāṃ sauvarcalavatīṃ mūtrakṛcchrī piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhu māṃsopadaṃśaṃ vā pibed vāpy atha gauḍikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.31"> pibet kuṅkumakarṣaṃ vā madhūdakasamāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             rātriparyuṣitaṃ prātas tathā sukhamavāpnuyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.32"> dāḍimāmlāṃ yutāṃ mukhyām elājīrakanāgaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.33"> pṛthakparṇyādivargasya mūlaṃ gokṣurakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             ardhaprasthena toyasya pacet kṣīracaturguṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.34"> kṣīrāvaśiṣṭaṃ tacchītaṃ sitākṣaudrayutaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             naro mārutapittotthamūtraghātanivāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.35"> niṣpīḍya vāsasā samyag varco rāsabhavājinoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rasasya kuḍavaṃ tasya piben mūtrarujāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.36"> mustābhayādevadārumūrvāṇāṃ madhukasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ mūtradoṣanivāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.37"> abhayāmalakākṣāṇāṃ kalkaṃ badarasaṃmitam |
            <caesura/>
             ambhasālavaṇopetaṃ piben mūtrarujāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.38"> udumbarasamaṃ kalkaṃ drākṣāyā jalasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             pibet paryuṣitaṃ rātrau śītaṃ mūtrarujāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.39"> nidigdhikāyāḥ svarasaṃ pibet kuḍavasaṃmitam |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaharaṃ kalyam athavā kṣaudrasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.40"> prapīḍyāmalakānāṃ tu rasaṃ kuḍavasaṃmitam |
            <caesura/>
             pītvāgadī bhavej jantur mūtradoṣarujāturaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.41"> dhātrīphalarasenaivaṃ sūkṣmailāṃ vā piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             piṣṭvāthavā suśītena śālitaṇḍulavāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.42"> tālasya taruṇaṃ mūlaṃ trapusasya rasaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śvetaṃ karkaṭakaṃ caiva prātas tu payasā pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.43"> śṛtaṃ vā madhuraiḥ kṣīraṃ sarpirmiśraṃ piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaviśuddhyarthaṃ tathaivāśmarināśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.44"> balāśvadaṃṣṭrākrauñcāsthikokilākṣakataṇḍulān |
            <caesura/>
             śataparvakamūlaṃ ca devadāru sacitrakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.45"> akṣabījaṃ ca surayā kalkīkṛtya piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaviśuddhyarthaṃ tathaivāśmarināśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.46"> pāṭalākṣāram āhṛtya saptakṛtvaḥ parisrutam |
            <caesura/>
             piben mūtravikāraghnaṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tailamātrayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.47"> nalāśmabhedadarbhekṣutrapusair vārubījakān |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīre pariśṛtān tatra pibet sarpiḥ samāyutān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.48"> pāṭalyā yāvaśūkāc ca pāribhadrāt tilād api |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārodakena matimān tvageloṣaṇacūrṇakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.49"> pibed guḍena miśraṃ vā lihyāllehān pṛthak pṛthak |
            <caesura/>
             ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi mūtradoṣe kramaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.50"> snehasvedopapannānāṃ hitaṃ teṣu virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ saṃśuddhadehānāṃ hitāś cottarabastayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.51"> strīṇāmatiprasaṅgena śoṇitaṃ yasya dṛśyate |
            <caesura/>
             maithunoparamas tasya bṛṃhaṇaś ca vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.52"> tāmracūḍavasā tailaṃ hitaṃ cottarabastiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             vidhānaṃ tasya pūrvaṃ hi vyāsataḥ parikīrtitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.53"> kṣaudrārdhapātraṃ dattvā ca pātraṃ tu kṣīrasarpiṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāyāś ca cūrṇaṃ ca drākṣācūrṇaṃ ca tatsamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.54"> svayaṅguptāphalaṃ caiva tathivekṣurakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīcūrṇasaṃyuktamardhabhāgaṃ prakalpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.55"> tadaikadhyaṃ samānīya khajenābhipramanthayet |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ pāṇitalaṃ cūrṇaṃ līḍhvā kṣīraṃ tataḥ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.56"> etat sarpiḥ prayuñjānaḥ śuddhadeho naraḥ sadā |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣāñjayet sarvānanyayogaiḥ sudurjayān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.57"> jayec choṇitadoṣāṃś ca vandhyā garbhaṃ labheta ca |
            <caesura/>
             nārī caitat prayuñjānā yonidosāt pramucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.58"> balā kolāsthi madhukaṃ śvadaṃṣṭrātha śatāvarī |
            <caesura/>
             mṛṇālaṃ ca kaśeruś ca bījānīkṣurakasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.59"> sahasravīryāṃśumatī payasyā saha kālayā |
            <caesura/>
             śṛgālavinnātibalā bṛṃhaṇīyo gaṇas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.60"> etāni samabhāgāni matimān saha sādhayet |
            <caesura/>
             caturguṇena payasā guḍasya tulayā saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.61"> droṇāvaśiṣṭaṃ tat pūtaṃ pacettena ghṛtāḍhakam |
            <caesura/>
             tat siddhaṃ kalaśe sthāpyaṃ kṣaudraprasthena saṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.62"> sarpiretat prayuñjāno mūtradoṣāt pramucyate |
            <caesura/>
             tugākṣīryāś ca cūrṇāni śarkarāyās tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.63"> kṣaudreṇa tulyānyāloḍya praśaste 'hani lehayet |
            <caesura/>
             tasya khādedyathāśakti mātrāṃ kṣīraṃ tataḥ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.64"> śukradoṣāñjayenmartyaḥ prāśya samyak suyantritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vyavāyakṣīṇaretās tu sadyaḥ saṃlabhate sukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.65"> ojasvī balavānmartyaḥ piben neva ca hṛṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             citrakaḥ sārivā caiva balā kālānusārivā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.66"> drākṣā viśālā pippalyas tathā citraphalā bhevet |
            <caesura/>
             tathaiva madhukaṃ pathyāṃ dadyādāmalakāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.67"> ghṛtāḍhakaṃ pacedebhiḥ kalkaiḥ karṣasamanvitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīradroṇe jaladroṇe tat siddham avatārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.68"> śītaṃ parisrutaṃ caiva śarkarāprasthasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             tugākṣīryāś ca tat sarvaṃ matimān parimiśrayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.69"> tato mitaṃ pibetkāle yathādoṣaṃ yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             vātaretāḥ śleṣmaretāḥ pittaretās tu yo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.70"> raktaretā granthiretāḥ pibed icchan naro gatām |
            <caesura/>
             jīvanīyaṃ ca vṛṣyaṃ ca sarpir etad balāvaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.71"> prakṣāhitaṃ ca dhanyaṃ ca sarvarogāpahaṃ śivam |
            <caesura/>
             sarpir etat prayuñjānā strī garbhaṃ labhate 'cirāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.72"> asṛgdoṣāñ jayec cāpi yonidoṣāṃś ca saṃhatān |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣeṣu sarveṣu kuryād etac cikitsitam ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            mūtrāghātapratiṣedho nāma (viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) aṣṭapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||58 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="59" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ūnaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1"> athāto mūtrakṛcchrapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.3"> vātena pittena kaphena sarvais tathā+ābhighātaiḥ śakṛdaśmarībhyām |
            <caesura/>
             tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ kathito 'ṣṭamas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.4"> alpam alpaṃ samutpīḍya muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             phaladbhir iva kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5"> hāridramuṣṇaṃ raktaṃ vā muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             agninā dahyamānābhaiḥ pittāghātena mehati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.6"> snigdhaṃ śuklamanuṣṇaṃ ca muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.7"> dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇaṃ muhur muhuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāmyamānas tu kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.8"> mūtravāhiṣu śalyena kṣateṣv abhihateṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu mūtrāghātas tu jāyate bhṛśavedanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.9"> vātabastes tu tulyāni tasya liṅgāni lakṣayet |
            <caesura/>
             śakṛtas tu pratīghātād vāyur viguṇatāṃ gataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.10"> ādhmānaṃ ca saśūlaṃ ca mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti hi |
            <caesura/>
             aśmarīhetukaḥ pūrvaṃ mūtraghāta udāhṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.11"> aśmarī śarkarā caiva tulye saṃbhavalakṣaṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāyā viśeṣaṃ tu śṛṇu kīrtayato mama || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.12"> pacyamānasya pittena bhidyamānasya vāyunā |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmaṇo 'vayavā bhinnāḥ śarkarā iti saṃjñitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13"> hṛtpīḍā vepathuḥ śūlaṃ kukṣau vahniḥ sudurbalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tābhir bhavati mūrcchā ca mūtrāghātaś ca dāruṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.14"> mūtraveganirastāsu tāsu śāmyati vedanā |
            <caesura/>
             yāvadanyā punarnaiti guḍikā srotaso mukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.15"> śarkarāsaṃbhavasyaitanmūtrāghātasya lakṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             cikitsitamathaiteṣāmaṣṭānām api vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.16"> aśmarīṃ ca samāśritya yad uktaṃ prasamīkṣya tat |
            <caesura/>
             yathādoṣaṃ prayuñjīta snehādim api ca kramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.17"> śvadaṃṣṭrāśmabhidau kumbhīṃ hapuṣāṃ kaṇṭakārikām |
            <caesura/>
             balāṃ śatāvarīṃ rāsnāṃ varuṇaṃ girikarṇikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.18"> tathā vidārigandhādiṃ saṃhṛtya traivṛtaṃ pacet |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tat peyaṃ tena vāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.19"> dadyād uttarabastiṃ ca vātakṛcchropaśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             śvadaṃṣṭrāsvarase tailaṃ saguḍakṣīranāgaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.20"> paktvā tat pūrvavadyojyaṃ tatrānilarujāpaham |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṇotpalādikākolīnyagrodhādigaṇaiḥ kṛtam(śṛtam) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.21"> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ nāśayet kṣīram eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca pittakṛcchropaśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.22"> ebhir eva kṛtaḥ snehastrividheṣv api bastiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasair yutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.23"> surasoṣakamustādau varuṇādau ca yat kṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ tathā yavāgvādi kaphāghāte praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.24"> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryād etān eva ca sarvaje |
            <caesura/>
             phalguvṛś cīradarbhāśmasāracūrṇaṃ ca vāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.25"> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ kṛcchrarujāpaham |
            <caesura/>
             tathābhighātaje kuryāt sadyovraṇacikitsitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.26"> mūtrakṛcchre śakṛjjāte kāryā vātaharī kriyā |
            <caesura/>
             svedāvagāhāvabhyaṅgabasticūrṇakriyās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.27"> ye tvanye tu tathā kṛcchre tayoḥ proktaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            mūtrakṛcchrapratiṣedho nāma (ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekonaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
            ||59 ||</p>
