        <div n="60" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.1"> athāto 'mānuṣopasargapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.3"> niśācarebhyo rakṣyas tu nityam eva kṣatāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             iti yat prāgabhihitaṃ vistaras tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.4"> guhyānāgatavijñānamanavasthāsahiṣṇutā |
            <caesura/>
             kriyā vāmānuṣī yasmin sagrahaḥ parikīrtyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.5"> aśuciṃ bhinnamaryādaṃ kṣataṃ vā yadi vākṣatam |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsyurhiṃsāvihārārthaṃ satkārārtham athāpi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.6"> asaṅkhyeyā grahagaṇā grahādhipatayas tu ye |
            <caesura/>
             vyajyante vividhākārā bhidyante te tathāṣṭadhā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.7"> devās tathā śatrugaṇāś ca teṣāṃ gandharvayakṣāḥ pitaro bhujaṅgāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣāṃsi yā cāpi piśācajātireṣo 'ṣṭako devagaṇo grahākhyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.8"> saṃtuṣṭaḥ śucir api ceṣṭagandhamālyo nistandrī hy
            avitathasaṃskṛtaprabhāṣī |
            <caesura/>
             tejasvī sthiranayano varapradātā brahmaṇyo bhavati naraḥ sa devajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.9"> saṃsvedī dvijagurudevadoṣavaktā jihmākṣo vigatabhayo vimārgadṛṣṭiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             santuṣṭo bhavati na cānnapānajātairduṣṭātmā bhavati ca devaśatrujuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.10"> hṛṣṭātmā pulinavanāntaropasevī svācāraḥ priyaparigītagandhamālyaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             nṛtyan vai prahasati cāru cālpaśabdaṃ gandharvagrahaparipīḍito manuṣyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.11"> tāmrākṣaḥ priyatanuraktavastradhārī gambhīro drutamatiralpavāk
            sahiṣśuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tejasvī vadati ca kiṃ dadāmi kasmai yo yakṣagrahaparipīḍito manuṣyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.12"> pretebhyo visṛjati saṃstareṣu piṇḍān śāntātmā jalam api
            cāpasavyavastraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsepsustilaguḍapāyasābhikāmastadbhukto bhavati pitṛgrahābhibhūtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.13"> bhūmau yaḥ prasarati sarpavat kadācit sṛkkiṇyau vilikhati jihvayā
            tathaiva |
            <caesura/>
             nidrālurguḍamadhudugdhapāyasepsurvijñeyo bhavati bhujaṅgamena juṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.14"> māṃsāsṛgvividhasurāvikāralipsurnirlajjo bhṛśamatiniṣṭhuro 'tiśūraḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             krodhālurvipulabalo niśāvihārī śaucadviḍ bhavati ca rakṣasā gṛhītaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.15"> uddhastaḥ kṛśaparuṣaś cirapralāpī durgandho
            bhṛśamaśucistathātilolaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bahvāśī vijanahimāmburātrisevī vyāvigno bhramati rudan piśācajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.16"> sthūlākṣastvaritagatiḥ svaphenalehī nidrāluḥ patati ca kampate ca
            yo 'ti |
            <caesura/>
             yaś cādridviradanagādivicyutaḥ san saṃsṛṣṭo na bhavati vārdhakena juṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.17ab"> devagrahāḥ paurṇamāsyāmasurāḥ sandhyayor api |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.17cd"> gandharvāḥ prāyaśo 'ṣṭamyāṃ yakṣāś ca pratipadyatha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.18"> kṛṣṇakṣaye ca pitaraḥ paś camyām api coragāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣāṃsi niśi paiśācāś caturdaśyāṃ viśanti ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.19"> darpaṇādīn yathā chāyā śītoṣṇaṃ prāṇino yathā |
            <caesura/>
             svamaṇiṃ bhāskarasyosrā yathā dehaṃ ca dehadhṛk |
            <caesura/>
             viśanti ca na dṛśyante grahāstadvaccharīriṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.20"> tapāṃsi tīvrāṇi tathaiva dānaṃ vratāni dharmo niyamāś ca satyam |
            <caesura/>
             guṇāstathāṣṭāvapi teṣu nityā vyastāḥ samastāś ca yathāprabhāvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.21"> na te manuṣyaiḥ saha saṃviśanti na vā manuṣyān kvacidāviśanti |
            <caesura/>
             ye tv āviśantīti vadanti mohāt te bhūtavidyāviṣayād apohyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.22"> teṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ paricārakā ye koṭīsahasrāyutapadmasaṃkhyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asṛgvasāmāṃsabhujaḥ subhīmā niśāvihārāś ca tamāviśanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.23"> niśācarāṇāṃ teṣāṃ hi ye devagaṇamāśritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             te tu tat sattvasaṃsargād vijñeyās tu tadañjanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.24"> devagrahā iti punaḥ procyante 'śucayaś ca ye |
            <caesura/>
             devavac ca namasyante pratyarthyante ca devavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.25"> svāmiśīlakriyācārāḥ krama eṣa surādiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             nirṛteryā duhitarastāsāṃ sa prasavaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.26"> satyatvād apavṛtteṣu vṛttis teṣāṃ gaṇaiḥ kṛtā |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsāvihārā ye keciddevabhāvabhupāśritāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.27"> bhūtānīti kṛtā saṃjñā teṣāṃ saṃjñāpravaktṛbhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             grahasaṃjñāni bhūtāni yasmādvettyanayā bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.28"> vidyayā bhūtavidyātvamata eva nirucyate |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāṃ śāntyarthamanvicchan vaidyas tu susamāhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.29"> japaiḥ saniyamair homair ārabheta cikitsitum |
            <caesura/>
             raktāni gandhamālyāni bījāni madhusarpiṣī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.30"> bhakṣyāś ca sarve sarveṣāṃ sāmānyo vidhir ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             vastrāṇi gandhamālyāni māṃsāni rudhirāṇi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.31"> yāni yeṣāṃ yatheṣṭāni tāni tebhyaḥ pradāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsanti manujān yeṣu prāyaśo divaseṣu tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.32ab"> dineṣu teṣu deyāni tadbhūtavinivṛttaye |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.32cd"> devagrahe devagṛhe hutvāgniṃ prāpayed (dāpayed )balim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.33"> kuśasvastikapūpājyacchatrapāyasasaṃbhṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             asurāya yathākālaṃ vidadhyāc catvarādiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.34"> gandharvasya gavāṃ madhye madyamāṃsāmbujāṅgalam |
            <caesura/>
             hṛdye veśmani yakṣasya kulmāṣāsṛksurādibhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.35"> atimuktakakundābjaiḥ puṣpaiś ca vitaredbalim |
            <caesura/>
             nadyāṃ pitṛgrahāyeṣṭaṃ kuśāstaraṇabhūṣitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.36"> tatraivopaharec cāpi nāgāya vividhaṃ balim |
            <caesura/>
             catuṣpathe rākṣasasya bhīmeṣu gahaneṣu vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.37ab"> śūnyāgāre piśācasya tīvraṃ balimupāharet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.37cd"> pūrvamācaritairmantrairbhūtavidyānidarśitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.38"> na śakyā balibhir jetuṃ yogaistān samupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             ajarkṣacarmaromāṇi śalyakolūkayos tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.39"> hiṅguṃ mūtraṃ ca bastasya dhūmamasya prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             etena śāmyati kṣipraṃ balavānapi yo grahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.40"> gajāhvapippalīmūlavyoṣāmalakasarṣapān |
            <caesura/>
             godhānakulamārjāraṛṣyapittaprapeṣitān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.41ab"> nasyābhyañjanasekeṣu vidadhyādyogatattvavit | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.41a"/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.41b"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.41cd"> svarāśvāśvatarolūkakarabhaśvaśṛgālajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.42"> purīṣaṃ gṛdhrakākānāṃ varāhasya ca peṣayet |
            <caesura/>
             bastamūtreṇa tatsiddhaṃ tailaṃ syāt pūrvavaddhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.43"> śirīṣabījaṃ laśunaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ siddhārthakaṃ vacām |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhāṃ rajanīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ bastamūtreṇa peṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.44"> vartyaś chāyāviśuṣkāstāḥ sapittā nayanāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             naktamālaphalaṃ vyoṣaṃ mūlaṃ śyonākabilvayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.45"> haridre ca kṛtā vartyaḥ pūrvavannayanāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             saindhavaṃ kaṭukāṃ hiṅguṃ vayaḥsthāṃ ca vacām api |
            <caesura/>
             bastamūtreṇa saṃpiṣṭaṃ matsyapittena pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.46ab"> ye ye grahā na sidhyanti sarveṣāṃ nayanāñjanam |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.46cd"> pūrāṇasarpirlaśunaṃ hiṅgu siddhārthakaṃ vacā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.47"> golomī cājalomī ca bhūtakeśī jaṭā tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kukkuṭā sarpagandhā ca tathā kāṇavikāṇike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.48"> vajraproktā vayaḥsthā ca śṛṅgī mohanavallikā |
            <caesura/>
             arkamūlaṃ trikaṭukaṃ latā srotojam añjanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.49"> naipālī haritālaṃ ca rakṣoghnā ye ca kīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             siṃhavyāghrarkṣamārjāradvīpivājigavāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.50"> śvāvicchalyakagodhānāmuṣṭrasya nakulasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             viṭtvagromavasāmūtraraktapittanakhādayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.51"> asmin varge bhiṣak kuryāt tailāni ca ghṛtāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             pānābhyañjananasyeṣu tāni yojyāni jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.52"> avapīḍe 'ñjane caiva vidadhyād guṭikīkṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             vidadhīta parīṣeke kvathitaṃ cūrṇitaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.53"> uddhūlane ślakṣṇapiṣṭaṃ pradehe cāvacārayet |
            <caesura/>
             eṣa sarvavikārāṃs tu mānasānaparājitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.54"> hanyādalpena kālena snehādirapi ca kramaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             na cācaukṣaṃ prayuñjīta prayogaṃ devatāgrahe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.55"> ṛte piśācādanyatra pratikūlaṃ na cācaret |
            <caesura/>
             vaidyāturau nihanyuste dhruvaṃ kruddhā majaujasaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.56ab"> hitāhitīye yac coktaṃ nityam eva samācaret |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.56cd"> tataḥ prāpsyati siddhiṃ ca yaśaś ca vipulaṃ bhiṣak ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate nāma (prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ,
            āditaḥ) ṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||60 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="61" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.1"> athāto 'pasmārapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.3ab"> smṛtir bhūtārthavijñānam apaś ca parivarjane |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.3cd"> apasmāra iti proktas tato 'yaṃ vyādhir antakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.4"> mithyātiyogendriyārthakarmaṇāmabhis evanāt |
            <caesura/>
             viruddhamalināhāravihārakupitairmalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.5"> veganigrahaśīlānāmahitāśucibhojinām |
            <caesura/>
             rajastamobhibhūtānāṃ gacchatāṃ ca rajasvalām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.6"> tathā kāmabhayodvegakrodhaśokādibhir bhṛśam |
            <caesura/>
             cetasy abhihate puṃsām apasmāro 'bhijāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.6a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.7"> hṛtkampaḥ śūnyatā svedo dhyānaṃ mūrcchā pramūḍhatā |
            <caesura/>
             nidrānāśaś ca tasmiṃs tu bhaviṣyati bhavanty atha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.8ab"> saṃjñāvaheṣu srotaḥsu doṣavyāpteṣu mānavaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.8cd"> rajastamaḥparīteṣu mūḍho bhrāntena cetasā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.9ab"> vikṣipan hastapādaṃ ca vijihmabhrūrvilocanaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.9cd"> dantān khādan vaman phenaṃ vivṛtākṣaḥ patet kṣitau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.10ab"> alpakālānataraṃ cāpi punaḥ saṃjñāṃ labheta saḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.10cd"> so 'pasmāra iti proktaḥ sa ca dṛṣṭaś caturvidhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.11"> vātapittakaphairnṝṇāṃ caturthaḥ sannipātataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vepamāno daśan dantān śvasan phenaṃ vamannapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.12"> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ māmanudhāvati |
            <caesura/>
             tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt so 'pasmāro 'nilātmakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.13ab"> tṛṭtāpasvedamūrcchārto dhunvannaṅgāni vihvalaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.13cd"> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ pītaṃ māmanudhāvati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.14"> tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt sa pittabhava ucyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.14cd"> śītahṛllāsanidrārtaḥ patan bhūmau vaman kapham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.15"> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ śuklaṃ māmanudhāvati |
            <caesura/>
             tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt so 'pasmāraḥ kaphātmakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.16"> hṛdi todastṛḍutkledastriṣvapyeteṣu saṃkhyayā |
            <caesura/>
             pralāpaḥ kūjanaṃ kleśaḥ pratyekaṃ tu bhavediha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.17"> sarvaliṅgasamavāyaḥ sarvadoṣaprakopaje |
            <caesura/>
             animittāgamād vyādher gamanād akṛte 'pi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.18"> āgamāc cāpy apasmāraṃ vadanty anye na doṣajam |
            <caesura/>
             kramopayogād doṣāṇāṃ kṣaṇikatvāt tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.19"> āgamād vaiśvarūpyāc ca sa tu nirvarṇyate budhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             deve varṣaty api yathā bhūmau bījāni kānicit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.20"> śaradi pratirohanti tathā vyādhisamudbhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sthāyinaḥ kecidalpena kālenābhipravardhitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.21"> darśayanti vikārāṃstu viśvarūpānnisargataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apasmāro mahāvyādhistasmād doṣaja eva tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.22"> tasya kāryo vidhiḥ sarvo ya unmādeṣu vakṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             purāṇasarpiṣaḥ pānamabhyaṅgaś caiva pūjitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23ab"> upayogo grahoktānāṃ yogānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23cd"> tataḥ sidhyanti te sarve yogair anyaiś ca sādhayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23ef"> śigrukaṭvaṅgakiṇvāhinimbatvagrasasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.24"> caturguṇe gavāṃ mūtre tailābhyañjane hitam |
            <caesura/>
             godhānakulanāgānāṃ pṛṣatarkṣagavām api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.25"> pitteṣu siddhaṃ tailaṃ ca pānābhyaṅgeṣu pūjitam |
            <caesura/>
             tīkṣṇair ubhayatobhāgaiḥ śiraś cāpi viśodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.26ab"> pūjāṃ rudrasya kurvīta tad gaṇānāṃ ca nityaśaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.26cd"> vātikaṃ bastibhiś cāpi paittikaṃ tu virecanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.27ab"> kaphajaṃ vamanairdhīmānapasmāramupācaret |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.27cd"> kulatthayavakolāni śaṇabījaṃ palaṅkaṣām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.28"> jaṭilāṃ pañcamūlyau dve pathyāṃ cotkvāthya yatnataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bastamūtrayutaṃ sarpiḥ pacettadvātike hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.29"> kākolyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ ca prathame gaṇe |
            <caesura/>
             payomadhusitāyuktaṃ ghṛtaṃ tat paittike hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.30"> kākolyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ ca prathame gaṇe |
            <caesura/>
             payomadhusitāyuktaṃ ghṛtaṃ tat paittike hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.31"> suradrumavacākuṣṭhasiddhārthavyoṣahiṅgubhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhārajanīyugmasamaṅgātriphalāmbudaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.32"> karañjabījaśairīṣagirikarṇīhutāśanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ siddhārthakaṃ nāma sarpirmūtracaturguṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.33"> kṛmikuṣṭhagaraśvāsabalāsaviṣamajvarān |
            <caesura/>
             sarvabhūtagrahonmādānapasmārāṃś ca nāśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.34"> daśamūlendravṛkṣatvaṅmūrvābhārgīphalatrikaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śampākaśreyasīsaptaparṇāpāmārgaphalgubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.35"> śṛtaiḥ kalkaiś ca bhūnimbapūtīkavyoṣacitrakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trivṛtpāṭhāniśāyugmasārivādvayapauṣkaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.36"> kaṭukāyāsadantyugrānīlinīkrimiśatrubhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarpir ebhiś ca gokṣīradadhimūtraśakṛdrasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.37"> sādhitaṃ pañcagavyākhyaṃ sarvāpasmārabhūtanut |
            <caesura/>
             cāturthakakṣayaśvāsānunmādāṃś ca niyacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.38"> bhārgīśṛte pacet kṣīre śālitaṇḍulapāyasam |
            <caesura/>
             tryahaṃ śuddhāya taṃ bhoktuṃ varāhāyopakalpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.39"> jñātvā ca madhurībhūtaṃ taṃ viśasyānnamuddharet |
            <caesura/>
             trīn bhāgāṃs tasya cūrṇasya kiṇvabhāgena saṃsṛjet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.40"> maṇḍodakārthe deyaś ca bhārgīkvāthaḥ suśītalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śuddhe kumbhe nidadhyāc ca saṃbhāraṃ taṃ surāṃ tataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.61.41"> jātagandhāṃ jātarasāṃ pāyayed āturaṃ bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             sirāṃ vidhyed atha prāptāṃ maṅgalyāni ca dhārayet ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti susrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate bhūtavidyātantre
            'pasmārapratiṣedho nāma (dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||61 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="62" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dviṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.1"> athāta unmādapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.3"> madayanty uddhatā (madayanty udgatā) doṣā yasmād unmārgam āśritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mānaso 'yamato vyādhirunmāda iti kīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.4"> ekaikaśaḥ samastaiś ca doṣairatyarthamūrcchitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mānasena ca duḥkhena sa pañcavidha ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.5"> viṣādbhavati ṣaṣṭhaś ca yathāsvaṃ tatra bheṣajam |
            <caesura/>
             sa cāpravṛddhastaruṇo madasaṃjñāṃ bibharti ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.6"> mohodvegau svanaḥ śrotre gātrāṇāmapakarṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             atyutsāho 'ruciś cānne svapne kaluṣabhojanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.7"> vāyunonmathanaṃ cāpi bhramaś cakragatasya vā |
            <caesura/>
             yasya syādacireṇaiva unmādaṃ so 'dhigacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.8ab"> rūkṣacchaviḥ paruṣavāgdhamanītato vā śītāturaḥ kṛśatanuḥ
            sphuritāṅgasandhiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.8cd"> āsphoṭayasyaṭati gāyati nṛtyaśīlo vikrośati bhramati cāpy
            anilaprakopāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.9ab"> tṛṭsvedadāhabahulo bahubhigvinidrāś
            chāyāhimānilajalāntavihārasevī | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.9cd"> tīkṣṇo himāmbuni caye 'pi sa vahniśaṅkī pittāddivā nabhasi
            paśyati tārakāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.10ab"> chardyagnisādasadanārucikāsayukto yoṣid viviktaratir
            alpamatipracāraḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.10cd"> nidrāparo 'lpakathano 'lpabhuguṣṇasevī rātrau bhṛśaṃ bhavati
            cāpi kaphaprakopāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.11"> sarvātmake pavanapittakaphā yathāsvaṃ saṃharṣitā iva ca
            liṅgamudīrayanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.11a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.12"> caurairnarendrapuruṣairaribhis tathānyairvitrāsitasya
            dhanabāndhavasaṃkṣayādvā |
            <caesura/>
             gāḍhaṃ kṣate manasi ca priyayā riraṃsorjāyeta cotkaṭataro manaso vikāraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.13"> citraṃ sa jalpati manonugataṃ visaṃjño gāyatyatho hasati roditi
            mūḍhasaṃjñaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktekṣaṇo hatabalendriyabhāḥ sudīnaḥ śyāvānano viṣakṛto 'tha bhavet parāsuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.14"> snigdhaṃ svinnaṃ tu manujamunmādārtaṃ viśodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tīkṣṇair ubhayatobhāgaiḥ śirasaś ca virecanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.15ab"> vividhair avapīḍaiś ca sarṣapasnehasaṃyutaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.15cd"> yojayitvā tu taccūrṇaṃ ghrāṇe tasya prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.16"> satataṃ dhūpayec cainaṃ śvagomāṃsaiḥ supūtibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarṣapānāṃ ca tailena nasyābhyaṅgau hitau sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.17"> darśayed adbhutānyasya vadennāśaṃ priyasya vā |
            <caesura/>
             bhīmākārairnarairnāgairdāntairvyālaiś ca nirviṣaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.17a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.18ab"> bhīṣayet saṃyataṃ pāśaiḥ kaśābhir vātha tāḍayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.18cd"> yantrayitvā suguptaṃ vā trāsayettaṃ tṛṇāgninā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.18a"/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.18b"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.19ab"> jalena tarjayed vāpi rajjughātair vibhāvayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.19cd"> balavāṃś cāpi saṃrakṣet jale 'ntaḥ parivāsayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.19ef"> pratuded ārayā cainaṃ marmāghātaṃ vivarjayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.19gh"> veśmano 'ntaḥ praviśyainaṃ rakṣaṃs tad veśma dīpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.20"> sāpidhāne jaratkūpe satataṃ vā nivāsayet |
            <caesura/>
             tryahāt tryahād yavāgūś ca tarpaṇān vā pradāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.21ab"> kevalān ambuyuktān vā kulmāṣān vā bahuśrutaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.21cd"> hṛdyaṃ yad dīpanīyaṃ ca tat pathyaṃ tasya bhojayet (yojayet) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.22"> (viḍaṅgatriphalāmustamañjiṣṭhādāḍimotpalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.23"> barhiṣṭharajanīkuṣṭhaparṇinīsārivādvayaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hareṇukātrivṛddantīvacātālīsakeśaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.24"> dvikṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ sarpirmālatīkusumaiḥ saha |
            <caesura/>
             gulmakāsajvaraśvāsakṣayonmādanivāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.25"> etad eva hi saṃpakvaṃ jīvanīyopasaṃbhṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             caturguṇena dugdhena mahākalyāṇam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.26"> apasmāraṃ grahaṃ śoṣaṃ klaibyaṃ kārśyam abījatām |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtam etan nihanty āśu ye cādau gaditā gadāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.27"> barhiṣṭhakuṣṭhamañjiṣṭhākaṭukailāniśāhvayaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tagaratriphalāhiṅguvājigandhāmaradrumaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.28"> vacājamodākākolīmedāmadhukapadmakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkaraṃ hitaṃ sarpiḥ pakvaṃ kṣīracaturguṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.29"> bālānāṃ grahajuṣṭānāṃ puṃsāṃ duṣṭālparetasām |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.30"> brahmīmaindrīṃ viḍaṅgāni vyoṣaṃ hiṅgu surāṃ jaṭhām |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.31"> jyotiṣmatīṃ nāgaraṃ ca anantāmabhayāṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.33"> uropāṅgalalāṭeṣu sirāś cāsya vimokṣayet |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.34cd"> unmādeṣu ca sarveṣu kuryāc cattaprasādanam |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.35ab"> śokaśalyaṃ vyapanayed unmāde pañcame bhiṣak |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.62.35cd"> viṣaje mṛdupūrvāṃ ca viṣaghnīṃ kārayet kriyām ||</l>

        <div n="63" type="adhyāya">
          <head>triṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.1"> athāto rasabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.3"> doṣāṇāṃ pañcadaśadhā prasaro 'bhihitas tu yaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             triṣaṣṭyā rasabhedānāṃ tat prayojanam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.4"> avidagdhā vidagdhāś ca bhidyante te triṣaṣṭidhā |
            <caesura/>
             rasabhedatriṣaṣṭiṃ tu vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.5"> ekaikenānugamanaṃ bhāgaśo yadudīritam |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāṇāṃ tatra matimān triṣaṣṭiṃ tu prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.6"> yathākramapravṛttānāṃ dvikeṣu madhuro rasaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pañcānukramate yogānamlaś catura eva tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.7"> trīṃś cānugacchati raso lavaṇaḥ kaṭuko dvayam |
            <caesura/>
             tiktaḥ kaṣāyamanveti te dvikā daśa pañca ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.8"> tad yathā madhurāmlaḥ, madhuralavaṇaḥ, madhurakaṭukaḥ,
            madhuratiktaḥ, madhurakaṣāyaḥ, ete pañcānukrāntā madhureṇa; amlalavaṇaḥ, amlakaṭukaḥ,
            amlatiktaḥ, amlakaṣāyaḥ, ete catvāro 'nukrāntā amlena; lavaṇakaṭukaḥ, lavaṇatiktaḥ,
            lavaṇakaṣāyaḥ, ete trayo 'nukāntā lavaṇena; kaṭutiktaḥ, kaṭukaṣāyaḥ, dvāvetāvanukrāntau
            kaṭukena; tiktakaṣāyaḥ eka evānukrāntastiktena; evam ete pañcadaśa dvikasaṃyogā
            vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.9"> trikān vakṣyāmaḥ ādau prayujyamānas tu madhuro daśa gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṭamlo lavaṇastasmād ardhamekaṃ tathā kaṭuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.10"> tad yathā madhurāmlalavaṇaḥ, madhurāmlakaṭukaḥ, madhurāmlatiktaḥ,
            madhurāmalakaṣāyaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṭukaḥ, madhuralavaṇātiktaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṣāyaḥ,
            madhurakaṭukatiktaḥ, madhurakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, madhuratiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ daśānāṃ
            trikasaṃyogānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate; amlalavaṇakaṭukaḥ, amlalavaṇatiktaḥ,
            amlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ, amlakaṭutiktaḥ, amlakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, amlatiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ
            ṣaṇṇāmādāvamlaḥ prayujyate; lavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ, lavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, lavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ,
            evam eṣāṃ trayāṇāmādau lavaṇaḥ prayujyate; kaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam ekasyādau kaṭukaḥ
            prayujyate; evam ete trikasaṃyogā viṃśatir vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.11"> catuṣkān vakṣyāmaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             catuṣkarasasaṃyogānmadhuro daśa gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             caturo 'mlo 'nugacchec ca lavaṇastvekam eva tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.12"> madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭukaḥ, madhurāmlalavaṇatiktaḥ,
            madhurāmlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ, madhurāmlakaṭukatiktaḥ, madhurāmlakaṭukaṣāyaḥ,
            madhurāmlatiktakaṣāyaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṭukatiktaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ,
            madhuralavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ, madhurakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ daśānāmādau madhuraḥ
            prayujyate; amlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ, amlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, amlalavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ,
            amlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ caturṇāmādāvamlaḥ; lavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam
            ekasyādau lavaṇaḥ; evam ete catuṣkarasasaṃyogāḥ pañcadaśa kīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.13"> pañcakān vakṣyāmaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pañcakān pañca madhura ekamamlas tu gacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.14"> madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ, madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ,
            madhurāmlalavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ, madhurāmlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ,
            evam eṣāṃ pañcānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate; amlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam
            ekasyādāvamlaḥ; evam ete ṣaṭ pañcakasaṃyogā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.15"> ṣaṭkamekaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ; ekas tu ṣaṭkasaṃyogaḥ
            madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ; eṣa eka eva ṣaṭsaṃyogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.16"> ekaikaś ca ṣaṭsā bhavanti madhuraḥ, amlaḥ, lavaṇaḥ, kaṭukaḥ,
            tiktaḥ, kaṣāyaḥ, iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.17"> bhavati cātra eṣā triṣaṣṭirvyākhyātā rasānāṃ rasacintakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣabhedatriṣaṣṭyāṃ tu prayoktavyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāyeṣu
            rasabhedavikalpādhyāyo nāma (prathamaḥ, āditaḥ) triṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||63 ||</p>

          <head>pañcaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1"> athātas tantrayuktim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3"> dvātriṃśat tantrayuktayo bhavanti śāstre |
            <caesura/>
             tad yathā adhikaraṇaṃ, yogaḥ, padārthaḥ, hetvarthaḥ, uddeśaḥ, nirdeśaḥ, upadeśaḥ,
            apadeśaḥ, pradeśaḥ, atideśaḥ, apavarjaḥ, vākyaśeṣaḥ, arthāpattiḥ, viparyayaḥ, prasaṅgaḥ,
            ekāntaḥ, anekāntaḥ, pūrvapakṣaḥ, nirṇayaḥ, anumataṃ, vidhānam, anāgatāvekṣaṇam,
            atikrāntāvekṣaṇaṃ, saṃśayaḥ, vyākhyānaṃ, svasaṃjñā, nirvacanaṃ, nidarśanaṃ, niyogaḥ,
            vikalpaḥ, samuccayaḥ, ūhyam, iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4"> atrāsāṃ tantrayuktīnāṃ kiṃ prayojanam ucyate vākyayojanam
            arthayojanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5"> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ—
            <caesura/>
             asadvādiprayuktānāṃ vākyānāṃ pratiṣedhanam |
            <caesura/>
             svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6"> vyāktā noktās tu ye hy arthā līnā ye cāpy anirmalāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāṃ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"> yathāmbujavanasyārkaḥ pradīpo veśmano yathā |
            <caesura/>
             prabodhasya prakāśārthaṃ tathā tantrasya yuktayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8"> tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate tad adhikaraṇaṃ; yathā rasaṃ doṣaṃ
            vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9"> yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavalli<pc> </pc>nimba<pc> </pc>hiṃsrābhayā<pc
            > </pc>vṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge |
            <caesura/>
             ity atra tailaṃ siddhaṃ pibed iti prathamaṃ vaktavye tṛtīyapāde siddham iti prayuktaṃ,
            evaṃ dūrasthānām api padānām ekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.10"> yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre pade vā sa padārthaḥ; padasya padayoḥ
            padānāṃ vārthaḥ padārthaḥ; aparimitāś ca padārthāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā sneha<pc> </pc>svedāñjaneṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu dvayos trayāṇāṃ vārthānām upapattir
            dṛśyate, tatra yo 'rthaḥ pūrvāparayoga<pc> </pc>siddho bhavati sa grahītavyaḥ; yathā
            vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ity ukte sandihyate buddhiḥ katamasya vedasyotpattiṃ
            vakṣyatīti, yataḥ ṛgvedādayas tu vedāḥ; vida vicāraṇe, vidḷ lābhe, ity etayoś ca dhātvor
            anekārthayoḥ prayogāt, tatra pūrvāpara<pc> </pc>yogam upalabhya pratipattir bhavati
            āyurvedotpattim ayaṃ vivakṣur iti; eṣa padārthaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.11"> yad anyad uktam anyārthasādhakaṃ bhavati sa hetvarthaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā mṛtpiṇḍo 'dbhiḥ praklidyate tathā māṣa<pc> </pc>dugdha<pc> </pc>prabhṛtibhir
            vraṇaḥ praklidyata iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.12"> samāsa<pc> </pc>vacanam uddeśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā śalyam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.13"> vistaravacanaṃ nirdeśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā śārīram āgantukaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.14"> evam ity upadeśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā tathā na jāgṛyād rātrau divāsvapnaṃ ca varjayet iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.15"> anena kāraṇenety apadeśaḥ, yathāpadiśyate madhuraḥ śleṣmāṇam
            abhivardhayatīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.16"> prakṛtasyātikrāntena sādhanaṃ pradeśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā devadattasyānena śalyam uddhṛtaṃ tathā yajñadattasyāpy ayam uddhariṣyatīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.17"> prakṛtasyānāgatasya sāghanam atideśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā yato 'sya vāyur ūrdhvam uttiṣṭhate tenodāvartī syād iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.18"> abhivyāpyāpakarṣaṇam apavargaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā asvedyā viṣopasṛṣṭāḥ, anyatra kīṭaviṣād iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.19"> yena padenānuktena vākyaṃ samāpyeta sa vākyaśeṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā śiraḥpāṇipādapārśvapṛṣṭhodarorasām ity ukte puruṣagrahaṇaṃ vināpi gamyate
            puruṣasyeti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.20"> yadakīrtitamarthādāpadyate sārthāpattiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā odanaṃ bhokṣye ity ukte 'rthādāpannaṃ bhavati nāyaṃ pipāsur yavāgūm iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.21"> yadyatrābhihitaṃ tasya prātilomyaṃ viparyayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā kṛśālpaprāṇabhīravo duścikitsyā ity ukte viparītaṃ gṛhyate dṛḍhādayaḥ sucikitsyā
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.22"> prakaraṇāntareṇa samāpanaṃ prasaṅgaḥ, yadvā prakaraṇāntarito yo
            'rtho 'sakṛduktaḥ samāpyate sa prasaṅgaḥ | yathā pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣas
            tasmin kriyā so 'dhiṣṭhānam iti vedotpattāv abhidhāya, bhūtacintāyāṃ punar uktaṃ yato
            'bhihitaṃ pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa iti, sa khalv eṣa karmapuruṣaś
            cikitsādhikṛta iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.23"> (sarvatra) yad avadhāraṇenocyate sa ekāntaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā trivṛd virecayati, madanaphalaṃ vāmayati (eva) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.24"> kvacit tathā kvacid anyatheti yaḥ so 'nekāntaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā kecid ācāryā bruvate dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, kecid rasaṃ, kecid vīryaṃ kecid vipākam
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.25"> ākṣepapūrvakaḥ praśnaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā kathaṃ vātanimittāś catvāraḥ pramehā asādhyā bhavantīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.26"> tasyottaraṃ nirṇayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā śarīraṃ prapīḍya paścād adho gatvā vasāmedomajjānuviddhaṃ mūtraṃ visṛjati vātaḥ,
            evam asādhyā vātajā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.27"> tathā coktam kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ niṣpīḍya medomajjāvasāyutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             adhaḥ prakupyate vāyus tenāsādhyās tu vātajāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.28"> paramatamapratiṣiddham anumatam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā anyo brūyāt sapta rasā iti, tac cāpratiṣedhād anumanyate kathaṃcid iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.29"> prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitaṃ vidhānam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā sakthimarmāṇy ekādaśa prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.30"> evaṃ vakṣyatīty anāgatāvekṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā ślokasthāne brūyāt cikitsiteṣu vakṣyāmīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.31"> yat pūrvam uktaṃ tad atikrāntāvekṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāt ślokasthāne yad īritam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.32"> ubhayahetudarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā talahṛdayābhighātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ, pāṇipādacchedanam aprāṇaharam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.33"> tantre 'tiśayopavarṇanaṃ vyākhyānam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā iha pañcaviṃśatikaḥ puruṣo vyākhyāyate, anyeṣv āyurvedatantreṣu
            bhūtādiprabhṛtyārabhya cintā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.34"> anyaśāstrāsāmānyā svasaṃjñā |
            <caesura/>
             yathā mithunam iti madhusarpiṣor grahaṇaṃ; lokaprasiddham udāharaṇaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.35"> niścitaṃ vacanaṃ nirvacanam | yathā āyur vidyate 'sminn anena vā
            āyur vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.36"> dṛṣṭāntavyaktir nidarśanam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā agnir vāyunā sahitaḥ kakṣe vṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo vraṇa iti
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.37"> idam eva kartavyam iti niyogaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā pathyam eva bhoktavyam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.38"> idaṃ cedaṃ ceti samuccayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā māṃsavarge eṇahariṇādayo lāvatittiriśāraṅgāś ca pradhānānīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.39"> idaṃ vedaṃ veti vikalpaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā rasaudanaḥ saghṛtā yavāgūr vā (bhavatv iti) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.40"> yad anirdiṣṭaṃ buddhyā +avagamyate tad ūhyam |
            <caesura/>
             yathā abhihitam annapānavidhau caturvidhaṃ cānnam upadiśyate bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ lehyaṃ
            peyam iti, evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividham abhihitam; idam atrohyam annapāne
            viśiṣṭayor dvayor grahaṇe kṛte caturṇām api grahaṇaṃ bhavatīti; caturvidhaś cāhāraḥ
            praviralaḥ, prāyeṇa dvividha eva; ato dvitvaṃ prasiddham iti |
            <caesura/>
             kiñ cānyat annena bhakṣyam avaruddhaṃ, ghanasādharmyāt; peyena lehyaṃ, dravasādhamyāt
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.41"> bhavanti cātra sāmānyadarśanenāsāṃ vyavasthā saṃpradarśitā |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣas tu yathāyogam upadhāryo vipaś citā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.42"> dvātriṃśadyuktayo hy etās tantrasāragaveṣaṇe |
            <caesura/>
             mayā samyag vinihitāḥ śabdārthanyāyasaṃyutāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.43"> yo hy etā vidhivad vetti dīpībhūtās tu buddhimān |
            <caesura/>
             sa pūjārho bhiṣakśreṣṭha iti dhanvantarer matam ||</l>

          <p xml:id="SS.6.65.colophon" ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre
            tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāyeṣu tantrayuktir nāma (tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcaṣaṣṭitamo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||65 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="66" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"> athāto doṣabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3"> aṣṭāṅgavedividvāṃsaṃ divodāsaṃ mahaujasam |
            <caesura/>
             chinnaśāstrārthasaṃdehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhāgamodadhim | </l>
          <l/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4"> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmān suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati |
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.5"> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā dviśo vāpy athavā triśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.6"> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūlaḥ suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca purīṣaṃ mūtram eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.7"> dehaṃ sandhārayanty ete hy avyāpannā rasair hitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaśakalaḥ prāṇāś caikādaśaiva ye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8ab"> rogāṇāṃ tu sahasraṃ yac chataṃ viṃśatir eva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8cd"> śataṃ ca pañca dravyāṇāṃ trisaptatyadhikottaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.9"> vyāsataḥ kīrtitaṃ taddhi bhinnā doṣāstrayo guṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niś cayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.10"> traya eva pṛthak doṣā dviśo nava samādhikaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayodaśādhikaikadvisamam adhyolbaṇais triśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.11"> pañcāśad evaṃ tu saha bhavanti kṣayam āgataiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇamadhyādhikakṣīṇakṣīṇavṛddhais tathāparaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.12"> dvādaśaivaṃ samākhyātās trayo doṣā dviṣaṣṭidhā |
            <caesura/>
             miśrā dhātumalairdoṣā yānty asaṃkhyeyatāṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.13"> tasmāt prasaṅgaṃ saṃyamya doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathair itaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14"> bhiṣak kartātha karaṇaṃ rasā doṣās tu kāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam ato 'nyathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14a"/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14b"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.15"> adhyāyānāṃ tu ṣaṭṣaṣṭyā grathitārthapadakramam |
            <caesura/>
             evam etad aśeṣeṇa tantram uttaram ṛddhimat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16"> spaṣṭagūḍhārthavijñānam agāḍham andacetasām |
            <caesura/>
             yathāvidhi yathāpraśnaṃ bhavatāṃ parikīrtitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17"> sahottaraṃ tv etad adhītya sarvaṃ brāhmaṃ vidhānena yathoditena |
            <caesura/>
             na hīyate 'rthān manaso 'bhyupetād etad vaco brahmam atīvasatyam ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17i"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17ii"/>


          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre doṣabhedavikalpo nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||66 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div>
          <p ana="trailer">iti sauśrute āyurvedaśāstre uttarasthānaṃ samāptam || </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </body>
  </text>
</TEI>
